### [1] [PITMuS: A Tool for Automated Bug Dataset Generation via Source-Level Mutant Reconstruction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21930v1)
*Tasfia Tasnim,Soneya Binta Hossain*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: PITMuS从突变测试中生成源代码级别的错误修复对数据集，用于LLM软件工程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有突变测试工具PIT通过XML报告突变体，难以重用为结构化源代码级数据集，且现有基准易受污染。

Method: 结合PIT XML元数据与编译类文件的调试信息，定位并重建每个突变体的源代码编辑，自动生成结构化数据集。

Result: 在八个开源Java系统上成功应用，生成了包含源代码级错误/修复对、文档和元数据的结构化数据集。

Conclusion: PITMuS可应用于任何集成PIT的Java系统，为下游训练和评估提供新鲜、可重用的数据集。

中文摘要：基于LLM的软件工程越来越依赖于可执行的、上下文丰富的错误工件：配对的正确代码和有缺陷代码、被测方法（MUT）、文档和元数据。这些工件支持自动错误定位和修复技术的训练和评估、测试和测试预言生成方法，以及文档驱动的自动化。尽管精心策划的基准（例如Defects4J）仍然有价值，但它们是的，并且随着代码模型在大型公共语料库上进行训练，它们越来越容易受到污染。一个互补的策略是通过选择真实的系统版本并在源代码级别注入受控的错误来生成新鲜的、截止日期感知的数据集。突变测试是这一策略的自然基础：它向程序应用预定义的突变算子，并记录现有的测试套件是否检测到每个注入的变化。PIT是一个用于Java的实践中的突变测试工具，它在字节码级别执行突变。这种设计使得突变测试快速且实用，但PIT主要通过XML报告突变体，使得它们难以检查、重放或作为结构化的源代码级数据集记录重用。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了PITMuS，它结合了PIT XML元数据和编译的Java类文件中的调试信息，以定位和重建对应于每个突变体的源代码编辑。然后PITMuS自动生成结构化的数据集，包含源代码级别的错误和修复代码对、文档上下文和元数据，用于下游训练和评估。尽管我们在八个开源Java系统上评估了PITMuS，但它可以应用于任何可以集成PIT的Java系统。

Original abstract: LLM-based software engineering increasingly depends on executable, context-rich bug artifacts: paired correct and buggy code, methods under test (MUTs), documentation, and metadata. These artifacts support the training and evaluation of automated bug localization and repair techniques, testing and test oracle generation methods, and documentation-driven automation. Although curated benchmarks (e.g., Defects4J) remain valuable, they are static and increasingly vulnerable to contamination as code models are trained on large public corpora. A complementary strategy is to generate fresh, cutoff-aware datasets by selecting real system versions and injecting controlled bugs at the source level.
  Mutation testing is a natural basis for this strategy: it applies predefined mutation operators to programs and records whether the existing test suite detects each injected change. PIT is a state-of-the-practice mutation testing tool for Java that performs mutation at the bytecode level. This design makes mutation testing fast and practical, but PITMuS reports mutants primarily through XML, making them difficult to inspect, replay, or reuse as structured source-level dataset records. To address this gap, we present PITMuS, which combines PITMuS XML metadata with debug information from compiled Java class files to localize and reconstruct the source edit corresponding to each mutant. PITMuS then automatically produces structured datasets containing source-level buggy and fixed code pairs, documentation context, and metadata for downstream training and evaluation. Although we evaluate PITMuS on eight open-source Java systems, it can be applied to any Java system where PITMuS can be integrated.

</details>


### [2] [Deterministic vs. Probabilistic Summarisation: An Empirical Trade-off Study in Design Pattern Centric Java Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21943v1)
*Najam Nazar,Christoph Treude*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文对比了基于规则/SWUM的确定性方法与基于Mixtral LLM的概率性方法在面向意图的设计模式代码摘要上的表现，发现概率方法语义更强但存在变异性，确定性方法更简洁可复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化代码摘要有助于程序理解和文档化，但确定性和概率性流水线的优缺点尚不明确，需要系统比较。

Method: 使用150个设计模式Java文件，比较了规则型NLG、SWUM和Mixtral LLM三种流水线；采用BERTScore、余弦相似度和Llama 3多维度评判进行评价，并进行了Wilcoxon等统计分析。

Result: 概率性摘要语义对齐和上下文覆盖更好，但确定性摘要更简洁和可复现；LLM输出有变异性，但趋势稳定。

Conclusion: 概率方法适合需要语义深度的场景，确定性方法适合需要简洁性和可复现性的场景。

中文摘要：背景：自动化代码摘要支持程序理解和文档编写，然而确定性（基于启发式）和概率性（基于LLM）流水线的相对优势和局限性仍不清楚。目的：本文针对面向意图的设计模式代码摘要，对这两种范式进行了受控的实证比较。方法：使用以设计模式为中心的Java代码作为结构化测试平台（来自三个开源存储库的150个文件，涵盖九种模式），我们比较了基于规则的自然语言生成（NLG）流水线、基于软件词汇使用模型（SWUM）的方法以及基于Mixtral LLM的概率流水线。使用BERTScore和余弦相似度将摘要与人工参考进行比较，并辅以Llama 3基于评分标准在五个维度上生成的判断：准确性、简洁性、充分性、代码上下文意识和设计模式保真度。统计分析包括Wilcoxon符号秩检验（含效应量）、带有事后校正的Friedman检验以及用于评分标准一致性敏感性分析的Spearman相关性。结果：概率性摘要显示出更强的语义对齐和更丰富的上下文覆盖，而确定性方法则产生更简洁且完全可复现的输出。提示敏感性和多次运行分析表明LLM输出存在变异性，但相对趋势保持稳定。结论：存在明显的权衡：概率性方法偏向语义深度和上下文准确性，而确定性流水线更适合简洁性和可复现性。这些发现为选择代码摘要技术提供了实用指导。

Original abstract: Background: Automated code summarisation supports program comprehension and documentation, yet the relative strengths and limitations of deterministic (heuristic-based) and probabilistic (LLM-based) pipelines remain unclear. Aims: This paper presents a controlled empirical comparison of these paradigms for intent-oriented design-pattern code summarisation. Method: Using design-pattern-centric Java code as a structured testbed (150 files from three open-source repositories covering nine patterns), we compare a rule-based natural language generation (NLG) pipeline, a Software Word Usage Model (SWUM)-based approach, and a probabilistic pipeline based on the Mixtral LLM. Summaries are evaluated against human references using BERTScore and cosine similarity, complemented by rubric-based judgements produced by Llama 3 across five dimensions: accuracy, conciseness, adequacy, code-context awareness, and design-pattern fidelity. Statistical analysis includes Wilcoxon signed-rank tests (with effect sizes), Friedman tests with post-hoc corrections, and Spearman correlation for sensitivity analysis of rubric consistency. Results: Probabilistic summaries show stronger semantic alignment and richer contextual coverage, while deterministic approaches produce more concise and fully reproducible outputs. Prompt-sensitivity and multi-run analyses indicate variability in LLM outputs, though relative trends remain stable. Conclusions: A clear trade-off emerges: probabilistic methods favour semantic depth and contextual accuracy, whereas deterministic pipelines are preferable for brevity and reproducibility. These findings provide practical guidance for selecting code summarisation techniques.

</details>


### [3] [From Patches to Trajectories: Privileged Process Supervision for Software-Engineering Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21996v1)
*Murong Ma,Tianyu Chen,Yun Lin,Shuai Lu,Qinglin Zhu,Yeyun Gong,Zhiyong Huang,Peng Cheng,Yan Lu,Jin Song Dong*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: P2T利用参考补丁作为特权信息，通过双目标优化从教师轨迹中整理出高质量训练数据，显著提升SWE代理性能并降低推理成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有监督微调方法使用二元终端验证器过滤教师轨迹，无法确保每一步的有效性和高效性，且忽略了参考补丁中的宝贵信息。

Method: 提出Patches-to-Trajectories (P2T)，包括反向阶段将参考补丁提炼为潜在过程图，正向阶段根据该图对盲化教师延续进行评分并保留最短有效片段。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上Pass@1提高10.8点，推理成本降低15%；在SWE-bench Lite上一致提升。

Conclusion: P2T通过使用参考补丁作为特权信息，能够有效提高训练数据的质量和效率，从而提升SWE代理性能。

中文摘要：监督微调（SFT）在长教师轨迹上是为开放软件工程（SWE）代理注入调查和推理能力的主要方式。由于每个保留的响应都成为模仿目标，学生继承了最终结果和中间缺陷，包括无根据的跳跃和冗余循环。高质量的训练数据必须有效（每一步都有根据，缩小代理到正确修复的知识差距）和高效（每一步都携带信息而非冗余或循环）。现有方法仅使用二元终端验证器过滤或重新标记教师轨迹，这并不直接针对这些轴，并且在教师失败的情况下不提供监督。大多数真实问题包括开发人员撰写的参考补丁$p^\star$，揭示了正确修复预设的文件路径、运行时行为和编码约定，但标准流程丢弃了它。我们提出补丁到轨迹（P2T），它在整理过程中使用$p^\star$作为特权信息，并将轨迹构建公式化为每步有效性和轨迹长度的双目标优化。反向阶段将$p^\star$提炼为上下文事实和解决方案里程碑的潜在过程图$G^\star$。正向阶段通过根据$G^\star$在泄漏阻止的有根据性检查下对每步进展评分，并保留最短的有效片段，从盲化的教师延续中整理轨迹。仅使用1.8k个整理后的SWE-Gym实例，P2T在效果和效率上都优于基于结果过滤的SFT及其工具错误掩码变体。在SWE-bench Verified上，它将Pass@1提高了多达10.8个百分点，同时将每实例推理成本降低了约15%，在SWE-bench Lite上也取得了一致的收益。规模匹配的消融研究和定性分析进一步将轨迹质量与数据规模分离。

Original abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on long teacher trajectories is the dominant way to instill investigation and reasoning in open software-engineering (SWE) agents. Since every retained response becomes an imitation target, the student inherits the final outcome and intermediate flaws, including ungrounded leaps and redundant loops. High-quality training data must be effective(each step is grounded and narrows the agent's epistemic gap to the correct fix) and efficient(each step is information-bearing rather than redundant or looping). Existing recipes filter or relabel teacher rollouts using only a binary terminal verifier, which does not directly target these axes and provides no supervision on instances where the teacher fails.
  Most real issue includes a developer-authored reference patch, $p^\star$, revealing the file paths, runtime behaviors, and coding conventions presupposed by the correct fix, yet standard pipelines discard it. We propose Patches-to-Trajectories (P2T), which uses $p^\star$ as privileged information during curation and formulates trajectory construction as bi-objective optimization over per-step effectiveness and trajectory length. A reverse phase distills $p^\star$ into a latent process graph, $G^\star$, of contextual facts and solution milestones. A forward phase curates trajectories from blinded teacher continuations by scoring per-step progress against $G^\star$ under a leakage-blocking groundedness check and retaining the shortest effective segments.
  Using only 1.8k curated SWE-Gym instances, P2T improves effectiveness and efficiency over outcome-filtered SFT and its tool-error-masking variant. On SWE-bench Verified, it raises Pass@1 by up to 10.8 points while reducing per-instance inference cost by ~15%, with consistent gains on SWE-bench Lite. Size-matched ablations and qualitative analysis further isolate trajectory quality from data scale.

</details>


### [4] [Finding Missing Input Validation in TEEs via LLM-Assisted Symbolic Execution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22058v1)
*Chengyan Ma,Jieke Shi,Ruidong Han,Ye Liu,Yuqing Niu,David Lo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SymTEE是一个LLM辅助的符号执行框架，无需真实TEE环境即可高精度检测缺失输入验证漏洞，成本低至0.05美元。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TEE应用分析因配置复杂和硬件隔离导致的低可观测性而困难重重，现有方法成本高且难以扩展。

Method: 通过AST分析提取疑似缺失输入验证的TEE代码片段，再用LLM自动生成KLEE兼容的轻量级模拟环境进行符号执行。

Result: 在26个漏洞测试中达到100%精确率和92.3%召回率，平均分析成本仅0.05美元。

Conclusion: SymTEE的LLM辅助符号执行范式有效且实用，能自主生成模拟环境实现自动化安全分析，使TEE应用分析更易访问和可扩展。

中文摘要：可信执行环境（TEE）通过硬件强制隔离保护敏感代码和数据免受不可信软件的侵害。尽管具有强大的安全保证，但由于配置完整TEE构建和运行时环境的高成本和高复杂度，以及硬件隔离带来的有限可观测性，分析TEE应用程序仍然具有挑战性。本文提出SymTEE，一种新颖的大语言模型（LLM）辅助的符号执行框架，用于检测TEE应用程序中缺失的输入验证问题，而无需实际TEE设置。SymTEE首先利用抽象语法树（AST）分析提取可能缺乏足够输入验证的TEE代码片段，然后使用LLM（本文中为GPT-5）自动将提取的片段转换为兼容KLEE的测试程序，其中包含用于符号分析的轻量级模拟执行环境。对26个漏洞（11个真实世界和15个合成）的评估显示，SymTEE在检测缺失输入验证漏洞方面实现了100%的精确率和92.3%的召回率，同时平均分析成本仅为0.05美元。这些结果证明了SymTEE开创性范式（即LLM辅助的符号执行）的有效性和实用性，其中LLM自主生成模拟环境，无需复杂设置即可实现自动化安全分析，为可信计算系统提供了更易访问和可扩展的框架。

Original abstract: Trusted Execution Environments (TEEs) provide hardware-enforced isolation that protects sensitive code and data from untrusted software. Despite their strong security guarantees, analyzing TEE applications remains challenging due to the high cost and complexity of configuring complete TEE build and runtime environments, as well as the limited observability imposed by hardware isolation. This paper presents SymTEE, a novel large language model (LLM)-assisted symbolic execution framework for detecting missing input validation issues in TEE applications without requiring real TEE setups. SymTEE begins by leveraging Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) analysis to extract TEE code slices that may lack sufficient input validation, and then employs an LLM (GPT-5 in our case) to automatically convert the extracted slices into KLEE-compatible harness programs containing lightweight mock execution environments for symbolic analysis. Evaluations on 26 vulnerabilities (11 real-world and 15 synthetic) show that SymTEE achieves 100% precision and 92.3% recall in detecting missing input validation vulnerabilities while incurring an average analysis cost of only $0.05. These results demonstrate the effectiveness and practicality of SymTEE's pioneering paradigm of LLM-assisted symbolic execution, where LLMs autonomously generate mock environments to enable automated security analysis without complex setup, providing a more accessible and scalable framework for trusted computing systems.

</details>


### [5] [Automated Repair of TEE Partitioning Issues via DSL-Guided and LLM-Assisted Patching](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22087v1)
*Chengyan Ma,Jieke Shi,Ruidong Han,Ye Liu,Feng Li,Yuqing Niu,David Lo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出TEERepair框架，利用DSL和LLM自动修复TEE应用中的划分漏洞，修复成功率达87.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TEE应用与不可信OS交互导致划分漏洞，现有工作缺乏自动修复方法。

Method: 引入DSL编码修复规则，利用LLM合成上下文感知补丁，并生成测试客户端验证。

Result: 在PartitioningE-Bench上修复成功率87.6%，提交5个PR，2个被合并。

Conclusion: TEERepair有效自动修复TEE划分漏洞，具有实际应用价值。

中文摘要：可信执行环境（TEE）提供基于硬件的隔离，以保护敏感数据和计算免受潜在受损操作系统（OS）的影响。然而，TEE应用不可避免地通过SDK接口与不可信操作系统交互，不当的划分可能引入严重漏洞，如数据泄漏和代码注入。虽然先前的工作提出了静态分析工具来检测此类问题，但自动修复仍基本未被探索。由于三个TEE特定因素，这一问题尤其具有挑战性：缺乏标准化的安全开发指南、从低级C代码中提取语义信息的困难、以及缺乏成熟的测试和验证方法。在这项工作中，我们提出了TEERepair，一个自动修复TEE应用中不良划分问题的框架。我们的方法通过引入领域特定语言（DSL）来编码修复规则，表达和捕获常见TEE安全模式，这些规则被实例化为带有上下文特定变量占位符的补丁模板。然后，我们利用大型语言模型（LLM）推理代码语义并合成上下文感知的补丁，并进一步生成测试客户端以验证修复。我们在TEE划分错误基准（PartitioningE-Bench）上评估TEERepair，与基线相比实现了显著更高的修复成功率87.6%。此外，将TEERepair应用于真实世界的TEE项目，我们提交了5个修复拉取请求，其中2个已被项目维护者确认并合并。

Original abstract: Trusted Execution Environments (TEEs) provide hardware-based isolation to protect sensitive data and computations from potentially compromised operating systems (OS). However, TEE applications inevitably interact with the untrusted OS through SDK interfaces, and improper partitioning can introduce severe vulnerabilities such as data leakage and code injection. While prior work has proposed static analysis tools to detect such issues, automated repair remains largely unexplored. This problem is particularly challenging due to three TEE-specific factors: the lack of standardized secure development guidelines, the difficulty of extracting semantic information from low-level C code, and the absence of mature testing and validation methods. In this work, we present TEERepair, a framework for automatically repairing bad partitioning issues in TEE applications. Our approach tackles the above challenges by introducing a domain-specific language (DSL) to encode repair rules that express and capture common TEE security patterns, which are instantiated as patch templates with placeholders for context-specific variables. We then leverage large language models (LLMs) to reason about code semantics and synthesize context-aware patches, and further generate test clients to validate the repairs. We evaluate TEERepair on the TEE Partitioning Errors Benchmark (PartitioningE-Bench), achieving a significantly higher repair success rate of 87.6% compared to baselines. Furthermore, applying TEERepair to real-world TEE projects, we submitted 5 repair pull requests, 2 of which have been confirmed and merged by project maintainers.

</details>


### [6] [SWE-Mutation: Can LLMs Generate Reliable Test Suites in Software Engineering?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22175v1)
*Yuxuan Sun,Yuze Zhao,Yufeng Wang,Yao Du,Zhiyuan Ma,Jinbo Wang,Mengdi Zhang,Kai Zhang,Zhenya Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SWE-Mutation基准，通过系统变异评估LLM生成的测试套件质量，发现现有LLM生成的测试套件区分能力不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM评估中测试套件质量不足，是制约扩展的关键瓶颈。

Method: 引入SWE-Mutation基准，通过系统变异解决方案生成更难通过的测试用例，并利用智能代理自动生成复杂变异。

Result: 在7个LLM上测试，DeepSeek-V3.1验证率仅10.20%，检测率36.15%；智能变异策略将检测率从71.04%降至39.81%。

Conclusion: 当前LLM生成可靠且具区分性的测试套件能力不足。

中文摘要：评估软件工程能力已成为现代大型语言模型（LLM）的核心组成部分；然而，阻碍进一步扩展的关键瓶颈并非高质量解决方案的稀缺，而是高质量测试套件的缺乏。测试套件对于合成程序修复轨迹以及在强化学习中提供精确反馈信号都是不可或缺的。不幸的是，由于标注成本高昂且困难，高质量测试套件长期以来难以获得，而由LLM自动生成的测试套件往往流于表面且缺乏足够的区分能力。作为构建高质量测试套件的第一步，我们引入了SWE-Mutation，一个用于评估LLM生成的测试套件的基准。该基准通过引入系统性变异的解决方案来表征测试套件，这些变异试图“欺骗”测试套件并通过验证。我们进一步提出了一个基于智能体且语言无关的框架，用于自动生成复杂变异体。我们的基准包含来自800个原始实例的2636个变异变体，并包括一个涵盖九种编程语言的多语言子集。在七个LLM上的实验表明，即使是DeepSeek-V3.1也仅能达到10.20%的验证率和36.15%的检测率，凸显了当前LLM的不足。此外，我们的智能体变异策略增强了现实性，将平均检测率从传统方法的71.04%降低到39.81%。这些发现暴露了当前LLM在生成可靠且具有区分性的测试套件方面持续存在的缺陷。

Original abstract: Evaluating software engineering capabilities has become a core component of modern large language models (LLMs); however, the key bottleneck hindering further scaling lies not in the scarcity of high-quality solutions, but in the lack of high-quality test suites. Test suites are indispensable both for synthesizing program repair trajectories and for providing precise feedback signals in reinforcement learning. Unfortunately, due to the high cost and difficulty of annotation, high-quality test suites have long been hard to obtain, while those automatically generated by LLMs tend to be superficial and lack sufficient discriminative power. As a first step toward constructing high-quality test suites, we introduce SWE-Mutation, a benchmark for evaluating LLM-generated test suites. The benchmark characterizes test suites by introducing systematically mutated solutions that attempt to ``fool'' the test suites and pass validation. We further propose an agentic, language-agnostic framework for automatically generating complex mutants. Our benchmark consists of 2,636 mutated variants derived from 800 original instances and includes a multilingual subset spanning nine programming languages. Experiments on seven LLMs reveal that even DeepSeek-V3.1 achieves only 10.20% verification and 36.15% detection rates, highlighting the inadequacy of current LLMs. Additionally, our agentic mutation strategy enhances realism, reducing average detection rates from 71.04% to 39.81% compared to conventional methods. These findings expose persistent deficiencies in the ability of current LLMs to generate reliable and discriminative test suites.

</details>


### [7] [An Architecture for Decentralised Deployment and Operation of Blockchain Applications](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22239v1)
*Fabian Stiehle,Kirill Inozemtsev,Ingo Weber*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合DevOps最佳实践的区块链去中心化应用治理与部署架构，通过扩展注册模式实现确定性部署，并提供了开源参考实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有区块链DevOps基础设施常由单一实体控制，而大型应用需要去中心化治理（如DAO）但集成复杂，缺乏统一的、与治理和升级实现无关的架构。

Method: 集成DAO治理与DevOps实践，扩展注册模式支持确定性部署，设计去中心化部署框架（含CI/CD管道、UI、版本控制），并基于开源参考实现验证。

Result: 提出了一个与具体治理和升级实现无关的架构，提供了开源参考实现，并通过评估证明了其有效性和实用性。

Conclusion: 该架构可作为未来集成的参考，开源框架有助于降低实际采用此类流程的复杂性。

中文摘要：区块链和分布式账本技术使得多种去中心化应用（dApps）得以运行。这些应用基于智能合约，这是一种以去中心化方式执行的可编程抽象。为确保智能合约的正确性，区块链应用开发者依赖于DevOps实践，如自动化测试和持续集成与部署。然而，此类基础设施通常由单一实体控制。对于较大的区块链应用，这个问题通过依赖去中心化自治组织（DAO）的概念来解决，这允许提案在达到预定义的法定人数后自动执行。这种治理架构复杂，需要与现有的合约发现和可升级性模式集成。在本文中，我们将这些概念结合DevOps最佳实践集成到一个新颖的架构中，该架构保持对不同治理和升级实现的不可知性。我们扩展了已知的注册模式以支持确定性部署，并提出了一个去中心化部署框架，包括集成和部署管道、用户界面和版本控制集成。在我们的方法中，各方在参与使用（新部署的）智能合约之前，实施并验证自己的测试。我们提供了一个参考实现，作为开源提供，并彻底评估了该提案。我们的架构可以作为未来集成的参考，而我们的开源框架旨在降低在实践中采用此类流程的复杂性。

Original abstract: Blockchains and distributed ledger technologies allow the operation of manifold decentralised applications (dApps). Such applications are based on smart contracts, a programmable abstraction that is executed in a decentralised manner. To ensure the correctness of smart contracts, blockchain application developers rely on DevOps practices such as automated testing and continuous integration and deployment. However, such infrastructure is often controlled by single entities. For larger blockchain applications, this issue is resolved by relying on concepts of Decentralised Autonomous Organisations (DAOs), which allow proposals to be autonomously executed once they reach a pre-defined quorum. Such a governance architecture is complex and requires integration with existing patterns for contract discovery and upgradeability. In this paper we integrate these concepts considering DevOps best-practices into a novel architecture that remains agnostic to different governance and upgrade implementations. We extend the known registry pattern to support deterministic deployments and present a decentralised deployment framework, including integration and deployment pipelines, user-interfaces, and version control integration. In our approach, each party implements and verifies their own tests before engaging in the use of a (newly deployed) smart contract. We provide a reference implementation, available as open-source, and evaluate the proposal thoroughly. Our architecture can serve as a reference for future integrations, while our open-source framework is aimed at reducing the complexity of adopting such a process in practice.

中文摘要：生成式人工智能（GenAI）正在迅速重塑软件开发，人们越来越强调提高生产率和优化性能。然而，过度关注这些维度可能会忽视对开发者福祉的关键影响。GenAI工具可能增加认知负荷，引入新的监督工作形式，并提高产出和速度方面的期望，从而导致压力、倦怠和工作生活平衡的恶化。GenAI运动也在改变职业规范，改变职业入门点，要求持续适应，并加深了在获取和支持方面的不平等。这篇立场论文呼吁重新定位软件开发中的GenAI研究议程，并提出了一个理论框架，以便超越狭隘的性能指标，转向同时关注人类体验、社会背景和可持续生产力的研究。

Original abstract: Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI) is rapidly reshaping software development, with growing emphasis on accelerating productivity and optimizing performance. However, excessive focus on such dimensions risks overlooking the critical implications for developer well-being. GenAI tools can amplify cognitive load, introduce new forms of oversight labor, and escalate expectations around output and pace, contributing to stress, burnout, and diminished work-life balance. The GenAI movement is also transforming professional norms, altering career entry points, demanding continuous adaptation, and deepening inequalities in access and support. This position paper calls for a reorientation of the GenAI research agenda in software development and proposes a theoretical framework to move beyond narrow performance metrics toward investigations that also center on human experience, social context, and sustainable productivity.

### [9] ["Refactoring Runaway": Understanding and Mitigating Tangled Refactorings in Coding Agents for Issue Resolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22526v1)
*Zhao Tian,Zifan Zhang,Tao Xiao,Dong Wang,Masanari Kondo,Junjie Chen,Yasutaka Kamei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 编码智能体在问题解决中引入的重构纠缠比人类少，且与可编译性降低相关，但与功能正确性无关；提出的重构感知方法能提升可编译性并解决更多问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实问题解决中人类开发者会自然引入重构纠缠，而编码智能体可能继承此行为，但对此缺乏系统研究。

Method: 在Multi-SWE-bench上对3,691个由三个智能体框架和12个LLM生成的补丁进行实证分析，并使用逻辑回归分析重构纠缠与可编译性和功能正确性的关系。

Result: 智能体引入重构纠缠的频率和强度均低于人类，但类型更多样；重构纠缠与可编译性下降显著相关，与功能正确性无显著关联；提出的方法将可编译性从19.34%提升至38.33%，并额外解决2.79%问题。

Conclusion: 本工作是理解智能体问题解决中重构纠缠的第一步，为未来研究提供了方向。

中文摘要：近期编码智能体的进展在软件问题解决方面显示出显著的进步。在实践中，现实世界的问题通常是错误修复或功能请求，人类开发者自然会将重构作为解决过程的一部分，从而导致重构纠缠。由于LLM在大型开源代码库上进行训练，编码智能体可能继承这种行为。在本文中，我们在Multi-SWE-bench上进行了一项实证研究，分析了由三个智能体框架和12个LLM生成的3,691个有效补丁。我们发现，编码智能体引入重构纠缠的频率较低（21.43%对比36.72%）且强度较低（0.66对比1.75），尽管它们表现出更广泛的重构类型多样性。逻辑回归分析进一步表明，重构纠缠与可编译性降低密切相关，而与功能正确性没有显著关联。基于这些发现，我们提出了一种重构感知的优化方法，该方法评估重构纠缠的必要性和安全性，并选择性地移除或修复有问题的操作。我们的方法将可编译性从19.34%提高到38.33%，并额外解决了2.79%先前未解决的问题。总体而言，本工作迈出了理解智能体问题解决中重构纠缠实践的第一步，并为未来工作开辟了途径。

Original abstract: Recent advances in coding agents have shown remarkable progress in software issue resolution. In practice, real-world issues are typically bug fixes or feature requests in which human developers naturally incorporate refactoring as part of the resolution process, resulting in tangled refactoring. Since LLMs are trained on large-scale open-source repositories, coding agents may inherit such behaviors. In this paper, we conduct an empirical study on Multi-SWE-bench, analyzing 3,691 valid patches generated by three agent frameworks with 12 LLMs. We find that coding agents introduce tangled refactorings less frequently (21.43% vs. 36.72%) and with lower intensity (0.66 vs. 1.75) than human developers, although they exhibit a broader diversity of refactoring types. Logistic regression analysis further shows that tangled refactorings are strongly associated with reduced compilability, while exhibiting no significant association with functional correctness. Based on these findings, we propose a refactoring-aware refinement approach that assesses the necessity and safety of tangled refactorings and selectively removes or repairs problematic operations. Our approach improves compilability from 19.34% to 38.33%, and additionally resolves 2.79% previously unresolved issues. Overall, this work presents the first step towards understanding tangled refactoring practices in agentic issue resolution and opens up avenues for future work.

</details>


### [10] [Why Are Agentic Pull Requests Merged or Rejected? An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22534v1)
*Sien Reeve O. Peralta,Fumika Hoshi,Hironori Washizaki,Naoyasu Ubayashi,Inase Kondo,Yoshiki Higo,Hiroki Mukai,Norihiro Yoshida,Kazuki Kusama,Hidetake Tanaka,Youmei Fan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 仅凭PR合并/拒绝结果评估AI代理性能不可靠，需考虑审查交互行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅用PR结果标签，可能无法真实反映代理能力，需探索审查交互的影响。

Method: 对11,048个Agentic PR进行决策导向分析，筛选9,799个人工审查PR，手动检查717个案例以恢复决策理由。

Result: 拒绝PR中仅35.7%为代理失败，31.2%由工作流约束导致；合并PR中15.4%需审查员参与；不同代理交互模式有差异。

Conclusion: 否定仅用PR结果评估的假设，主张基于审查行为的交互感知评估。

中文摘要：AI编码代理越来越多地向开源仓库提交拉取请求（Agentic-PRs），但它们的性能通常仅通过合并和拒绝结果来评估。我们假设，如果不考虑审查交互，这些结果标签不能可靠地反映代理能力。为了验证这一点，我们对11,048个已关闭的Agentic拉取请求进行了决策导向分析，筛选出9,799个人工审查的PR，并手动检查了717个代表性案例，从交互产物中恢复决策理由。我们发现拒绝结果显著夸大了代理错误：只有35.7%的拒绝PR反映了明确的代理失败，而31.2%是由工作流约束导致的，33.1%缺乏可观察的决策理由。在合并的PR中，15.4%需要审查员通过反馈或直接提交进行显式参与，5.5%没有可见的交互痕迹。我们进一步观察到不同代理之间的系统性差异：Copilot和Devin更常嵌入审查员中介的工作流，而Codex和Cursor的PR通常以最小交互合并。这些结果否定了仅凭PR结果就能捕捉代理性能的假设，并表明需要基于审查行为的交互感知评估。

Original abstract: AI coding agents increasingly submit pull requests (Agentic-PRs) to open-source repositories, yet their performance is commonly assessed using merge and rejection outcomes alone. We hypothesized that these outcome labels do not reliably reflect agent capability without considering review interactions. To test this, we conducted a decision-oriented analysis of 11,048 closed Agentic Pull Requests, refined to 9,799 human-reviewed PRs, and manually inspected 717 representative cases to recover decision rationale from interaction artifacts. We found that rejection outcomes substantially overstate agent error: only 35.7% of rejected PRs reflected clear agentic failures, while 31.2% were driven by workflow constraints and 33.1% lacked observable decision rationale. Among merged PRs, 15.4% required explicit reviewer involvement through feedback or direct commits, and 5.5% showed no visible interaction trace. We further observed systematic differences across agents, with Copilot and Devin more often embedded in reviewer-mediated workflows, while Codex and Cursor PRs were typically merged with minimal interaction. These results reject the assumption that PR outcomes alone capture agent performance and demonstrate the need for interaction-aware evaluation grounded in review behavior.

</details>


### [11] [Contractual Skills: A GovernSpec Design Framework for Enterprise AI Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22634v2)
*Ting Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出契约式技能框架将技能文件组织为任务合约，通过三项实证研究验证其能提升质量并降低错误率，本质是治理层而非安全机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业技能需要表达目标、权限、审批等复杂约束，现有技能封装机制不足以支持这些需求。

Method: 提出GovernSpec-inspired的契约式技能框架，组织SKILL.md文件为可读任务合约，并进行三项离线实证研究（文本生成、A/B扩展、工具调用挑战）。

Result: 第二项研究中，契约式技能将平均质量从4.692提升至4.914，关键错误率从0.083降至0.013。

Conclusion: 契约式技能是使任务意图、边界和验收标准显式化的治理层，而非独立的安全机制。

中文摘要：技能已成为智能体指令、工作流、脚本和参考材料的一种实用封装机制。然而在企业环境中，技能通常需要表达比任务指导更多的内容：目标、输入边界、权限、人工审批点、证据要求、输出合约、质量标准、验证步骤以及移交规则。本文提出了契约式技能，这是一种受GovernSpec启发的设计框架，用于将SKILL.md文件组织为可读的任务合约，同时保持轻量级的技能发现和渐进式加载。该框架明确了契约式技能、GovernSpec YAML合约、模型上下文协议（MCP）接口、工具适配器、运行时护栏、追踪和评估系统之间的边界。我们通过三项离线实证研究对该框架进行了评估。第一项文本生成实验涵盖三项企业技能、十五个合成任务、四种指令条件和八种生成模型，产生了960个输出和1680条交叉评判分数记录。第二项研究是公开技能A/B扩展：将八个公开技能与其契约式重写版本在四十八个合成任务、六种生成模型、两次重复、1152个输出和两份完整评判文件下进行比较。在该设定下，契约式技能将平均质量从4.692提升至4.914，并将关键错误率从0.083降至0.013。第三项研究是包含八个模型和192条模拟工具调用记录的离线工具调用挑战。结果表明，契约式技能最好被理解为一种使任务意图、边界和验收标准显式化的治理层，而非独立的安全机制。

Original abstract: Skills have become a practical packaging mechanism for agent instructions, workflows, scripts, and reference materials. In enterprise settings, however, a skill often needs to express more than task guidance: goals, input boundaries, permissions, human approval points, evidence requirements, output contracts, quality criteria, verification steps, and handoff rules. This paper proposes contractual skills, a GovernSpec-inspired design framework for organizing SKILL.md files as readable task contracts while preserving lightweight skill discovery and progressive loading. The framework clarifies the boundary between contractual skills, GovernSpec YAML contracts, Model Context Protocol (MCP) surfaces, tool adapters, runtime guardrails, tracing, and evaluation systems.
  We evaluate the framework with three offline empirical studies. The first text-generation experiment covers three enterprise skills, fifteen synthetic tasks, four instruction conditions, and eight generation models, producing 960 outputs and 1680 cross-judge score records. The second study is a public-skill A/B expansion: eight public skills are compared with contractual rewrites across forty-eight synthetic tasks, six generation models, two repeats, 1152 outputs, and two complete judge files. In this setting, contractual skills raise mean quality from 4.692 to 4.914 and reduce critical-error rate from 0.083 to 0.013. The third study is an offline tool-calling challenge with eight models and 192 simulated tool-call records. The results suggest that contractual skills are best understood as a governance layer that makes task intent, boundaries, and acceptance criteria explicit, not as a standalone safety mechanism.

</details>


### [12] [FAME: Failure-Aware Mixture-of-Experts for Message-Level Log Anomaly Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22779v1)
*Huanchi Wang,Zihang Huang,Yifang Tian,Kristina Dzeparoska,Hans-Arno Jacobsen,Alberto Leon-Garcia*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: FAME是一种利用LLM离线生成标签和划分故障域的消息级异常检测框架，通过轻量级路由器和专家模型实现高效在线检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有异常检测方法粒度粗（会话/窗口级），消息级检测面临模板歧义、故障异构和标注成本高等挑战，而直接使用LLM进行在线检测成本过高。

Method: 提出FAME框架，仅离线使用LLM一次：对每个模板最多标注K个行以生成正常/异常指示和示例；LLM提出模板到故障域的划分并经过认证；训练轻量级路由器和域专家模型，在线本地运行并输出异常预测和故障域标签。

Result: 在BGL数据集上，K=100时F1=98.16，标注量减少76倍，检测出86.3%来自未见EventID的异常；在Thunderbird数据集上，F1=99.95，召回率达到100%。

Conclusion: FAME实现了标签高效、细粒度的消息级日志异常检测，在保持高精度的同时大幅降低标注成本和在线推理开销。

中文摘要：生产系统每天生成数百万条日志行，然而大多数异常检测器在会话或窗口级别操作，标记的是行组而非识别具体负责的消息。这种粗粒度强制操作员每次警报检查许多常规行。消息级检测提供更细粒度，但仍有挑战。单个事件模板可能对应正常和异常消息，故障来自异构子系统，且大规模行级标记不切实际。尽管大语言模型（LLM）可以推理日志语义，但将每条线应用于持续监控成本过高。我们提出FAME（故障感知混合专家），一种标签高效的消息级混合专家框架，仅离线使用LLM一次。每个模板最多注释K个标记行，以推导二进制正常/异常指标和代表性示例。LLM提出将模板划分为故障域，认证步骤在训练前验证该提议。FAME训练轻量级路由器和域专家，它们本地运行并输出异常预测和故障域标签。在BGL上，FAME在K=100时达到F1=98.16，减少了76倍的注释工作，并检测到86.3%来自未见EventID的异常。在Thunderbird上，FAME达到F1=99.95，召回率完美。

Original abstract: Production systems generate millions of log lines daily, yet most anomaly detectors operate at the session or window-level, flagging groups of lines rather than identifying the specific message responsible. This coarse granularity forces operators to inspect many routine lines per alert. Message-level detection offers finer granularity, but remains challenging. A single event template may correspond to both normal and anomalous messages, failures arise from heterogeneous subsystems, and line-level labeling at scale is impractical. Although large language models (LLMs) can reason over log semantics, applying them to every line is too costly for continuous monitoring. We present FAME (Failure-Aware Mixture-of-Experts), a label-efficient message-level mixture-of-experts framework that uses an LLM only once offline. We annotate at most K labeled lines per template to derive binary normal/anomaly indicators and representative examples. The LLM proposes a partition of templates into failure domains, and a certification step validates the proposal before training. FAME trains a lightweight router and domain experts that run on-premise and output anomaly predictions and failure-domain labels. On BGL, FAME achieves F1 = 98.16 at K = 100 reducing annotation effort by 76x and detects 86.3% of anomalies from unseen EventIDs. On Thunderbird, FAME reaches F1 = 99.95 with perfect recall.

</details>


### [13] [LLM Code Smells: A Taxonomy and Detection Approach](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22976v1)
*Zacharie Chenail-Larcher,Brahim Mahmoudi,Naouel Moha,Quentin Stiévenart,Florent Avellaneda*

TL;DR: 本文提出了LLM代码异味的分类法和检测工具，实验表明这些异味在大多数开源项目中普遍存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不良的LLM集成编程实践会损害软件质量，需要系统化的分类和检测方法以帮助开发者避免这些问题。

Method: 通过整理和细化LLM代码异味的分类法和目录，开发静态代码分析工具SpecDetect4LLM，并在692个开源项目上进行实证评估。

Result: LLM代码异味影响了73.5%的已分析系统，工具检测精确率为91.3%，召回率为71.8%。

Conclusion: LLM代码异味问题普遍存在，所提工具能有效检测这些异味，但仍有改进空间。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）因其多功能性、灵活性和一定程度上模拟人类推理的能力，正越来越多地被集成到软件系统中用于各种目的。然而，在源代码中不佳的LLM推理集成可能会损害软件系统的质量。因此，必须记录不当的LLM集成编码实践，以帮助开发人员减轻此类问题。继我们先前关于LLM代码异味的工作之后，本文通过提出一个独立的分类法和九个LLM代码异味的目录来巩固和细化这一概念。我们还创建了SpecDetect4LLM，一个用于检测这些异味的静态源代码分析工具，并对其检测效果（精确率和召回率）以及LLM代码异味在692个开源软件项目（171,194个源文件）中的普遍性进行了广泛的实证评估。我们的结果表明，LLM代码异味影响了73.5%的被分析系统，检测精确率为91.3%，召回率为71.8%。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into software systems for diverse purposes, due to their versatility, flexibility, and ability to simulate human reasoning to some extent. However, poor integration of LLM inference in source code can undermine software system quality. Therefore, inadequate LLM integration coding practices must be documented to help developers mitigate such issues. Following our earlier work on LLM code smells, this paper consolidates and refines the concept by presenting a self-contained taxonomy and a catalog of nine LLM code smells. We also create SpecDetect4LLM, a static source code analysis tool for their detection, and conduct extensive empirical evaluations of its detection effectiveness (precision and recall) as well as the prevalence of LLM code smells across 692 open-source software projects (171,194 source files). Our results show that LLM code smells affect 73.5% of the analyzed systems, with a detection precision of 91.3% and a recall of 71.8%.

### [14] [Finding Performance Issues in Database Systems by Exploiting Dormant Code Paths](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22992v1)
*Jinsheng Ba,Zhendong Su*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出分支翻转分析（BFA）方法，通过翻转代码分支强制启用或禁用优化来系统性发现数据库性能问题，在四个DBMS上找到21个新问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据库管理系统存在性能问题，但缺乏系统性测试优化的方法，现有黑盒方法无法细粒度测试优化逻辑。

Method: 提出白盒分支翻转分析（BFA），通过翻转代码分支强制启用或禁用优化，若性能显著改善则表明存在性能问题。

Result: 在PostgreSQL、MySQL、CockroachDB和MariaDB上使用TPC-H和TPC-DS基准，发现21个先前未知的性能问题。

Conclusion: BFA是一种简单且通用的方法，可有效发现性能问题并测试优化逻辑，适用于其他软件系统。

中文摘要：性能是基础系统（如数据库管理系统DBMS）的关键特性。学术界和工业界花费了数十年探索高效的优化算法。尽管付出了这些努力，DBMS仍然容易出现性能问题，导致次优性能。由于缺乏真实性能基准，发现此类问题是一个长期挑战。现有工作采用黑盒方法来检查执行过程中的性能一致性，但无法系统性地测试优化。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新颖的、通用的白盒方法——分支翻转分析（BFA），以系统且有效地发现性能问题。BFA翻转代码分支以强制启用或禁用某项优化，预期性能不会显著更好。否则，即存在性能问题。BFA提供了发现性能问题和细粒度测试优化逻辑的新视角。我们在原型系统QueryZen中实现了BFA，并在四个广泛使用且成熟的DBMS上进行了评估：PostgreSQL、MySQL、CockroachDB和MariaDB。QueryZen在使用广泛使用的基准TPC-H和TPC-DS的工作负载中发现了21个先前未知且独特的性能问题。BFA的核心概念简单且广泛适用，并可适用于分析其他软件系统的性能。

Original abstract: Performance is a critical characteristic of fundamental systems, such as Database Management Systems (DBMSs). Both academia and industry have invested decades in exploring efficient optimization algorithms. Despite these efforts, DBMSs are prone to performance issues, which incur suboptimal performance. Finding such issues is a longstanding challenge as no ground-truth performance is available. Existing work adopts black-box methods to examine performance consistency across executions, but cannot systematically test optimizations. In this work, we propose a novel, general white-box methodology, Branch Flip Analysis (BFA), to systematically and effectively uncover performance issues. BFA flips code branches to enforce or disable an optimization, and the performance is expected to be not significantly better. Otherwise, a performance issue exists. BFA provides a new perspective to finding performance issues and testing optimization logics in a fine-grained manner. We realized BFA in a prototype system QueryZen, and evaluated it on four widely-used and mature DBMSs: PostgreSQL, MySQL, CockroachDB, and MariaDB. QueryZen found 21 previously unknown and unique performance issues with the workload of the extensively used benchmarks TPC-H and TPC-DS. The core concept of BFA is simple and broadly applicable, and can be adapted to analyze the performance of other software systems.

### [15] [On the Reliability of Code Comprehension Proxies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23008v1)
*Erfan Arvan,Nadeeshan De Silva,Oscar Chaparro,Martin Kellogg*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过专家共识和学生研究评估了代码理解研究中常用代理的可靠性，发现基于输入输出问题和响应时间的代理更可靠，而基于语法的问题代理不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码理解研究使用不同代理（如李克特评分或输入输出问题）来近似代码可理解性，但其相对可靠性未知，因此需要系统评估。

Method: 进行两项研究：1）专家共识研究，采用德尔菲协议让5名专业工程师对8个代码片段进行排名以建立基准；2）学生研究，44名学生完成14种代理测量任务；对结果进行相关性分析。

Result: 源自输入输出问题的代理和测量响应时间而非准确率的代理特别可靠；源自语法问题的代理无论测量策略如何都特别不可靠。

Conclusion: 研究结果对现有理解性文献的可靠性提出质疑，特别是基于语法的问题部分，并建议优先使用输入输出问题和响应时间测量。

中文摘要：先前关于代码理解的研究使用了不同的理解代理——例如，李克特评分或关于程序片段的输入输出问题的答案，通常从学生中收集，以近似代码是否对软件工程师可理解，但这些代理的相对可靠性尚不清楚。本文通过两项人类研究调查了现有文献中常见的一系列代理的相对可靠性。首先，我们与五位专业软件工程师组成的小组进行了一项专家共识研究，通过改编德尔菲专家共识协议，建立了八个代码片段的真实理解性排名。德尔菲协议在其他领域（如医学和国家安全预测）中广泛用于不确定性条件下的专家共识，但据我们所知，这是其在软件工程中的首次应用。其次，我们进行了一项有44名学生参与者的研究，他们完成了任务，使我们能够测量从文献中得出的关于同一组八个代码片段的14个理解代理。最后，我们对结果进行了相关性分析，得出结论：1）源自输入输出问题的代理和2）测量响应时间而非准确率的代理特别可靠。我们还发现，源自关于程序语法（而非语义）问题的代理特别不可靠，无论测量策略如何，这使现有理解性文献的部分可靠性受到质疑。

Original abstract: Prior work on code comprehension uses different comprehension proxies-for example, Likert-scale ratings or answers to input-output questions about program snippets, usually collected from students, to approximate whether code is comprehensible to software engineers, but the relative reliability of these proxies is not known. This paper investigates the relative reliability of a collection of proxies common in the extant literature with a pair of human studies. First, we conducted an expert-consensus study with a panel of five professional software engineers to establish a ground-truth comprehensibility ranking of eight code snippets by adapting the Delphi expert-consensus protocol. The Delphi protocol is widely used for expert consensus under conditions of uncertainty in other domains, such as medicine and national-security forecasting, but to our knowledge, this is its first application in software engineering. Second, we conducted a study with 44 student participants who completed tasks, allowing us to measure 14 comprehension proxies derived from the literature on the same set of eight code snippets. Finally, we conducted a correlation analysis on the results, concluding that proxies 1) derived from input-output questions and 2) that measure response time rather than accuracy are especially reliable. We also found that proxies derived from questions about program syntax (rather than semantics) are especially unreliable, regardless of measurement strategy, which draws into question the reliability of parts of the existing comprehensibility literature.

</details>


### [16] [Code Smells in Clojure: Initial Findings from a Grey Literature Review](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24049v1)
*Walber Araújo,José Truta,Lucas Vegi,Marco Tulio Valente,João Brunet*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过灰色文献分析，识别了Clojure中的26种代码坏味（12个Clojure特有、9个函数式风格、5个传统坏味），并指出现有linter仅覆盖2种，工具支持严重不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 函数式编程语言中代码坏味研究不足，尤其是Clojure，因此需要通过灰色文献方法探索其代码坏味现象。

Method: 采用灰色文献研究，手动检查Google搜索中的开发者讨论，提取质量关注点，并由44名从业者评估非传统坏味候选的相关性。

Result: 编目了26个代码坏味，包括12个Clojure特定、9个函数式风格和5个传统Fowler坏味；现有Clojure linter仅覆盖2个，工具支持存在显著差距。

Conclusion: 初步描述了Clojure开发者讨论代码坏味的方式，提供了该生态系统的坏味集合，并评估了检测工具支持的不足。

中文摘要：代码坏味是广泛使用的代码质量不佳的指标，揭示结构问题和改进空间。虽然面向对象语言中已广泛研究，函数式编程语言在文献中相对较少探索。本文展示了对Clojure（一种现代函数式编程语言，运行在Java虚拟机（JVM）上，广泛用于开源和工业系统）中代码坏味的灰色文献研究的初步结果。受之前关于Elixir的工作启发，我们手动检查了通过Google搜索检索到的开发者讨论，提取了开发者讨论的质量问题，并让44位从业者评估非传统坏味候选的相关性。作为初步结果，我们编目了26个代码坏味，包括12个Clojure特定、9个函数式风格和5个传统Fowler坏味。我们还分析了工具支持，观察到显著差距，现有Clojure linter只覆盖了这26个坏味中的2个。这些早期发现提供了Clojure开发者如何讨论代码坏味的初步描述，一组初步的特定于该生态系统的坏味问题，以及对其检测工具支持的早期评估。

Original abstract: Code smells are widely used indicators of poor code quality, revealing structural problems and areas where improvement can be made. Although extensively studied in object-oriented languages, functional programming languages remain comparatively underexplored in literature. This paper presents early results from a grey literature investigation of code smells in Clojure, a modern functional programming language that runs on the Java Virtual Machine (JVM) and is widely adopted in open source and industrial systems. Inspired by prior work on Elixir, we manually inspected developer discussions retrieved through Google search, extracted quality concerns discussed by developers, and had 44 practitioners evaluate the relevance of non-traditional smell candidates. As preliminary results, we cataloged 26 code smells, including 12 Clojure-specific, 9 functional-style, and 5 traditional Fowler smells. We also analyzed tool support and observed a significant gap, as existing Clojure linters cover only 2 of these 26 smells. These early findings provide an initial characterization of how Clojure developers discuss code smells, a preliminary set of smell-like problems specific to this ecosystem, and an early assessment of tool support for their detection.

### [17] [A measurement substrate for agentic Kubernetes operations: Methodology and a case study in retrieval-compounding falsification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23058v1)
*Joshua Odmark,Gideon Rubin,Deon van der Vyver*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出agent-breakage框架用于可证伪的Kubernetes运维代理评估，发现检索过去故障分析效果微弱，并揭示常见错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于自主Kubernetes运维代理的实证研究不可证伪，缺乏对照比较、选择偏差普遍、无预注册决策矩阵且样本量小，导致结论不可靠。

Method: 设计agent-breakage闭环测量框架，向Kubernetes集群注入故障，观察代理响应并评分，区分框架错误与推理错误，使用确定性嵌入器实现关闭条件控制，强制执行预注册决策矩阵。

Result: 案例研究中检索过去故障分析的效果部分证伪：1/3显著，合并效果+3.9%，n=60不显著；360次运行显示机制对齐主导。同时发现三个混淆因素（pgvector索引错误、+19%选择偏差、小样本夸大3倍效果）。

Conclusion: 框架开源，强调需要更严格的实验控制来评估Kubernetes运维代理，避免错误发布结论。

中文摘要：关于自主Kubernetes运维代理的实证主张在很大程度上是不可证伪的。已发表的工作报告了观察性结果，但没有与禁用代理的基线进行对照比较，选择偏差普遍存在，缺乏预注册的决策矩阵，并且样本通常太小，无法适应底层评分系统的噪声水平。原因在于限制代理本身的同一个差距：代码代理有一个验证基础，可以将“是否有效”转化为快速、可证伪的、真实信号，而运维中没有等效的东西。我们提出了agent-breakage，这是一个闭环测量框架，它向目标Kubernetes集群注入故障，观察自主代理如何响应，根据真实情况从四个维度对响应进行评分，并累积结果标签（状态、动作、结果）元组。该框架区分框架错误和推理错误，通过确定性嵌入器机制支持真正的关闭条件控制，并强制执行预注册的决策矩阵。我们将其作为案例研究，测试检索过去的故障分析是否增强代理的能力。方法论上的收获是该基础在那个案例研究中捕捉到的三个混淆因素，每一个都会在同一个工作但较少检测的版本上产生错误的已发表主张：一个pgvector索引错误，一个+19%的选择偏差伪影，以及将效果夸大约3倍的小样本估计。检索结果本身是一个部分证伪：3个密集语料场景中有1个在p<0.05显著，合并效应+3.9个百分点，在n=60时不显著。在360次运行的场景内语料密度扫描显示，近邻的机制对齐主导了原始计数。该框架已开源发布。

Original abstract: Empirical claims about autonomous Kubernetes operations agents are largely unfalsifiable. Published work reports observational results without controlled comparisons against an agent-disabled baseline, selection bias is endemic, pre-registered decision matrices are absent, and samples are typically too small for the noise level of the underlying scoring system. The cause is the same gap that limits the agents themselves: code agents have a verification substrate that turns "did it work" into a fast, falsifiable, ground-truth signal, and operations has nothing equivalent. We present agent-breakage, a closed-loop measurement framework that injects faults into a target Kubernetes cluster, observes how an autonomous agent responds, scores the response on four axes against ground truth, and accumulates outcome-labeled (state, action, outcome) tuples. The framework distinguishes framework error from reasoning error, supports a true off-condition control via a deterministic-embedder mechanism, and enforces pre-registered decision matrices. We use it as a case study to test whether retrieval over past postmortems compounds an agent's capability. The methodological payload is three confounds the substrate caught during that case study, each of which would have produced a wrong published claim on a less instrumented version of the same work: a pgvector index bug, a +19% selection-bias artifact, and small-sample estimates that overstated effects by roughly 3x. The retrieval result itself is a partial falsification: 1 of 3 dense-corpus scenarios significant at p<0.05, pooled effect +3.9 percentage points, not significant at n=60. A within-scenario corpus-density sweep at 360 runs shows that mechanistic alignment of near-neighbors dominates raw count. The framework is released open source.

</details>


### [18] [Security of LLM-generated Code: A Comparative Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23091v1)
*Srivathsan G Morkonda,Mahmoud Selim,Hala Assal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究实证评估了七个流行LLM生成代码的安全性，发现所有模型生成的代码均包含严重或高危漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI工具被广泛使用以提高生产力，但其生成的代码存在安全风险，本文聚焦于软件安全风险。

Method: 基于先前工作，模拟开发者使用LLM生成代码的行为，并评估七个流行LLM生成代码的安全性。

Result: 所有七个LLM生成的代码均包含漏洞，且大多数为严重或高危级别。

Conclusion: LLM生成的代码存在严重安全漏洞，需警惕其风险。

中文摘要：大多数软件开发者正在使用或计划在其开发过程中使用人工智能（AI）工具。他们的首要原因包括提高生产力和加速学习。事实上，大型语言模型（LLM）生成的代码已投入生产，包括在主要科技公司中。然而，人们也对使用AI工具生成代码相关的风险提出了担忧。在本文中，我们将注意力集中在软件安全风险上。我们实证评估了七个流行LLM生成的代码的安全性。我们基于先前的工作，模拟开发人员使用LLM生成代码时的行为。我们的结果表明，我们评估的所有七个LLM都会生成包含漏洞的代码，其中大多数漏洞属于严重或高危级别。

Original abstract: The majority of software developers use or are planning to use Artificial Intelligence (AI) tools in their development processes. Their top reasons include improving productivity and faster learning. In fact, Large Language Model (LLM)-generated code is currently in production, including in major tech companies. However, concerns were raised about the risks associated with the use of AI tools to generate code. In this paper, we focus our attention on the risks to software security. We empirically evaluate the security of code generated by seven popular LLMs. We build upon previous work to mimic the behaviours of developers when using LLMs to generate code. Our results show that all seven LLMs that we have evaluated generate code that contains vulnerabilities, the majority of which are of critical or high severity.

</details>


### [19] [More Skills, Worse Agents? Skill Shadowing Degrades Performance When Expanding Skill Libraries](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24050v2)
*Hongwen Song,Song Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文发现技能库扩大会导致LLM代理性能下降，主要原因是技能选择错误（技能遮蔽），而非上下文开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决非专家用户通过自然语言使用技能库时性能随库规模下降的问题。

Method: 将性能下降分解为技能遮蔽和上下文开销两种效应，并推导它们的上界以量化影响。

Result: 技能遮蔽效应随库大小增长且显著，上下文开销效应小且不显著。

Conclusion: 技能选择失败是扩展技能库的主要瓶颈。

中文摘要：技能库允许LLM代理按需加载任务特定指令，让非专家用户通过自然语言解决领域特定任务，而无需知道存在哪些技能或它们如何工作。然而，随着库的扩大，性能会下降——当从一小套有帮助的技能扩展到包含202个技能的库时，性能下降高达21%。在这项工作中，我们将这种性能下降公式化为从加载已知有帮助的技能库到完整库之间的通过率下降。此外，我们提出通过以技能调用为条件——即代理在轨迹中选择哪些技能——将通过率下降分解为两种效应：技能遮蔽（skill shadowing），即随着库的扩展，代理更频繁地选择错误技能；以及上下文开销（context overhead），即即使选择正确，扩大的上下文也会降低执行性能。我们推导了这两种效应的上界，以表征它们对通过率下降的影响程度。我们的经验估计和上界都表明，技能遮蔽效应随着库的大小而增长，并且显著地导致了性能下降，而上下文开销效应仍然很小且与零无法区分。这种观察到的不对称性表明，技能选择失败，而不是扩大的上下文，是扩展技能库时的主要瓶颈。

Original abstract: Skill libraries allow LLM agents to load task-specific instructions on demand, letting non-expert users solve domain-specific tasks through natural language without knowing which skills exist or how they work. However, performance degrades as libraries grow -- by up to 21\% when scaling from a small set of helpful skills to a 202-skill library. In this work, we formulate this performance degradation as the pass rate drop between loading a library of known-helpful skills and the full library. Moreover, we propose to decompose the pass rate drop by conditioning on the skill(s) invocation -- which skills the agent selects during a trajectory -- into two effects: \emph{skill shadowing}, where the agent selects wrong skills more often as the library expands, and \emph{context overhead}, where the enlarged context degrades execution even when selection is correct. We derive upper bounds on both effects to characterize their magnitudes of impacts to the pass rate drop. Our empirical estimates of the effects and their upper bounds both show that the \emph{skill shadowing} effect grows with library size and significantly contributes to the performance degradation, whereas the \emph{context overhead} effect remains small and indistinguishable from zero. This observed asymmetry establishes that the skill selection failure, not the enlarged context, is the primary bottleneck when expanding the skill libraries.

</details>


### [20] [Philosophical Dispositions as Behavioral Constraints for AI-Assisted Code Review: An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23108v1)
*Kaushal Bansal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一种通过哲学倾向（如怀疑论、逻辑学等）约束AI代码审查行为的方法，评估表明能产生独特且有效的发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI代码审查工具产生同质化发现，缺乏针对不同分析类型的适应性，需要更灵活和多样化的审查视角。

Method: 设计基于多种哲学传统的倾向系统，每种倾向有否定定义、自我监控失败模式和顺序角色协议；在50个PR上评估，并对比通用提示。

Result: 倾向系统与人类评审收敛46%，独特发现率75%，无假阳性；51%的发现不来自通用提示，且聚焦结构/操作/逻辑问题；跨模型验证显示框架约束有效。

Conclusion: 基于哲学倾向的约束方法能有效引导AI生成多样且高质量的代码审查发现，优于通用专家模式。

中文摘要：AI辅助代码审查工具通常以通用“专家审阅者”代理的方式运行，无论所需分析类型如何，都会产生同质化的结果。我们提出了一种系统，通过哲学倾向约束AI审阅者的行为——这些倾向是基于特定认识论传统（皮浪怀疑论、正理逻辑、犬儒主义、儒家关系伦理）的一致人格视角，将注意力引导到结构上不同类型的问题。每种倾向都是通过否定的方式（即它拒绝做什么）来定义，配备有自我监控的失败模式（hamartia），并通过角色协议按顺序编排。我们在50个合并的拉取请求上评估了这个系统，这些请求来自7个代码库，涵盖5种编程语言（Python、Go、C++、Java、Terraform）、5个组织（2个企业、3个开源）以及2个时间时代（AI前的2020年，AI后的2024—2026年）。该倾向系统与人类审阅者的收敛率为46%（验证了信号质量），以75%的比率识别出独特发现，并且在601个总发现中，没有发现被作者判定为假阳性（未评估评分者间一致性，这是一个局限性）。受控基线比较表明，51%的倾向发现并非由同一模型使用通用“专家审阅者”提示产生，并且这些独特发现针对的是结构性、操作性和逻辑性问题，而非标准代码级别的问题。初步跨模型验证（Claude Opus vs. GPT Codex 5.3-xhigh）在3个PR上显示100%的框架结构遵循度，发现级别一致性为39%，表明该框架提供了真实的行为约束，同时保留了模型特定的分析视角。

Original abstract: AI-assisted code review tools typically operate as generic "expert reviewer" agents, producing homogeneous findings regardless of the analysis type needed. We present a system that constrains AI reviewer behavior through philosophical dispositions -- coherent personality lenses grounded in specific epistemological traditions (Pyrrhonist Skepticism, Navya-Ny=aya logic, Diogenes' Cynicism, Confucian relational ethics) that direct attention to structurally different types of issues. Each disposition is defined apophatically (by what it refuses to do), equipped with a self-monitoring failure mode (hamartia), and orchestrated in sequence by role protocols.
  We evaluate this system on 50 merged pull requests across 7 repositories spanning 5 programming languages (Python, Go, C++, Java, Terraform), 5 organizations (2 enterprise, 3 open-source), and 2 temporal eras (pre-AI 2020, post-AI 2024--2026). The disposition system achieves 46% convergence with human reviewers (validating signal quality), identifies unique findings at a 75% rate, and produces no findings judged false-positive by the author across 601 total findings (inter-rater agreement was not assessed and remains a limitation). A controlled baseline comparison demonstrates that 51% of disposition findings are not produced by the same model using generic "expert reviewer" prompting, and these unique findings target structural, operational, and logical concerns rather than standard code-level issues. Preliminary cross-model validation (Claude Opus vs.\ GPT Codex 5.3-xhigh) on 3 PRs shows 100% framework-structure adherence with 39% finding-level agreement, suggesting the framework provides real behavioral constraint while preserving model-specific analytical perspective.

</details>

### [21] [ImProver 2: Iteratively Self-Improving LMs for Neurosymbolic Proof Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22885v1)
*Riyaz Ahuja,Tate Rowney,Jeremy Avigad,Sean Welleck*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 神经符号框架自动优化形式证明，与代码优化类似且含自我改进agent。

TL;DR: 提出了ImProver 2，一个用于Lean 4自动证明优化的神经符号框架，通过专家迭代和脚手架训练小模型，使其性能超越大模型并与前沿模型竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化数学库快速扩展，需要重构证明以维护和提高训练数据质量，但面临目标异构、数据稀缺和成本高昂的挑战。

Method: ImProver 2结合数据高效的专家迭代流水线和暴露形式结构与轻量级非正式抽象的脚手架，并引入证明结构属性度量标准。

Result: 训练的7B参数模型优于同系列更大模型，与中端前沿模型竞争力相当；神经符号脚手架显著提升小型和前沿模型性能。

Conclusion: 证明优化是可扩展、可学习的任务，通过适当脚手架和训练，小模型能有效重构研究级证明，匹配更大系统。

中文摘要：形式化数学库正在迅速扩展，这日益需要重构已验证的证明以保持可维护性，并提高神经证明器的训练数据质量。然而，可扩展的证明优化受到异构且启发式指定的目标、稀缺的数据以及高训练和推理成本的阻碍。为了克服这些挑战，我们引入了ImProver 2，这是一个用于在Lean 4中自动证明优化的神经符号框架。ImProver 2结合了一个数据高效的专家迭代流水线和一个暴露形式结构以及轻量级非正式抽象的脚手架。我们进一步引入了一套捕捉证明结构属性的度量标准。使用ImProver 2，我们训练了一个7B参数的模型，其在同一模型家族中优于数量级更大的模型，并在各项度量中与中端前沿模型具有竞争力。我们还证明了我们的神经符号脚手架显著提高了小型和前沿模型的性能。我们表明，通过适当的脚手架和训练，小型模型可以在复杂多样的度量标准上有效地重构研究级别的证明，与更大的系统相匹配，并将证明优化确立为一个可扩展、可学习的任务。

Original abstract: Formal mathematics libraries are rapidly expanding, creating a growing need to refactor verified proofs for maintainability and to improve training data quality for neural provers. However, scalable proof optimization is hindered by heterogeneous and heuristically specified objectives, scarce data, and high training and inference costs. To overcome these challenges, we introduce ImProver 2, a neurosymbolic framework for automated proof optimization in Lean 4. ImProver 2 combines a data-efficient expert-iteration pipeline with a scaffold that exposes formal structure alongside lightweight informal abstractions. We further introduce a suite of metrics capturing structural proof properties. Using ImProver 2, we train a 7B-parameter model that outperforms orders-of-magnitude larger models within the same model family, and is competitive with mid-tier frontier models across metrics. We additionally demonstrate that our neurosymbolic scaffold significantly improves performance across both small and frontier models. We show that with proper scaffolding and training, small models can effectively restructure research-level proofs over complex and varied metrics, matching substantially larger systems and establishing proof optimization as a scalable, learnable task.

</details>


### [22] [Planning in the LLM Era: Building for Reliability and Efficiency](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21902v1)
*Michael Katz,Harsha Kokel,Kavitha Srinivas,Shirin Sohrabi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 综述LLM规划方法，分析可靠性与效率，对agent规划设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文认为LLM用于规划的趋势已从直接规划转向生成可验证的符号求解器，以提高可靠性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期LLM规划方法存在不健全、不完备、资源消耗大等问题，需要更可靠高效的规划方法。

Method: 考察了三大类规划器生成方法，分析其局限性，并提出未来研究方向。

Result: 总结了当前趋势和局限性，但未提供具体实验结果。

Conclusion: LLM时代规划领域正在重新调整，朝向生成可维护、低依赖的规划器。

中文摘要：随着对智能体的日益关注，其核心能力之一——规划——成为焦点。早期利用大型语言模型（LLM）进行规划的尝试依赖于单次规划生成，随后出现了将LLM与有限外部搜索相结合的混合方法。这些方法本质上不健全且不完备，通常需要大量资源，却未能在未见问题上产生更好的解决方案。随着LLM局限性的日益明显，近期工作转向在解决方案构建时使用它们——为一系列可验证的问题生成符号求解器，然后在推理时高效使用。这一趋势反映出对既可靠又资源高效的智能体的需求日益增长。它也提供了一条路径，以生成在推理时对语言模型依赖最小的可维护规划器。在本文中，我们认为这一转变反映了LLM时代规划领域的更广泛重新调整。我们考察了三大类规划器生成方法，讨论了它们当前的局限性，并勾勒出迈向更可靠、更高效的基于LLM的规划器生成的研究步骤。

Original abstract: Growing attention to intelligent agents has put a spotlight on one of their central capabilities: planning. Early attempts to leverage large language models (LLMs) for planning relied on single-shot plan generation, followed by hybrid approaches that coupled LLMs with limited external search. These methods, unsound and incomplete by their very nature, often require substantial resources without yielding better solutions on unseen problems. As the limitations of LLMs become clearer, recent work has shifted toward using them at solution construction time -- generating symbolic solvers for a family of problems that can be verified and then used efficiently at inference time. This trend reflects the growing need for agents that are both reliable and resource-efficient. It also offers a path towards generating maintainable planners with minimal dependence on language models at inference time. In this paper, we argue that this shift reflects a broader realignment of the planning field in the LLM era. We examine three major categories of planner-generation methods, discuss their current limitations, and outline research steps towards a more reliable and efficient LLM-based generation of planners.

</details>


### [23] [AI-Enabled Serious Games: Integrating Intelligence and Adaptivity in Training Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21962v1)
*Priyamvada Tripathi,Bill Kapralos*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 综述AI在严肃游戏中的智能与适应，涉及LLM/RL/agent架构，有通用启发。

TL;DR: 本章探讨AI如何支持严肃游戏的实时教学适应，区分教学智能与适应性，综述历史发展，并讨论LLM、RL和智能体架构的贡献与挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 严肃游戏存在静态设计、创作瓶颈、有限建模和适应困难等问题，AI提供新能力但带来新挑战，需要系统分析其支持实时教学适应的潜力与问题。

Method: 通过历史综合自适应学习系统发展（从CAI到ITS、DDA、学习分析等），并基于此分析LLM、RL和智能体架构在严肃游戏中的应用。

Result: 识别了AI在动态场景、反馈、节奏、学习者建模方面的潜力，以及可解释性、验证、成本等挑战，指出目前缺乏长期学习效果的实证。

Conclusion: AI有望提升严肃游戏的智能与适应性，但需克服诸多挑战，未来需更多实证研究验证其学习效果。

中文摘要：严肃游戏广泛应用于医疗、国防和教育等领域的学习和培训。然而，仍然存在持续挑战，包括静态场景设计、创作瓶颈、有限的学习者建模以及难以实现有意义的实时教学适应。人工智能的最新进展引入了动态场景变化、情境反馈、自适应节奏和学习者状态建模等新能力，可能有助于解决其中一些局限性。与此同时，将人工智能融入严肃游戏引发了与有效性、透明度、系统控制和学习者信任相关的重要问题。本章探讨了当代人工智能方法如何支持严肃游戏中的实时教学适应。它区分了教学智能（定义为系统推断学习者知识并推理出教学上适当反应的能力）和适应性（定义为在交互过程中修改教学行动的能力）。本文对自适应学习系统进行了历史性综合，追溯了从早期计算机辅助教学到智能辅导系统、动态难度调整、创作平台、学习分析以及近期人工智能支持架构的发展。基于这一视角，本章讨论了大型语言模型、强化学习和基于智能体的架构如何可能为严肃游戏带来更集成形式的智能和适应性。它还强调了人工智能支持系统相关的实践和研究挑战，包括可解释性、验证、计算成本以及关于人工智能支持严肃游戏中长期学习成果的有限经验证据。

Original abstract: Serious games are widely used for learning and training across domains such as healthcare, defense, and education. Persistent challenges remain, however, including static scenario design, authoring bottlenecks, limited learner modeling, and difficulty implementing meaningful real-time instructional adaptation. Recent advances in artificial intelligence (AI) introduce novel capabilities such as dynamic scenario variation, contextual feedback, adaptive pacing, and learner-state modeling that may help address some of these limitations. At the same time, integrating AI into serious games raises important questions related to validity, transparency, system control, and learner trust. This chapter examines how contemporary AI approaches may support real-time instructional adaptation in serious games. It distinguishes between instructional intelligence, defined as a system's capacity to infer learner knowledge and reason about pedagogically appropriate responses, and adaptivity, defined as the ability to modify instructional actions during interaction. A historical synthesis of adaptive learning systems is presented, tracing developments from early computer-assisted instruction through intelligent tutoring systems (ITS), dynamic difficulty adjustment (DDA), authoring platforms, learning analytics, and recent AI-enabled architectures. Building on this perspective, the chapter discusses how large language models (LLMs), reinforcement learning (RL), and agent-based architectures may contribute to more integrated forms of intelligence and adaptivity in serious games. It also highlights practical and research challenges associated with AI-enabled systems, including explainability, validation, computational cost, and the limited empirical evidence regarding long-term learning outcomes in AI-enabled serious games.

### [24] [Echo: Learning from Experience Data via User-Driven Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21984v1)
*Hande Dong,Xiaoyun Liang,Jiarui Yu,Jiayi Lin,Changqing Ai,Feng Liu,Wenjun Zhang,Rongbi Wei,Chaofan Zhu,Linjie Che,Feng Wu,Xin Shen,Dexu Kong,Xiaotian Wang,Qiuyuan Chen,Bingxu An,Yueting Lei,Qiang Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: Echo框架利用用户反馈改进代码补全agent，直接相关coding agent优化。

TL;DR: Echo框架通过收集用户完善序列中的高质量训练信号，将原始经验转化为可学习知识，在代码补全任务中将接受率从25.7%提升至35.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态人类数据扩展成本高且受限于创建者知识，而原始经验数据噪声大、信息密度低，不适合直接训练模型，因此需要一种方法将原始经验转化为可学习的知识。

Method: 提出Echo框架，系统收集用户驱动的完善序列（用户将智能体错误提案转化为正确解决方案的过程），从中提取高质量训练信号，用于持续调整模型。

Result: 在代码补全生产环境中，接受率从25.7%提升至35.7%，突破了静态性能上限。

Conclusion: Echo能够有效利用用户完善反馈，将智能体的粗糙尝试转化为训练信号，持续对齐真实需求，提升模型性能。

中文摘要：静态的“人类数据”面临固有限制：扩展成本高昂，且受限于其创造者的知识。从“经验数据”——智能体与其环境之间的交互——中持续学习有望突破这些障碍。如今，AI智能体的广泛部署使我们能够以低成本获取海量的此类真实世界经验流。然而，原始的交互日志本质上是嘈杂的，充满了试错和低信息密度，使得它们无法直接用于高效的模型训练。
  我们引入了Echo，一个通用框架，旨在实现从原始经验到可学习知识的转化，有效地将环境反馈“回响”到训练循环中以进行模型优化。在当前的智能体生态系统中，用户完善是此类反馈的主要来源：出于对结果的责任感，用户严格地将有缺陷的智能体提案转化为经过验证的解决方案。这些用户驱动的完善序列本质上将智能体的粗糙尝试提炼为高质量的训练信号。Echo系统地收集这些信号，以持续将智能体与真实世界的需求对齐。在一个代码补全的生产环境中的大规模验证证实，Echo有效地利用了这一流程，将接受率从25.7%提升至35.7%，突破了静态性能上限。

Original abstract: Static "human data" faces inherent limitations: it is expensive to scale and bounded by the knowledge of its creators. Continuous learning from "experience data" - interactions between agents and their environments - promises to transcend these barriers. Today, the widespread deployment of AI agents grants us low-cost access to massive streams of such real-world experience. However, raw interaction logs are inherently noisy, filled with trial-and-error and low information density, rendering them inefficient for direct model training.
  We introduce Echo, a generalized framework designed to operationalize the transition from raw experience to learnable knowledge, effectively "echoing" environmental feedback back into the training loop for model optimization. In today's agent ecosystem, user refinement serves as a primary source of such feedback: driven by responsibility for the outcome, users rigorously transform flawed agent proposals into verified solutions. These user-driven refinement sequences inherently distill agents' crude attempts into high-quality training signals. Echo systematically harvests these signals to continuously align the agent with real-world needs. Large-scale validation in a production code completion environment confirms that Echo effectively harnesses this pipeline, breaking the static performance ceiling by increasing the acceptance rate from 25.7% to 35.7%.

</details>


### [25] [The Log is the Agent: Event-Sourced Reactive Graphs for Auditable, Forkable Agentic Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21997v1)
*Yohei Nakajima*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出事件溯源反应图作为agent运行时，可审计可fork，对agent架构有启发。

TL;DR: ActiveGraph通过将仅追加事件日志作为真相来源，工作图作为确定性投影，行为响应图变化，实现了确定性重放、廉价分叉和端到端谱系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体框架以语言模型为中心，状态可检索但缺乏确定性重放和完整谱系，ActiveGraph通过反转设计解决这些问题。

Method: 以仅追加事件日志为源，工作图为确定性投影，行为响应图变化并发出新事件，组件间通过共享图协调。

Result: 实现了确定性重放、廉价分叉和端到端谱系，并通过勤奋示例验证其因果关系可重构。

Conclusion: ActiveGraph基底特别适合自我改进智能体，并扩展了BabyAGI和图记忆研究，但未完全证明其优势。

中文摘要：大多数智能体框架都围绕语言模型构建：首先是对话循环，然后是工具，接着是规则，最后为了可观测性而添加日志层，状态则作为可检索的“记忆”持久化。我们描述了ActiveGraph，一个反转了这种安排的运行时。仅追加的事件日志是真相来源；工作图是该日志的确定性投影；而行为——普通函数、类、基于LLM的例程或附加到类型化边上的逻辑——响应图中的变化并发出新事件。没有组件指令另一个组件；协调完全通过共享图进行。这一单一设计决策产生了检索与总结记忆系统无法提供的三个特性：从日志中确定性重放任何运行、在任意事件处分支运行而无需重新执行共享前缀的廉价分叉，以及从高层目标向下到产生每个工件单个模型调用的端到端谱系。我们介绍了该架构、使重放正确的确定性契约，以及一个完整的因果关系结构仅从日志中即可重构的勤奋示例。我们讨论——但不声称证明——为什么这个基底特别适合自我改进的智能体，以及它如何扩展了BabyAGI系列和之前的图记忆研究。

Original abstract: Most agent frameworks are built around the language model: a conversation loop comes first, then tools, then rules, and finally a logging layer bolted on for observability, with state persisted as retrievable "memory." We describe ActiveGraph, a runtime that inverts this arrangement. The append-only event log is the source of truth; the working graph is a deterministic projection of that log; and behaviors--ordinary functions, classes, LLM-backed routines, or logic attached to typed edges--react to changes in the graph and emit new events. No component instructs another; coordination happens entirely through the shared graph. This single design decision yields three properties that retrieval-and-summarization memory systems do not provide: deterministic replay of any run from its log, cheap forking that branches a run at any event without re-executing the shared prefix, and end-to-end lineage from a high-level goal down to the individual model call that produced each artifact. We present the architecture, a determinism contract that makes replay sound, and a worked diligence example whose full causal structure is reconstructable from the log alone. We discuss--without claiming to demonstrate--why this substrate is unusually well suited to self-improving agents, and how it extends the BabyAGI lineage and prior graph-memory research.

Original abstract: Large language models perform well on static medical examinations, yet clinical diagnosis often requires iterative evidence gathering under uncertainty. Across 468 cases and 15 models in our protocol, we observe that multi-turn evidence seeking reduces diagnostic accuracy by 12.75% and lowers supporting-evidence quality by 24.36% relative to full-context evaluation; error analyses associate these drops with premature diagnostic closure and inefficient questioning. Together, these results suggest that static full-context benchmarks may overestimate performance in interactive evidence-seeking settings, motivating complementary interactive assessment for safer clinical decision support.

### [27] [ExComm: Exploration-Stage Communication for Error-Resilient Agentic Test-Time Scaling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22102v1)
*Woomin Song,Beomjun Kim,Daewon Choi,Sai Muralidhar Jayanthi,Saket Dingliwal,Jinwoo Shin,Aram Galstyan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出ExComm通信协议用于agent测试时缩放，通过跨agent冲突检测和反馈实现错误恢复，直接贡献agent可靠性。

TL;DR: ExComm是一个用于代理测试时扩展的通信协议，通过检测和解决跨代理事实冲突并引入轨迹多样化来减少错误传播，在多个基准测试中优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时间跨度代理测试时扩展中错误传播是关键失败模式，现有方法控制有限，依赖代理自行纠错或事后优化。

Method: 提出ExComm协议，定期审计代理信念状态检测跨代理事实冲突，通过工具验证循环解决冲突，以软信念更新整合反馈，并引入轨迹多样化模块防止多样性崩溃。

Result: 在AIME 2024、AIME 2025和GAIA上，ExComm分别比最佳基线平均提升5.7%和5.0%，并展现出更好的错误恢复、缩放行为、多样性和性能-成本权衡。

Conclusion: ExComm有效提升了代理测试时扩展的鲁棒性和性能，通过主动冲突检测与解决及轨迹多样化实现了优于现有方法的效果。

中文摘要：在长时间跨度的代理测试时扩展中，一个常见的失败模式是错误传播，即在中间步骤引入的事实错误或无效推理会持续存在于代理的信念状态中，并污染后续推理。现有的测试时扩展方法对此过程的控制有限，因为它们通常依赖代理自行检测错误、在有缺陷的轨迹中进行选择，或者仅在错误已经形成推理路径后才进行优化。我们提出了ExComm，一种用于探索阶段代理测试时扩展的通信协议。ExComm的动机来自实证观察：并行代理推理中的大多数中间错误会产生可检测的跨代理事实冲突。利用代理工作流的迭代结构，ExComm定期审计代理的信念状态以检测此类冲突，通过专用的基于工具的验证循环解决冲突，并向相关代理返回简洁、有针对性的反馈。纠正通过软信念更新来整合，即附加经过验证的反馈，而不是覆盖现有信念。此外，为了防止因通信导致轨迹多样性崩溃，ExComm进一步引入了轨迹多样化模块，将冗余轨迹重定向到正交策略。在AIME 2024、AIME 2025和GAIA上使用Gemini-2.5-Flash-Lite和Qwen3.5-4B进行的实验表明，ExComm持续优于强大的测试时扩展基线，分别比最佳性能基线平均提高了5.7%和5.0%。进一步的分析表明，ExComm具有更好的错误恢复能力、有利的缩放行为、比经过调整的通信基线更强的多样性，以及在评估方法中最佳的性能-成本权衡。

Original abstract: A common failure mode in long-horizon agentic test-time scaling is error propagation, where factual errors or invalid deductions introduced at intermediate steps persist in the agent's belief state and contaminate later reasoning. Existing test-time scaling methods provide limited control over this process, as they often rely on agents to detect their own mistakes, select among flawed trajectories, or refine solutions only after errors have already shaped the reasoning path. We propose ExComm, a communication protocol for exploration-stage agentic test-time scaling. ExComm is motivated by the empirical observation that the majority of intermediate errors in parallel agentic reasoning produce detectable cross-agent factual conflicts. Leveraging the iterative structure of agentic workflows, ExComm periodically audits agent belief states to detect such conflicts, resolves them through a dedicated tool-based verification loop, and returns concise, targeted feedback to the involved agents. Corrections are incorporated through soft belief updates, which append verified feedback rather than overwriting existing beliefs. Furthermore, to prevent collapsing trajectory diversity due to communication, ExComm further introduces a trajectory diversification module that redirects redundant trajectories toward orthogonal strategies. Experiments on AIME 2024, AIME 2025, and GAIA with Gemini-2.5-Flash-Lite and Qwen3.5-4B show that ExComm consistently outperforms strong test-time scaling baselines, achieving average performance gains of 5.7% and 5.0% over the best-performing baselines, respectively. Further analyses demonstrate improved error recovery, favorable scaling behavior, stronger diversity than adapted communication baselines, and the best performance-cost trade-off among the evaluated methods.

### [28] [ArborKV: Structure-Aware KV Cache Management for Scaling Tree-based LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22106v1)
*Yeqiu Chen,Ziyan Liu,Zhenxin Huang,Runquan Gui,Hong Wang,Lei Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 结构感知KV缓存管理支持树搜索推理，对agent推理效率有启发。

TL;DR: 提出ArborKV，一种结构感知的KV缓存逐出框架，通过利用搜索动态实现高达4倍的内存节省，同时保持准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Tree-of-Thoughts推理中KV缓存占用成为内存瓶颈，限制搜索深度和宽度。

Method: 基于搜索动态，设计轻量级价值估计器和树感知分配策略，执行标记提取逐出和惰性重补水。

Result: 在ToT基准上实现约4倍峰值KV内存减少，精度接近完全保留。

Conclusion: ArborKV有效缓解内存瓶颈，支持更大搜索配置而无需额外硬件。

中文摘要：近期大语言模型推理的进展越来越从单次生成转向对中间推理状态的显式搜索。树思维（ToT）将推理组织为具有分支和回溯的树结构搜索，但这显著放大了键值（KV）缓存：为前沿的部分轨迹保留KV状态很快成为内存瓶颈，限制了吞吐量，并在固定硬件预算下约束了搜索深度和宽度。我们通过观察到ToT风格推理中的KV复用受搜索动态支配来解决这一挑战：近期解码主要依赖于活动分支及其祖先，而非活跃子树短期复用概率低，但仍需可恢复以进行回溯。受此启发，我们提出了ArborKV，一种结构感知的逐出框架，它将轻量级价值估计器与树感知分配策略相结合，并执行纯标记提取逐出和惰性重补水以支持重访。在ToT风格推理基准上的实验表明，ArborKV实现了高达约4倍的峰值KV内存减少，同时保持接近完全保留的准确性，使得在固定设备预算下能够运行原本会耗尽内存的更大搜索配置。

Original abstract: Recent progress in LLM reasoning has increasingly shifted from single-pass generation to explicit search over intermediate reasoning states. Tree-of-Thoughts (ToT) organizes inference to tree-structured search with branching and backtracking, but it substantially amplifies the Key--Value (KV) cache: retaining KV states for a frontier of partial trajectories quickly becomes a memory bottleneck that limits throughput and constrains search depth and width under fixed hardware budgets. We address this challenge by observing that KV reuse in ToT-style inference is governed by search dynamics: near-term decoding depends primarily on the active branch and its ancestors, whereas inactive subtrees have low short-term reuse probability yet must remain recoverable for backtracking. Motivated by this, we propose ArborKV, a structure-aware eviction framework that couples a lightweight value estimator with a tree-aware allocation policy, and performs purely token-extractive eviction with lazy rehydration to support revisits. Experiments on ToT-style reasoning benchmarks show that ArborKV achieves up to ~4x peak KV-memory reduction while preserving near-full-retention accuracy, enabling larger search configurations under fixed device budgets that would otherwise run out of memory.

### [29] [Efficient Agentic Reasoning Through Self-Regulated Simulative Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22138v1)
*Mingkai Deng,Jinyu Hou,Lara Sá Neves,Varad Pimpalkhute,Taylor W. Killian,Zhengzhong Liu,Eric P. Xing*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自调节模拟规划框架，将agent推理分解为模拟、调节、执行，直接适用于agent设计。

TL;DR: 提出一种自我调节的模拟推理代理方法，通过将决策分解为模拟推理、自我调节和反应执行三个系统，在LLM的思维链中实现高效规划，显著减少推理令牌使用且性能与超大模型竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端训练的反应式代理缺乏对规划的存在、结构或深度的控制，导致推理长度不必要地增加，令牌使用效率低下且准确性提升不可靠。

Method: 将决策分解为三个系统：模拟推理（系统II，基于世界模型预测未来状态）、自我调节（系统III，学习配置器决定规划时机和深度）和反应执行（系统I，处理细粒度动作）。实例化为SR^2^AM模型，在LLM思维链中实现两个版本：v0.1基于提示式多模块系统记录决策，v1.0从预训练LLM推理轨迹重建结构化规划，并通过监督学习和强化学习训练。

Result: 在数学、科学、表格分析和网络搜索任务上，v0.1-8B和v1.0-30B的Pass@1分别与120-355B和685B-1T参数系统相当；v1.0-30B比可比代理型LLM减少25.8-95.3%推理令牌；强化学习使平均规划深度增加22.8%，规划频率仅增2.0%。

Conclusion: 学习到的自我调节原则可扩展到代理管理自身学习与适应的更广泛场景，而不仅限于规划。

中文摘要：代理应如何决定何时以及如何规划？一种主流方法是将代理构建为具有自适应计算（例如，思维链）的反应式策略，通过端到端训练期望规划隐式涌现。由于无法控制规划的存在、结构或深度，这些系统会大幅增加推理长度，导致令牌使用效率低下且无法带来可靠的准确性提升。我们认为，高效的代理推理得益于将决策过程分解为三个系统：模拟推理（系统II）通过世界模型将深思熟虑建立在未来状态预测之上；自我调节（系统III）通过一个学习到的配置器决定何时以及以多深的程度进行规划；以及反应式执行（系统I）处理细粒度动作。模拟推理在无需针对每个领域进行工程的情况下为多样化任务提供统一规划，而自我调节确保仅在需要时调用规划器。为验证这一观点，我们开发了SR$^2$AM（自调节模拟推理代理型LLM），将两者作为LLM思维链中的不同阶段实现，其中LLM充当世界模型。我们探索了两种实例化：从提示式多模块系统中记录决策（v0.1）以及从预训练推理LLM的轨迹中重建结构化规划（v1.0），并通过监督学习随后进行强化学习（RL）训练。在数学、科学、表格分析和网络信息检索等任务中，v0.1-8B和v1.0-30B分别达到了与120-355B和685B-1T参数系统相当的Pass@1性能，同时v1.0-30B比可比代理型LLM使用的推理令牌减少了25.8-95.3%。强化学习使平均规划深度增加了22.8%，而规划频率仅增加了2.0%，表明它学会了更远地规划而非更频繁地规划。更广泛地，学习到的自我调节实现了一个原则，我们期望该原则能从规划扩展到代理如何管理自身的学习与适应。

Original abstract: How should an agent decide when and how to plan? A dominant approach builds agents as reactive policies with adaptive computation (e.g., chain-of-thought), trained end-to-end expecting planning to emerge implicitly. Without control over the presence, structure, or horizon of planning, these systems dramatically increase reasoning length, yielding inefficient token use without reliable accuracy gains. We argue efficient agentic reasoning benefits from decomposing decision-making into three systems: simulative reasoning (System II) grounding deliberation in future-state prediction via a world model; self-regulation (System III) deciding when and how deeply to plan via a learned configurator; and reactive execution (System I) handling fine-grained action. Simulative reasoning provides unified planning across diverse tasks without per-domain engineering, while self-regulation ensures the planner is invoked only when needed. To test this, we develop SR$^2$AM (Self-Regulated Simulative Reasoning Agentic LLM), realizing both as distinct stages within an LLM's chain-of-thought, with the LLM as world model. We explore two instantiations: recording decisions from a prompted multi-module system (v0.1) and reconstructing structured plans from traces of pretrained reasoning LLMs (v1.0), trained via supervised then reinforcement learning (RL). Across math, science, tabular analysis, and web information seeking, v0.1-8B and v1.0-30B achieve Pass@1 competitive with 120-355B and 685B-1T parameter systems respectively, while v1.0-30B uses 25.8-95.3% fewer reasoning tokens than comparable agentic LLMs. RL increases average planning horizon by 22.8% while planning frequency grows only 2.0%, showing it learns to plan further ahead rather than more often. More broadly, learned self-regulation instantiates a principle we expect to extend beyond planning to how agents govern their own learning and adaptation.

</details>


### [30] [Ratchet: A Minimal Hygiene Recipe for Self-Evolving LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22148v1)
*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Ratchet框架用于LLM agent自我进化技能库，通过收编和退休机制提升性能，直接相关。

TL;DR: Ratchet通过结果驱动淘汰、有界活跃上限和元技能指导等生命周期管理机制，使冻结LLM代理的技能库性能大幅提升，在编程和软件工程基准上分别实现+0.328和+0.22的滚动均值增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自演化技能库中LLM编写的技能未能带来性能提升，瓶颈在于技能生命周期管理而非编写能力。

Method: 提出Ratchet单代理循环，由冻结LLM自主执行技能编写、检索、策划和淘汰，集成四种卫生机制：结果驱动淘汰、有界活跃上限、元技能编写指导和模式规范化。

Result: 在MBPP+ hard-100上，pass@1从0.258±0.047提升至0.584滚动均值（峰值0.658±0.042），增益+0.328±0.018，远优于无技能控制（+0.002±0.005）；在SWE-bench Verified上峰值提升0.22。消融实验表明淘汰和元技能先验是核心，显式去重可被元技能覆盖。

Conclusion: 通过有界上限和淘汰阈值即可防止性能退化并显著提升，显式去重非必需，简单的生命周期管理是关键。

中文摘要：由Voyager开创的自演化技能库允许冻结的LLM代理在无需权重更新的情况下积累可重复使用的知识，但最近的评估显示，LLM编写的技能相较于无技能基线带来+0.0个百分点的提升，而人工策划的技能则带来+16.2个百分点的提升：瓶颈不在于技能编写，而在于生命周期管理。我们提出\textbf{Ratchet}，一种单代理循环，其中冻结的LLM编写、检索、策划和淘汰自己的自然语言技能。Ratchet集成了四种候选卫生机制：结果驱动的淘汰、有界活跃上限、元技能编写指导和模式规范化。在MBPP+ hard-100上使用Claude Opus 4.7，Ratchet将保留的pass@1从$0.258 \pm 0.047$的基线提升到$0.584$的后期窗口滚动均值（峰值$0.658 \pm 0.042$），跨越100轮和3个随机种子，滚动均值增益为$+0.328 \pm 0.018$，而无技能控制漂移仅为$+0.002 \pm 0.005$；同样的方法迁移到SWE-bench Verified上的代理求解器（20轮内峰值提升+0.22）。八项消融实验（A1--A8）揭示，最小工作配方比我们的设计更简单：淘汰和元技能编写先验是承重结构，而显式去重（规范化、覆盖保护）被元技能本身所涵盖。一个非发散命题表明，有界上限和淘汰阈值共同防止预期性能低于无技能基线。

Original abstract: Self-evolving skill libraries, pioneered by Voyager, let frozen LLM agents accumulate reusable knowledge without weight updates, yet recent evaluation shows that LLM-authored skills deliver $+0.0$pp over no-skill baselines while human-curated ones deliver $+16.2$pp: the bottleneck is not skill authoring but lifecycle management. We introduce \textbf{Ratchet}, a single-agent loop in which a frozen LLM writes, retrieves, curates, and retires its own natural-language skills. Ratchet integrates four candidate hygiene mechanisms: outcome-driven retirement, a bounded active-cap, meta-skill authoring guidance, and pattern canonicalisation. On MBPP+ hard-100 with Claude Opus 4.7, Ratchet lifts held-out pass@1 from a $0.258 \pm 0.047$ baseline to a late-window rolling mean of $0.584$ (peak $0.658 \pm 0.042$) across 100 rounds and 3 seeds, a $+0.328 \pm 0.018$ rolling-mean gain where the no-skill control drifts at $+0.002 \pm 0.005$; the same recipe transfers to an agentic solver on SWE-bench Verified ($+0.22$ peak lift over 20 rounds). Eight ablations (A1--A8) reveal that the minimal working recipe is smaller than our design suggests: retirement and the meta-skill authoring prior are load-bearing, while explicit deduplication (canonicalisation, cover-guard) is subsumed by the meta-skill itself. A non-divergence proposition shows that bounded cap and retirement threshold together prevent expected performance from drifting below the no-skills floor.

### [31] [IdleSpec: Exploiting Idle Time via Speculative Planning for LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22154v1)
*Daewon Choi,Kyunghyun Park,Woomin Song,Saket Dingliwal,Sai Muralidhar Jayanthi,Jinwoo Shin,Aram Galstyan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出利用空闲时间进行推测性规划的agent方法，可迁移到coding agent的规划策略。

TL;DR: IdleSpec是一种利用空闲时间进行计划生成以提升LLM智能体性能的推理方法，通过采样互补草稿策略并聚合候选计划，在多种任务中显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在等待观测结果时存在空闲时间，但现有方法要么忽视该时间，要么无法适应不同计算预算和不确定性，导致利用率低。

Method: IdleSpec在空闲期间迭代生成计划候选，工具响应到达后聚合候选指导推理；通过学习分布采样渐进式和恢复式草稿策略，并利用后验反馈更新分布。

Result: 在GAIA和FRAMES上平均准确率提升5.1%（Gemini-2.5-Flash）；在MLE-Bench上任意奖牌率提升9.1%。

Conclusion: IdleSpec有效利用空闲时间提升智能体性能，且泛化到长周期任务，是一种可扩展的通用方法。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体通过利用多步推理和迭代工具调用与环境交互来解决复杂任务，这会在等待观测结果时产生空闲时间。尽管在大多数智能体场景中空闲时间普遍存在，现有工作要么将其视为不可避免的开销，要么提出受限的解决方案，忽视了不同工具调用之间的计算预算变化和未来观测的不确定性，从而导致空闲时间的利用欠优。在本文中，我们提出了IdleSpec，一种可扩展且通用的推理方法，它利用空闲时间计算来提升智能体性能，同时最小化延迟开销。具体来说，IdleSpec在空闲期间迭代生成计划候选，一旦观测结果可用，就聚合它们以指导下一步推理。为了在观测不确定性下有效生成计划，IdleSpec从通过后验反馈更新的学习分布中采样互补的草稿策略（即渐进式和恢复式）。我们的实验表明，IdleSpec通过有效利用空闲时间，在各种智能体场景中显著提升了智能体性能。特别是在GAIA和FRAMES上，IdleSpec在使用Gemini-2.5-Flash时达到了55.6%的平均准确率，比未使用空闲时间的基线高出5.1%。此外，对于涉及代码执行大量延迟的MLE-Bench，IdleSpec在任意奖牌率上实现了高达9.1%的性能提升，突显了其在长周期任务中的泛化能力。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based agents solve complex tasks by leveraging multi-step reasoning with iterative tool calls and environment interactions, which incur idle time while waiting for observations. Despite the prevalence of idle time in most agentic scenarios, existing works treat it as an unavoidable overhead or propose restricted solutions that overlook varying computational budgets across different tool calls and future observation uncertainty, thereby leading to suboptimal utilization of idle time. In this paper, we introduce IdleSpec, a scalable and generic inference approach that leverages idle-time computation to improve agent performance while minimizing latency overhead. Specifically, IdleSpec iteratively generates plan candidates during idle periods and, once observations become available, aggregates them to guide the next reasoning step. For effective plan generation under observation uncertainty, IdleSpec samples between complementary drafting strategies (i.e., progressive and recovery) from a learned distribution that is updated via posterior feedback. Our experiments demonstrate that IdleSpec significantly improves agent performance in various agentic scenarios by effectively utilizing idle time. In particular, on the GAIA and FRAMES, IdleSpec achieves 55.6% average accuracy with Gemini-2.5-Flash, surpassing the vanilla baseline without idle-time usage by 5.1%. Furthermore, for MLE-Bench, which involves substantial delay from code executions, IdleSpec achieves performance gains of up to 9.1% on the Any Medal rate, highlighting its generalizability to long-horizon tasks.
