### [32] [Adapting the Interface, Not the Model: Runtime Harness Adaptation for Deterministic LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22166v2)
*Tianshi Xu,Huifeng Wen,Meng Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出运行时harness适应方法改进冻结LLM agent，直接相关agent设计。

TL;DR: 提出Life-Harness，一种通过演化运行时连接器来改进冻结LLM智能体在确定性任务上表现的无需参数调整的方法，平均相对提升88.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体适应方法主要更新模型参数，但在确定性规则主导的领域中，许多失败源于模型-环境接口的不匹配。

Method: 从训练轨迹中演化运行时连接器，将重复交互失败转化为跨环境契约、程序技能、动作实现和轨迹调节的可复用干预，并在评估时保持固定。

Result: 在7个确定性环境的126个模型-环境设置中改进了116个，平均相对提升88.5%，且从单模型演化的连接器可迁移至17个其他模型。

Conclusion: 运行时接口适应可作为以模型为中心的智能体训练的互补替代方案。

中文摘要：LLM智能体不仅由其语言模型塑造，还由运行时连接器（runtime harness）塑造，该连接器中介观察、工具使用、动作执行、反馈解释和轨迹控制。虽然现有的智能体适应方法主要更新模型参数，但在确定性、规则主导的领域中，许多失败源于模型-环境接口的不匹配。我们提出Life-Harness，一种生命周期感知的运行时连接器，可在不改变模型权重或评估环境的情况下改进冻结的LLM智能体。Life-Harness从训练轨迹中演化，通过将重复交互失败转化为跨环境契约、程序技能、动作实现和轨迹调节的可复用干预，并在未见任务上保持固定以进行评估。在来自τ-bench、τ²-bench和AgentBench的七个确定性环境中，Life-Harness在18个模型骨干的126个模型-环境设置中改进了116个，平均相对提升88.5%。仅从Qwen3-4B-Instruct轨迹演化的连接器可迁移到其他17个模型，表明Life-Harness捕获了可复用的环境侧结构而非模型特定行为。这些结果将运行时接口适应定位为以模型为中心的智能体训练的补充替代方案。代码见https://github.com/Tianshi-Xu/Life-Harness。

Original abstract: LLM agents are shaped not only by their language models, but also by the runtime harness that mediates observation, tool use, action execution, feedback interpretation, and trajectory control. While existing agent adaptation methods mainly update model parameters, many failures in deterministic, rule-governed domains stem from mismatches at the model--environment interface. We propose Life-Harness, a lifecycle-aware runtime harness that improves frozen LLM agents without changing model weights or evaluation environments. Life-Harness evolves from training trajectories by converting recurring interaction failures into reusable interventions across environment contracts, procedural skills, action realization, and trajectory regulation, and remains fixed for evaluation on unseen tasks. On seven deterministic environments from $τ$-bench, $τ^2$-bench, and AgentBench, Life-Harness improves 116 out of 126 model--environment settings across 18 model backbones, with an average relative improvement of 88.5%. Harnesses evolved only from Qwen3-4B-Instruct trajectories transfer to 17 other models, showing that Life-Harness captures reusable environment-side structure rather than model-specific behavior. These results position runtime interface adaptation as a complementary alternative to model-centric agent training. Code is available at https://github.com/Tianshi-Xu/Life-Harness.

### [33] [Skill Weaving: Efficient LLM Improvement via Modular Skillpacks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22205v1)
*Zhuo Li,Guodong Du,Zesheng Shi,Weiyang Guo,Weijun Yao,Yuan Zhou,Jiabo Zhang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 模块化技能包改进LLM，可迁移到coding agent能力组合。

TL;DR: SkillWeave通过将LLM能力划分为压缩的技能包，在固定内存下实现多领域专业化，9B模型性能超越32B单体模型且速度提升4倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在严格的内存和推理约束下平衡多领域专业化能力，亟需高效模块化方案。

Method: 提出SkillWeave框架，将通用模型能力划分为轻量级领域特定技能包，并集成SkillZip压缩为推理就绪格式。

Result: 9B SkillWeave模型在多任务和智能体基准中超越多个基线，甚至超过32B单体LLM，同时实现高达4倍推理加速。

Conclusion: SkillWeave在固定内存预算下实现了高效的多领域专业化，验证了模块化压缩方法的有效性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型日益需要跨不同领域的专业化，但现有方法难以在严格的内存和推理约束下平衡多领域能力。在这项工作中，我们引入了SkillWeave，一个模块化改进框架，使LLM能够在固定内存预算下实现专业化。SkillWeave将通用模型的全部能力划分为技能包（skillpacks）——轻量级、领域特定的增量模块——从而重新组织和优化模型的内部知识。为了高效部署，SkillWeave集成了SkillZip，将技能包压缩成紧凑且可立即推理的格式，实现低延迟执行下的强多领域性能。在多任务和智能体基准测试中，9B参数的SkillWeave模型优于多个基线，甚至超过了32B的单体LLM，同时实现了高达4倍的速度提升。

Original abstract: Large language models increasingly require specialization across diverse domains, yet existing approaches struggle to balance multi-domain capacities with strict memory and inference constraints. In this work, we introduce SkillWeave, a modular improvement framework that enables LLMs to specialize under fixed memory budgets. SkillWeave partitions full capabilities of a general-purpose model into skillpacks -- lightweight, domain-specific delta modules -- that reorganize and refine the model's internal knowledge. For efficient deployment, SkillWeave integrates SkillZip to compress skillpacks into compact and inference-ready format, enabling strong multi-domain performance with low-latency execution. On multi-task and agentic benchmarks, a 9B SkillWeave model outperforms several baselines and even surpasses a 32B monolithic LLM, while achieving up to 4x speedup.

### [34] [CLORE: Content-Level Optimization for Reasoning Efficiency](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22211v1)
*Yuyang Wu,Qiyao Xue,Guanxing Lu,Weichen Liu,Zihan Wang,Manling Li,Olexandr Isayev*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 内容级优化提高推理效率，通过编辑轨迹，可迁移到agent自我改进。

TL;DR: CLORE通过编辑正确推理轨迹中的冗余和无关内容，结合无参考DPO优化，在保持准确率的同时提升推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习后训练产生过长、重复或语义模糊的推理，而高效方法仅控制响应长度，忽略中间内容质量。

Method: CLORE使用外部增强模型对正确策略轨迹进行局部删除（重复、模糊、无关及多余推理），保留答案，然后通过辅助无参考DPO和策略梯度训练优化增强-原始对。

Result: 在多个数学推理基准上，CLORE提升了准确率-效率权衡，兼容GRPO等方法，并减少了重复、模糊内容及后探索。

Conclusion: 内容级监督是长度级控制的有效补充方向，能进一步优化推理质量。

中文摘要：强化学习后训练提高了大型语言模型的推理能力，但常常产生不必要地长、重复或语义模糊的推理轨迹。现有的高效推理方法主要通过显式预算或长度感知奖励来调节响应长度，导致中间推理内容监督薄弱。我们提出了CLORE，一种内容级优化框架，通过编辑正确的在策略展开来提高推理效率。CLORE使用外部增强模型删除重复片段、难以辨认或任务无关的内容，以及在解决方案确定后多余的推理，同时保留最终答案。得到的增强-原始对通过辅助的无参考DPO目标以及标准策略梯度训练进行优化。通过限制增强在正确轨迹上并执行局部删除，CLORE保持编辑后的展开接近策略分布，减轻离策略失配。在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B和Qwen2.5-Math-7B上进行的五个数学推理基准实验表明，CLORE改善了准确率-效率权衡，并且与GRPO、DAPO、Training Efficient和ThinkPrune兼容。内容级分析进一步表明，CLORE减少了重复推理、难以辨认的内容和答案后探索，支持内容级监督作为长度级控制的补充方向。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning post-training has improved the reasoning ability of large language models, but often produces unnecessarily long, repetitive, or semantically opaque reasoning traces. Existing efficient reasoning methods mainly regulate response length through explicit budgets or length-aware rewards, leaving intermediate reasoning content weakly supervised. We propose CLORE, a content-level optimization framework that improves reasoning efficiency by editing correct on-policy rollouts. CLORE uses an external augmentation model to delete repetitive segments, illegible or task-irrelevant content, and superfluous reasoning after the solution is established, while preserving the final answer. The resulting augmented--original pairs are optimized with an auxiliary reference-free DPO objective alongside standard policy-gradient training. By restricting augmentation to correct trajectories and performing local deletion, CLORE keeps edited rollouts close to the policy distribution and mitigates off-policy mismatch. Experiments on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B and Qwen2.5-Math-7B across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that CLORE improves the accuracy--efficiency trade-off and remains compatible with GRPO, DAPO, Training Efficient, and ThinkPrune. Content-level analyses further show that CLORE reduces repetitive reasoning, illegible content, and post-answer exploration, supporting content-level supervision as a complementary direction to length-level control.

</details>


### [35] [SGR-Bench: Benchmarking Search Agents on State-Gated Retrieval](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22219v1)
*Ningyuan Li,Haiyang Shen,Mugeng Liu,Yudong Han,Zhuofan Shi,Sixiong Xie,Yun Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 搜索agent benchmark，涉及状态门控检索，属于agent评测。

TL;DR: 提出状态门控检索（SGR）概念并构建SGR-Bench基准，评估发现当前最强代理系统仅达66.18% F1，失败主因为检索范围漂移和标准不匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网页任务基准未充分覆盖需要站点特定状态配置的专门化数据检索场景，这类能力（状态门控检索）尚未被系统研究。

Method: 构建包含100个专家任务的SGR-Bench基准，覆盖6个源家族和12个生态系统，每任务需发现网站并配置检索状态。采用约束引导与目标导向双表述，评估8个CLI代理LLM和3个商业搜索代理。

Result: 最强系统项级F1为66.18%，行级F1更低；失败轨迹中检索范围漂移（37.2%）与标准不匹配（27.6%）为主因，答案组合仅10.3%。

Conclusion: 当前代理在状态门控检索任务上表现有限，主要瓶颈在于正确建立站点特定检索状态而非最终答案生成，需改进对检索状态配置的理解能力。

中文摘要：近期大语言模型与工具使用智能体的进展扩展了基准化网页任务的范围。然而，一类重要的专门化检索任务仍未得到充分刻画。在许多专门化数据检索网站上，只有通过过滤器、视图、层级结构或作用域建立正确的站点特定检索状态后，才能访问包含答案的证据。我们将这种能力称为状态门控检索（SGR）。我们引入了SGR-Bench，一个针对该场景的基准测试，包含100个由专家精心设计的任务，涵盖六个源家族和12个公共数据生态系统。每个任务需要发现合适的网站并配置其站点特定检索状态以生成结构化答案。SGR-Bench将同一基础问题的约束引导式与目标导向式表述配对，从而能够在状态门控检索的显式与隐式引导之间进行受控比较。我们评估了八个基于命令行的智能体大语言模型系统和三个商业搜索智能体产品。在SGR-Bench上，最强系统仅达到66.18%的项目级F1分数，而行级F1分数则更低。对156条可分析的失败命令行轨迹的人工审查揭示了原因：智能体常能到达相关网页源，但建立了错误的站点特定检索状态。检索范围漂移（37.2%）与标准不匹配（27.6%）占主导，而最终答案组合仅占10.3%。数据集与单案例评估说明可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/PKUAIWeb/SGR-BENCH获取。

Original abstract: Recent advances in large language models and tool-using agents have expanded the range of benchmarked web tasks. Yet an important class of specialized retrieval tasks remains undercharacterized. On many specialized data-retrieval websites, answer-bearing evidence becomes accessible only after establishing the correct site-specific retrieval state through filters, views, hierarchies, or scopes. We term this capability state-gated retrieval (SGR). We introduce SGR-Bench, a benchmark for this setting containing 100 expert-curated tasks spanning six source families and 12 public data ecosystems. Each task requires discovering the appropriate website and configuring its site-specific retrieval state to produce a structured answer. SGR-Bench pairs constraint-guided and goal-oriented formulations of the same underlying problems, enabling controlled comparisons between explicit and implicit guidance for state-gated retrieval. We evaluate eight CLI-based agentic LLM systems and three commercial search-agent products. On SGR-Bench, the strongest system reaches only 66.18% item-level F1, while row-level F1 remains much lower. A manual audit of 156 analyzable failed CLI trajectories shows why: agents often reach a relevant web source, but establish the wrong site-specific retrieval state. Retrieval-scope drift (37.2%) and criterion mismatch (27.6%) dominate, whereas final answer composition accounts for only 10.3%. The dataset and single-case evaluation instructions are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/PKUAIWeb/SGR-BENCH.

</details>


### [36] [Evaluating Large Language Models as Live Strategic Agents: Provider Performance, Hybrid Decomposition, and Operational Gaps in Timed Risk Play](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22238v1)
*H. C. Ekne*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 评估LLM作为实时策略agent，属于agent评测与机制分析。

TL;DR: 通过定时多阶段Risk环境比较LLM，发现模型在实际部署中表现差异主要来自端到端系统行为而非规划能力，Gemini在目标跟踪和执行转化上更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统静态基准无法反映LLM在真实循环系统中的行为，因此需要研究其在时间限制、格式约束和故障模式下的表现。

Method: 在定时多阶段Risk环境中举办跨提供商锦标赛，并设计实验分离规划与执行，分析轨迹。

Result: Gemini在32场冠军赛中赢20场，但分开规划后各模型表现接近，差异来自终端行为；Gemini更频繁关注目标并生成深度征服链。

Conclusion: LLM评估应考虑其在有界工作流中的整体表现，包括目标跟踪、执行转化、成本和可靠性。

中文摘要：静态基准测试只捕捉了大语言模型在实际行为中的一部分。现实系统将模型置于重复循环中，带有时间限制、格式约束和故障模式。我们在一个定时多阶段Risk环境中研究了这种设置，该环境具有明确的胜利目标和重复的规划与执行周期。在一项由规则固定的、跨提供商的32场冠军赛中，gemini-3.1-pro-preview在32场比赛中赢了20场，对手包括gpt-5.1、claude-opus-4-7和kimi-k2.6，且合并的获胜者分布显著不同于实力均等的零假设（p约1.5×10^-5）。然后，我们通过将执行标准化到更便宜的Gemini Flash脚手架上，将规划与执行分开。在这种设计下，合并的32场规划器竞赛与接近均等的结果一致（p约0.821），这表明之前的大部分提供商差异来自端到端系统行为，而非仅规划。为了研究机制，我们分析了提供商锦标赛中保存的规划与执行轨迹。Gemini远比其他模型更频繁地提及终端目标，并且随着胜利的临近，这种关注度增加。Gemini还将更多的回合转化为深度征服链，尽管它并非最干净的运行时。这些结果表明，实时代理的性能取决于目标跟踪、执行转化、成本和运行时可靠性，并支持将LLM评估为有界工作流中的组件，而非孤立的基准测试响应者。

Original abstract: Static benchmarks capture only part of how large language models behave in practice. Real systems place models inside repeated loops with time limits, formatting constraints, and failure modes. We study this setting in a timed multi-phase Risk environment with explicit victory targets and repeated planning and execution cycles. In a replicated 32-game cross-provider championship under frozen rules, gemini-3.1-pro-preview won 20 of 32 games against gpt-5.1, claude-opus-4-7, and kimi-k2.6, and the pooled winner distribution differs strongly from an equal-strength null (p approx 1.5 x 10^-5). We then separate planning from execution by standardizing execution on a cheaper Gemini Flash scaffold. Under this design, a pooled 32-game planner bakeoff is consistent with near-equality (p approx 0.821), which indicates that much of the earlier provider spread came from end-to-end system behavior rather than planning alone. To study mechanism, we analyze saved planning and execution traces from the provider championship. Gemini refers to the terminal objective far more often than the other models and increases that focus as victory approaches. Gemini also converts more turns into deep conquest chains, even though it is not the cleanest runtime. These results show that live-agent performance depends on objective tracking, execution conversion, cost, and runtime reliability, and they support evaluating LLMs as components in bounded workflows rather than as isolated benchmark respondents.

*Azure Zhang,Ning Gao,Yuqin Dai,Ruiyuan Wu,Jinpeng Wang,Rena Wei Gao,Bingdong Tan,Shuzheng Gao,Zongjie Li,Chaozheng Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练LLMs保守且奖励塑形强化学习效果有限，需要挖掘用户潜在顾虑以激发主动对话能力。

Method: 构建认知用户模拟器建模用户分层角色（外部特征+隐藏顾虑），并提出模拟器诱导的非对称视角策略优化，包括非对称在线自蒸馏和状态转换策略优化。

中文摘要：主动任务导向对话（TOD），例如外呼销售，需要一个有说服力的智能体，它能够主动探测用户的顾虑，并在有限的轮次内引导对话走向接受。然而，后训练的大语言模型天生保守，而奖励塑形的强化学习（如GRPO）效果不佳，因为它只是重新加权一个已经被动策略所采样的内容。我们证明，以用户潜在顾虑为条件可以解锁主动能力，而无论多少采样都无法削弱这种能力，从而将这些顾虑确立为关键的训练时信号。为了将这一发现付诸实践，我们构建了**认知用户模拟器**，它将每个用户建模为分层角色，包括可观察的外部特征和隐藏的内部顾虑。该模拟器产生忠实且多样的交互，同时输出每轮的状态动态，以跟踪说服进展。接着，我们引入**模拟器诱导的非对称视角策略优化**，它将建模的顾虑和模拟状态转换转化为互补的训练目标：（1）**非对称在线自蒸馏**，将来自同一策略的特权视角的顾虑感知行为转移到其可部署的、仅对话的视角中；（2）**状态转换策略优化**……

Original abstract: Proactive task-oriented dialogue (TOD), such as outbound sales, demands a persuasive agent that actively probes the user's concerns and steers the conversation toward acceptance within a bounded number of turns. Yet post-trained LLMs are inherently conservative, and reward-shaping RL (e.g., GRPO) struggles since it only re-weights what an already passive policy samples. We show that conditioning on the user's latent concerns unlocks proactive capability that no amount of sampling can undermine, establishing these concerns as a pivotal training-time signal. To operationalize this finding, we build the \textbf{Cognitive User Simulator}, which models each user as a stratified persona comprising observable external traits and hidden internal concerns. The simulator produces faithful and diverse interactions, while emitting per-turn state dynamics that track persuasion progress. We then introduce \textbf{Simulator-Induced Asymmetric-View Policy Optimization}, which converts the modeled concerns and the simulation state transition into complementary training objectives: (1) \emph{Asymmetric On-Policy Self-Distillation} that transfers concern-aware behavior from a privileged view of the same policy into its deployable, conversation-only view; and (2) \emph{State-Transition Policy Refinement} ...

### [38] [Cross-domain benchmarks reveal when coordinated AI agents improve scientific inference from partial evidence](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22300v1)
*Fiona Y. Wong,Markus J. Buehler*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 跨领域基准探究协调AI agent的价值，涉及多agent协作与评测

TL;DR: 该论文通过跨领域基准评估协调AI代理的价值，发现只有在不同学科各捕获部分现象时跨通道组合才显著提升性能，否则协调主要改善解释性或表示性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定协调AI代理何时比简单工作流程更有价值。

Method: 使用四个科学任务的跨领域基准，包含固定评估面板、预定义评分协议、基线和消融控制。

Result: 定义三种运行模式：跨通道组合在部分现象捕获时提升性能（AUROC达0.944/0.955），但有时与强基线持平；主导信号下协调改善解释性；分子声化中改善表示性。

Conclusion: 协调的价值需在明确比较器支持下才成立。

中文摘要：科学证据通常跨越仪器、数据库和学科，因此没有单一来源记录完整现象。这使得难以确定协调的AI代理何时比更简单的工作流程更具价值。我们通过一个跨领域基准来评估这一问题，该基准涵盖四个科学任务：将分子结构映射为音乐表示、检测科学中的历史范式转变、识别媒介传播疾病的出现以及审查凌星系外行星候选体。每个案例使用固定的评估面板、预定义的评分协议、明确的基线、消融或空控制，以及陈述的局限性。结果定义了三种运行模式。当不同学科各自仅捕获部分现象时，跨通道组合优于单通道基线：气候媒介出现达到AUROC 0.944，系外行星审查达到AUROC 0.955。然而，系外行星工作流程与一个强大的组合摘要基线实际上持平，表明分解并不总是改善顶级性能。当一个信号占主导地位时，如范式转变检测，协调主要改善解释和可追溯性。对于分子声化，增益是表示性的而非预测性的。ScienceClaw x Infinite为此评估提供了可审计的产物和溯源层。因此，该基准仅在相应的性能、溯源或表示主张得到明确比较器支持时才赋予协调价值。

Original abstract: Scientific evidence often spans instruments, databases, and disciplines, so no single source records the full phenomenon. This makes it difficult to determine when coordinated AI agents add value over simpler scientific workflows. We evaluate this question with a cross-domain benchmark spanning four scientific tasks: mapping molecular structure into musical representations, detecting historical paradigm shifts in science, identifying vector-borne disease emergence, and vetting transiting-exoplanet candidates. Each case uses a frozen evaluation panel, predefined scoring protocols, explicit baselines, ablations or null controls, and stated limitations. The results define three operating regimes. When different disciplines each capture only part of the phenomenon, cross-channel composites improve over single-channel baselines: climate-vector emergence reaches AUROC 0.944 and exoplanet vetting reaches AUROC 0.955. However, the exoplanet workflow is effectively tied with a strong combined-summary baseline, showing that decomposition does not always improve top-line performance. When one signal dominates, as in paradigm-shift detection, coordination mainly improves interpretation and traceability. For molecular sonification, the gain is representational rather than predictive. ScienceClaw x Infinite provides the auditable artifact and provenance layer for this evaluation. The benchmark therefore assigns value to coordination only when the corresponding performance, provenance, or representation claim is supported by explicit comparators.

### [39] [Scaling Observation-aware Planning in Uncertain Domains](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22364v1)
*Adrian Zvizdenco,Arthur Conrado Veiga Bosquetti,Alberto Lluch Lafuente,Christoph Matheja*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于POMDP的可扩展观察规划，涉及agent规划与传感选择

TL;DR: 本文通过分解POMDP的新方法，在求解OOP的SSP和POP问题上实现了实例大小和运行时间的大幅提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不确定领域中部署传感器需要在任务可行性和成本之间权衡，现有方法效率低。

Method: 开发了基于POMDP分解的新求解方法，结合（子）符号技术，改进参数合成。

Result: 新方法在实例大小上提升3个数量级，运行时间上提升5个数量级。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效扩展了OOP的求解规模，具有显著性能提升。

中文摘要：决定在不确定领域的智能体上部署哪些感知能力是一个基本的工程挑战，需要在任务可实现性与硬件和处理的高成本之间权衡。这个问题先前被形式化为最优可观测性问题（OOP），基于众所周知的用于决策的部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）模型。本文研究（子）符号技术，以扩展求解OOP的可判定片段，即传感器选择问题（SSP）和位置可观测性问题（POP）。除了改进基于参数合成的原始方法，我们还开发了一种新的求解方法，通过分解POMDP来识别合理的观测函数，分别在实例大小和运行时间上提升了3个和5个数量级。

Original abstract: Deciding which sensing capabilities to deploy on an agent in uncertain domains is a fundamental engineering challenge, in which one balances task achievability against the high costs of hardware and processing. This problem has previously been formalized as the Optimal Observability Problem (OOP), based on the well-known Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) model for decision-making. This work studies (sub-)symbolic techniques to scale solving of decidable fragments of the OOP, namely the Sensor Selection Problem (SSP) and the Positional Observability Problem (POP). Besides improving the original approach based on parameter synthesis, we develop a new solving method that identifies sensible observation functions via decomposition of POMDPs, improving performance by 3 and 5 orders of magnitude for instance size and runtime, respectively.

### [40] [S2ED: From Story to Executable Descriptions for Consistency-Aware Story Illustration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22448v1)
*Sijing Yin,Jiamou Liu,Xiao Tang,Yaser Shakib,Qian Liu*

TL;DR: 提出S2ED框架，通过提示层将故事转化为可执行描述，提升多帧故事插图的序列一致性和角色保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: S2ED是一个训练无关、模型无关的提示层框架，协调三个智能体（叙事分解、人物属性锚定、空间情感丰富）将故事转化为可编辑的可执行描述，支持状态传播和局部编辑修复漂移。

Result: 在Flintstones和Shakoo Maku数据集上，S2ED在自动指标和人工评估中均优于强提示、大模型规划和参考训练方法，提升了序列级一致性和人物保真度。

Original abstract: Multi-frame story illustration requires long-horizon coherence beyond single-image text-to-image generation, including narrative decomposition and persistent character identity, layout, and affect across frames. We propose Story-to-Executable Descriptions (S2ED), a training-free, model-agnostic, prompt-layer framework that converts a full story into a sequence of explicit, editable executable descriptions for more consistent rendering. S2ED coordinates three agents to segment the narrative, ground canonical character attributes, and enrich spatial and affective cues, enabling interpretable prompt-carried state propagation and local edits to repair drift without retraining the generator. Experiments on Flintstones and Shakoo Maku show that S2ED improves sequence-level consistency and character fidelity over strong prompting, large-model planning, and a reference training-based method, under both automatic metrics and human judgments. We also deploy S2ED in an end-to-end story-to-storybook system for children's illustrated stories, with a supplementary video.

Original abstract: While linear manufacturing relies on homogeneous materials and predefined process sequences, circular manufacturing reintroduces used products with heterogeneous and uncertain conditions. This shift demands manufacturing systems capable of handling variable product states, dynamically reconfigurable processes, and the integration of human and machine knowledge. Conventional manufacturing IT architectures, designed for stable structures and deterministic execution, are unable to meet these requirements, as they cannot adequately represent and manage the uniqueness of individual components at runtime. Following a design science methodology for developing a Cyber Physical Production System for circular manufacturing, we derive 14 requirements from five complementary perspectives. Based on these requirements, we design KAPPS, a knowledge-based architecture that uses an ontology-grounded knowledge graph as a unifying data backbone, combined with a semantic interface layer to enable consistent data and information integration, reasoning, and communication across heterogeneous systems and services, turning the knowledge graph from an integration layer into the factories authoritative write-time state. KAPPS incorporates modules for constraint enforcement and event-driven planning, enabling incremental adaptation of execution plans under uncertainty and human-machine knowledge exchange. The applicability of KAPPS is demonstrated through two implemented use cases: (i) Anomaly detection and learning through knowledge graph mediated services and (ii) runtime constraint enforcement in a modular conveyor system. Subsequently, the architecture is evaluated against the 14 requirements (ed. abstract shortened)

### [42] [Compiling Agentic Workflows into LLM Weights: Near-Frontier Quality at Two Orders of Magnitude Less Cost](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22502v1)
*Simon Dennis,Rivaan Patil,Kevin Shabahang,Hao Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将agent工作流编译为LLM权重，极大降低推理成本，直接相关agent方法与优化

TL;DR: 本文识别并实证解决了开发者采用地下智能体（过程编译入小模型权重）而非外部编排框架的三个感知障碍，在三个实际任务中证明其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管地下智能体相比外部编排在成本、隐私和效率上具有优势，但开发者仍倾向于采用编排框架，本文旨在探究并消除其背后的感知障碍。

Method: 识别三个感知障碍，并在旅行预订、Zoom支持和保险理赔三个实际任务中进行对照实验，实证分析每个障碍的影响。

Result: 三个感知障碍均被成功解决，地下智能体在任务完成质量、成本效率和隐私保护上均优于编排框架。

Conclusion: 地下智能体是一种可行的替代方案，能解决编排框架的固有缺陷，建议开发者优先考虑采用。

中文摘要：智能体编排框架已经大量涌现，在LangGraph、CrewAI、Google ADK、OpenAI Agents SDK、Semantic Kernel、Strands和LlamaIndex上累计超过29万颗GitHub星标。所有框架都遵循相同的模式：在LLM之上设置外部编排器，每轮注入指令并做出路由决策。近期工作表明，对于程序化任务，只需将过程放在前沿模型的系统提示中即可超越这种架构[Dennis等，2026a]，但代价是消耗上下文窗口、每次对话都需要前沿模型，并将专有过程暴露给第三方提供商。将过程编译到一个小型微调模型的权重中——创建地下智能体——应该能解决所有这些问题，且先前的工作（SimpleTOD、FireAct、SynTOD、WorkflowLLM、Agent Lumos）已经证明了该技术的有效性。然而，开发者采用却 overwhelmingly 偏向编排。我们识别了三个感知障碍，并在旅行预订（14个节点）、Zoom支持（14个节点，产品特定知识）和保险理赔（55个节点，6个决策枢纽）中针对每个障碍进行了实证研究。

Original abstract: Agent orchestration frameworks have proliferated, collectively exceeding 290,000 GitHub stars across LangGraph, CrewAI, Google ADK, OpenAI Agents SDK, Semantic Kernel, Strands, and LlamaIndex. All follow the same pattern: an external orchestrator above the LLM, injecting instructions and routing decisions every turn. Recent work has shown this architecture is dominated for procedural tasks by simply providing the procedure in a frontier model's system prompt [Dennis et al., 2026a], at the cost of consuming the context window, requiring a frontier model for every conversation, and exposing proprietary procedures to third-party providers. Compiling the procedure into the weights of a small fine-tuned model -- creating a subterranean agent -- should resolve all of these concerns, and prior work (SimpleTOD, FireAct, SynTOD, WorkflowLLM, Agent Lumos) has shown the technique works. Yet developer adoption has overwhelmingly favored orchestration. We identify three perceived barriers and address each empirically across travel booking (14 nodes), Zoom support (14 nodes, product-specific knowledge), and insurance claims (55 nodes, 6 decision hubs).

### [43] [Towards Direct Evaluation of Harness Optimizers via Priority Ranking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22505v1)
*Kai Tzu-iunn Ong,Minseok Kang,Dongwook Choi,Junhee Cho,Seungju Kim,Seungwon Lim,Geunha Jang,Minwoo Oh,Bogyung Jeong,Sunghwan Kim,Taeyoon Kwon,Jinyoung Yeo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出harness优化器的直接评估方法，优先级排名可预测优化器能力，与自动化agent创建和优化直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出优先级排序方法直接评估装备优化器，通过排序组件能力预测实际优化性能，并创建Shor数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前间接评估方法忽略优化器的中间错误，无法区分其行为是信息驱动还是试错，因此需要直接评估，但缺乏标准装备导致评估困难且昂贵。

Method: 提出优先级排序，要求优化器对装备组件按更新潜力排序，以低成本量化其步骤级能力。

Result: 优化器的排序能力与实际多步优化中改善代理的性能显著相关。

Conclusion: 优先级排序可作为优化能力的可靠预测指标，Shor数据集支持该评估方法。

中文摘要：装备优化通过让优化器代理迭代更新目标代理的装备来实现自动化代理创建。尽管取得了成功，但目前的研究仅通过观察目标代理的性能提升来评估优化器。这种间接的端改进评估忽略了优化器在中间步骤中的操作，这些操作通常是有错误的，并阻碍了代理性能。因此，尚不清楚装备优化是由优化器有依据的更新操作驱动，还是仅仅通过试错。这需要对装备优化器进行直接评估。然而，由于缺乏标准装备，直接评估装备优化器既困难又昂贵。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种简单、低成本的设计来直接评估它们，即优先级排序。通过让装备优化器对给定装备中的组件（例如工具）按其更新时改善/阻碍代理性能的潜力进行排序，我们的设计在不进行昂贵的展开或人工检查的情况下，在步骤级别量化了优化器的能力。更重要的是，优化器的排序能力与其在实际多步装备优化中改善代理的能力相关，从而将优先级排序确立为优化能力的可靠预测指标。优先级排序由Shor支持，这是一个包含182个人工验证的优化场景的数据集，涵盖领域、设计和时间阶段。代码和数据可在https://github.com/k59118/Harness_Optimizer_Evaluation获取。

Original abstract: Harness optimization enables automated agent creation by having an optimizer agent iteratively update the harness of target agents. Despite its success, current studies evaluate optimizers solely by observing target agents' performance gains. This indirect end-improvement evaluation neglects optimizers' actions at intermediate steps, which are often erroneous and hinder agent performance. Therefore, it is unclear whether harness optimization is driven by optimizers' informed update actions or simply trial-and-error. This necessitates direct evaluation of harness optimizers. However, evaluating harness optimizers directly is non-trivial and costly due to the lack of oracle harnesses. To address this, we present a simple, low-cost design to directly evaluate them, namely priority ranking. By asking harness optimizers to rank components (e.g., tools) in a given harness by their potential to improve/hinder agent performance when updated, our design quantifies optimizer ability at the step level without expensive rollouts or manual examination. More importantly, optimizers' ranking performance correlates with their ability to improve agents in actual multi-step harness optimization, establishing priority ranking as a reliable predictor of optimization ability. Priority ranking is enabled by Shor, a collection of 182 human-verified optimization scenarios spanning across domains, designs, and time stages. Codes and data can be found at https://github.com/k59118/Harness_Optimizer_Evaluation.

</details>


### [44] [Search-E1: Self-Distillation Drives Self-Evolution in Search-Augmented Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22511v2)
*Zihan Liang,Yufei Ma,Ben Chen,Zhipeng Qian,Xuxin Zhang,Huangyu Dai,Lingtao Mao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Search-E1方法，通过自蒸馏和GRPO实现搜索增强推理agent的自我进化，属于通用agent训练机制。

TL;DR: Search-E1是一种仅需标准GRPO和在线策略自我蒸馏的自我进化方法，在七个QA基准上以3B模型超越所有开源基线，证明了复杂增广并非必要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有搜索增强推理代理的后训练方法依赖外部监督、辅助模块、树搜索等复杂增广，导致训练流程臃肿且资源依赖性强，因此作者探究这些机制是否必要，并希望找到简单有效的替代方案。

Method: 提出Search-E1，采用标准GRPO与在线策略自我蒸馏（OPSD）交替进行：每轮GRPO后，策略在自身训练问题上展开，通过标记级前向KL散度将其推理时间分布与特权上下文下的自身分布对齐，从而提供密集的逐步骤监督。

Result: 在七个QA基准上，Search-E1使用Qwen2.5-3B达到0.440平均精确匹配分数，超越所有开源基线，包括更大规模的模型。

Conclusion: 简单的方法如GRPO结合在线策略自我蒸馏足以有效提升搜索增强推理代理的性能，复杂的增广并非必需，这为未来研究提供了更高效且更具可扩展性的方向。

中文摘要：后训练已成为将语言模型转变为称职的搜索增强推理代理的主要方法。最近的一系列工作通过在此标准流程之上添加精密的机制来进一步推动其性能。这些增强功能从更强的外部系统导入外部监督，附加辅助模块如过程奖励模型或回顾性批评者，通过树搜索或多阶段课程重构展开本身，或者用精心设计的奖励与惩罚来塑造奖励。每项增加都带来了可衡量的提升，但同时也使训练流程更加臃肿，并将该方法与可能并非始终可用的资源或设计绑定在一起。我们退一步思考，这些机制是否真的必要，并提出了Search-E1，一种自我进化方法，仅通过标准GRPO与在线策略自我蒸馏（OPSD）交替进行，就能让搜索增强代理自我提升。在每轮GRPO之后，策略在其自身的训练问题上进行展开。然后，一个标记级的前向KL散度目标将策略的推理时间分布与其自身在特权上下文下的分布对齐，该特权上下文暴露了一个更高效的兄弟轨迹。尽管方法简单，该过程自然提供了密集的逐步骤监督。在七个QA基准上，Search-E1使用Qwen2.5-3B达到了0.440的平均精确匹配分数，在两个规模上超越了所有开源基线。代码和完整版本将很快公开。

Original abstract: Post-training has become the dominant recipe for turning a language model into a competent search-augmented reasoning agent. A line of recent work pushes its performance further by adding elaborate machinery on top of this standard pipeline. These augmentations import external supervision from stronger external systems, attach auxiliary modules such as process reward models or retrospective critics, restructure the rollout itself with tree search or multi-stage curricula, or shape the reward with hand-crafted bonuses and penalties. Each addition delivers a measurable gain, but each also inflates the training pipeline and ties the recipe to resources or designs that may not always be available. We take a step back and ask whether any of this machinery is actually necessary, and propose Search-E1, a self-evolution method that lets a search-augmented agent improve through only vanilla GRPO interleaved with on-policy self-distillation (OPSD). After each GRPO round, the policy rolls out on its own training questions. A token-level forward KL objective then aligns the policy's inference-time distribution to its own distribution under a privileged context that exposes a more efficient sibling trajectory. Despite this simplicity, the procedure naturally provides dense per-step supervision. On seven QA benchmarks, Search-E1 reaches 0.440 average EM with Qwen2.5-3B, surpassing all open-source baselines at both scales. Code and complete version will be made public soon.

</details>


### [45] [TerminalWorld: Benchmarking Agents on Real-World Terminal Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22535v1)
*Zhaoyang Chu,Jiarui Hu,Xingyu Jiang,Pengyu Zou,Han Li,Chao Peng,Peter O'Hearn,Earl T. Barr,Mark Harman,Federica Sarro,He Ye*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 构建真实终端任务基准TerminalWorld，用于评估agent在复杂工作流中的表现，直接服务于agent评测。

TL;DR: TerminalWorld通过自动逆向工程终端记录生成高保真基准测试，揭示当前AI在真实终端任务上的表现不足（最高62.5%），并与现有基准弱相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准缺乏真实终端环境的真实性和可扩展性，无法准确评估智能体在开发者实践中的能力。

Method: 处理80,870个终端记录，自动逆向工程生成1,530个验证任务，并从中筛选200个人工审核的代表性任务组成TerminalWorld-Verified。

Result: 在TerminalWorld-Verified上，八个前沿模型和六个智能体的最高通过率仅为62.5%，且与Terminal-Bench分数相关性弱（r=0.20）。

Conclusion: TerminalWorld提供了一个真实、可扩展的基准，能够随着开发者实践演变评估智能体，揭示当前系统在真实终端工作流中的不足。

中文摘要：我们介绍了TerminalWorld，一个可扩展的数据引擎，能够从“野外”终端记录中自动逆向工程高保真评估任务。处理80,870个终端记录后，该引擎生成了一个包含1,530个验证任务的完整基准，跨越18个真实世界类别，范围从短小的日常操作到超过50步的工作流程，并覆盖了1,280个独特命令。从中，我们精选了一个包含200个代表性、人工审核任务的Verified子集。在TerminalWorld-Verified上对八个前沿模型和六个智能体进行全面的基准测试显示，当前系统仍难以处理真实的终端工作流程，最高通过率仅为62.5%。此外，TerminalWorld捕捉到了与现有专家策划的基准（例如Terminal-Bench）不同的真实世界终端能力，且与其分数的相关性较弱（Pearson r=0.20）。自动化引擎使TerminalWorld具有真实性和可扩展性，从而能够随着开发者实践的演变在真实终端环境中评估智能体。数据和代码可在https://github.com/EuniAI/TerminalWorld获取。

Original abstract: We introduce TerminalWorld, a scalable data engine that automatically reverse-engineers high-fidelity evaluation tasks from "in-the-wild" terminal recordings. Processing 80,870 terminal recordings, the engine yields a full benchmark of 1,530 validated tasks, spanning 18 real-world categories, ranging from short everyday operations to workflows exceeding 50 steps, and covering 1,280 unique commands. From these, we curate a Verified subset of 200 representative, manually reviewed tasks. Comprehensive benchmarking on TerminalWorld-Verified across eight frontier models and six agents reveals that current systems still struggle with authentic terminal workflows, achieving a maximum pass rate of only 62.5%. Moreover, TerminalWorld captures real-world terminal capabilities distinct from existing expert-curated benchmarks (e.g., Terminal-Bench), with only a weak correlation to their scores (Pearson r=0.20). The automated engine makes TerminalWorld authentic and scalable by construction, enabling it to evaluate agents in real-world terminal environments as developer practices evolve. Data and code are available at https://github.com/EuniAI/TerminalWorld.

### [46] [Think Thrice Before You Speak: Dual knowledge-enhanced Theory-of-Mind Reasoning for Persuasive Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22602v1)
*Minghui Ma,Bin Guo,Runze Yang,Mengqi Chen,Yan Liu,Jingqi Liu,Yahan Pei,Xuehao Ma,Qiuyun Zhang,Zhiwen Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出双知识增强的心智理论推理框架TTBYS用于说服agent，其知识增强推理方法可迁移至其他agent推理设计。

TL;DR: 提出基于ToM-BDI框架的说服对话任务、数据集和知识增强推理方法TTBYS，显著提升LLM对心理状态和说服策略的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM因简单提示和ToM知识不足，难以捕捉心理状态间依赖关系，导致推理碎片化且不稳定。

Method: 提出ToM-PD任务（基于BDI框架建模序列依赖）、构建ToM-BPD数据集，设计TTBYS框架（知识增强逐步推理，利用显式与隐式先验经验）。

Result: Qwen3-8B+TTBYS在欲望、信念和策略预测上分别比GPT-5高1.20%、22.80%、16.97%。

Conclusion: TTBYS增强LLM在说服对话中推理心理状态和策略的可解释性与一致性。

中文摘要：说服性对话需要推理他人潜在的 mental states，这种能力被称为心理理论（ToM）。然而，由于依赖简单的提示策略和 ToM 知识不足，现有的 LLM 通常无法捕捉 mental states 之间的内在依赖关系，导致碎片化表示和不稳定的推理。为了解决这些挑战，我们引入了基于 ToM 的说服性对话（ToM-PD）任务，该任务基于信念-欲望-意图（BDI）框架，明确建模多轮对话中 mental states 的序列依赖关系。为了促进该任务的研究，我们构建了一个大规模注释数据集 ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues（ToM-BPD），捕捉细粒度的 mental states 和相应的说服策略。我们进一步提出 Think Thrice Before You Speak（TTBYS），一种知识增强的逐步推理框架，利用显式和隐式的先验经验来提高 LLM 对欲望、信念和说服策略的推理。实验结果表明，配备 TTBYS 的 Qwen3-8B 在预测欲望、信念和说服策略方面分别比 GPT-5 高出 1.20%、22.80% 和 16.97%。案例研究进一步表明，我们的方法增强了推理的可解释性和一致性。

Original abstract: Persuasive dialogue requires reasoning about others' latent mental states, a capability known as Theory of Mind (ToM). However, due to reliance on simple prompting strategies and insufficient ToM knowledge, existing LLMs often fail to capture the intrinsic dependencies among mental states, leading to fragmented representations and unstable reasoning. To address these challenges, we introduce the ToM-based Persuasive Dialogue (ToM-PD) task, grounded in the Belief-Desire-Intention (BDI) framework, which explicitly models the sequential dependencies among mental states in multi-turn dialogues. To facilitate research on this task, we construct a large-scale annotated dataset, ToM-based Broad Persuasive Dialogues (ToM-BPD), capturing fine-grained mental states and corresponding persuasive strategies. We further propose Think Thrice Before You Speak (TTBYS), a knowledge-enhanced stepwise reasoning framework that leverages both explicit and implicit prior experiences to improve LLMs' inference of desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies. Experimental results demonstrate that Qwen3-8B equipped with TTBYS outperforms GPT-5 by 1.20%, 22.80%, and 16.97% in predicting desires, beliefs, and persuasive strategies, respectively. Case studies further show that our approach enhances interpretability and consistency in reasoning.

### [47] [Spreadsheet-RL: Advancing Large Language Model Agents on Realistic Spreadsheet Tasks via Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22642v1)
*Banghao Chi,Yining Xie,Mingyuan Wu,Jingcheng Yang,Jize Jiang,Zhaoheng Li,Shengyi Qian,Minjia Zhang,Klara Nahrstedt,Rui Hou,Xiangjun Fan,Hanchao Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: RL微调框架训练电子表格agent，涉及多步工具使用与长程任务，可迁移至代码优化agent的训练与评估。

TL;DR: Spreadsheet-RL是一种强化学习微调框架，通过自动化数据收集和专用环境设计，显著提升了AI智能体在电子表格任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有电子表格智能体依赖通用LLM的提示设计，难以处理复杂多步工作流，需要专门的训练方法。

Method: 提出Spreadsheet-RL框架，包括自动流水线收集配对电子表格、领域特定基准数据集Domain-Spreadsheet，以及多轮RL环境Spreadsheet Gym。

Result: 在SpreadsheetBench上Pass@1从12.0%提升至23.4%，在Domain-Spreadsheet上从8.4%提升至17.2%。

Conclusion: Spreadsheet-RL展现了强大的泛化能力和实际应用潜力，有望促进LLM与数据界面的日常交互。

中文摘要：电子表格系统（例如Microsoft Excel、Google Sheets）在现代以数据为中心的工作流中扮演着核心角色。随着AI智能体在自动化复杂任务（如控制计算机和生成演示文稿）方面的能力日益增强，构建AI驱动的电子表格智能体已成为一个前景广阔的研究方向。现有的大多数电子表格智能体依赖于对通用大语言模型进行专门的提示设计；虽然这种设计在简单的电子表格操作中具有潜力，但在处理实际应用中典型的复杂多步工作流时却显得力不从心。我们引入了Spreadsheet-RL，这是一个强化学习（RL）微调框架，旨在真实的Microsoft Excel环境中训练专门的电子表格智能体。Spreadsheet-RL包含一个自动化流水线，用于从在线论坛中可扩展地收集配对的起始-目标电子表格，以及金融和供应链管理等领域特定的评估任务，我们将其整理成新的领域电子表格基准数据集（Domain-Spreadsheet）。它还包含一个专为多轮RL设计的Spreadsheet Gym环境：Spreadsheet Gym通过Python沙箱暴露了广泛的Excel功能，并带有一个精炼的框架，集成了全面的工具集和为电子表格任务精心设计的工具路由规则。通过全面的实验，我们表明Spreadsheet-RL在通用和领域特定的电子表格任务上显著提升了AI智能体的性能：它将Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507在SpreadsheetBench上的Pass@1从12.0%提高到23.4%，并在我们整理的Domain-Spreadsheet数据集上将Pass@1从8.4%提高到17.2%。这些结果凸显了Spreadsheet-RL在电子表格自动化中强大的泛化能力和实际应用潜力，并广泛地展现了其在推进日常工作中基于LLM的数据界面交互方面的前景。

Original abstract: Spreadsheet systems (e.g., Microsoft Excel, Google Sheets) play a central role in modern data-centric workflows. As AI agents grow increasingly capable of automating complex tasks, such as controlling computers and generating presentations, building an AI-driven spreadsheet agent has emerged as a promising research direction. Most existing spreadsheet agents rely on specialized prompting over general-purpose LLMs; while this design has potentials on simple spreadsheet operations, it struggles to manage the complex, multi-step workflows typical of real-world applications.
  We introduce Spreadsheet-RL, a reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning framework designed to train specialized spreadsheet agents within a realistic Microsoft Excel environment. Spreadsheet-RL features an automated pipeline for scalable collection of paired start-goal spreadsheets from online forums, as well as domain-specific evaluation tasks in areas such as finance and supply chain management, which we compile into the new Domain-Spreadsheet benchmark dataset. It also includes a Spreadsheet Gym environment designed for multi-turn RL: Spreadsheet Gym exposes extensive Excel functionality through a Python sandbox, along with a refined harness that incorporates a comprehensive tool set and carefully designed tool-routing rules for spreadsheet tasks. Through comprehensive experiments, we show that Spreadsheet-RL substantially enhances AI agent's performance on both general and domain-specific spreadsheet tasks: it improves Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507's Pass@1 on SpreadsheetBench from 12.0% to 23.4%, and raises Pass@1 from 8.4% to 17.2% on our curated Domain-Spreadsheet dataset. These results highlight Spreadsheet-RL's strong potential for generalization and real-world adoption in spreadsheet automation, and broadly, its promise for advancing LLM-based interactions with data interfaces in everyday work.

### [48] [Claw AI Lab: An Autonomous Multi-Agent Research Team](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22662v1)
*Fan Wu,Cheng Chen,Zhenshan Tan,Taiyu Zhang,Xinzhen Xu,Yanyu Qian,Dingcheng Gao,Lanyun Zhu,Qi Zhu,Yi Tan,Deyi Ji,Guosheng Lin,Tianrun Chen,Deheng Ye,Fayao Liu*

Original abstract: We present Claw AI Lab, a lab-native autonomous research platform that advances automated research from a hidden prompt-to-paper pipeline into an interactive AI laboratory. Rather than centering the system around a single agent or a fixed serial workflow, we allow users to instantiate a full research team from one prompt, with customizable roles, collaborative workflows, real-time monitoring, artifact inspection, and rollback/resume control through a unified dashboard. The platform also supports distinct research modes for exploration, multi-agent discussion, and reproduction, making autonomous research substantially more steerable and laboratory-like in practice. A key practical contribution of Claw AI Lab lies in its Claw-Code Harness, which connects local codebases, datasets, and checkpoints to runnable experiments and feeds execution artifacts back into the research loop. As a result, the harness improves not only execution integration, but also experimental completion and result integrity: experiments are easier to inspect, iterate on, and faithfully transfer into final papers, reducing common failure modes such as partial runs and malformed result reporting. In our internal evaluation on five AI research case studies, using AutoResearchClaw as the baseline, Claw AI Lab is consistently preferred by AI expert judges on idea novelty, experiment completeness, and paper presentation quality. We view Claw AI Lab as an early step toward a new paradigm: autonomous research as usable, interactive, and reliability-aware scientific infrastructure.

### [49] [MBABench: Evaluating LLM Agents on End-to-End Spreadsheet Tasks in Finance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22664v4)
*Thomson Yen,Julian Poeltl,Harshith Srinivas Gear,Yilin Meng,Joshua Fan,Adam Shen,Yili Liu,Ali Bauyrzhan,Siri Du,Haoyang Liu,Daniel Guetta,Hongseok Namkoong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 端到端电子表格任务的agent评估基准，涉及长程执行与多维质量标准，对代码优化agent评估有启发。

TL;DR: 本文首次评估了LLM智能体在端到端电子表格任务上的表现，发现即使最强模型也达不到专业财务标准，且性能随任务复杂度增加而急剧下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有电子表格基准测试只关注问答或单公式编辑，无法衡量智能体构建完整电子表格的高级能力，而金融领域需要这种评估。

Method: 开发了一个包含准确性、公式和格式三个维度的评估分类体系，每个维度有细粒度标准，并在金融工作流（建模和情景分析）上测试了多个LLM智能体。

Result: Claude系列在基准测试中领先且输出最专业，但即使最强智能体也常达不到专业财务标准，当任务难度超过少数链式计算时性能急剧下降。

Conclusion: 当前LLM智能体尚无法可靠地生成满足现实工作流程复杂度的专业质量电子表格。

中文摘要：LLM智能体越来越被期望能够执行端到端的工作流程，从高层用户指令中生成完整的工件。为了满足企业需求，前沿AI实验室已经开发出能够从头构建整个电子表格的智能体。这在金融领域尤其重要，因为财务建模、预测和情景分析等核心工作流程通常通过电子表格进行。然而，现有的电子表格基准测试并未衡量这种高级能力，而是侧重于问答或单一公式编辑。为了填补这一空白，我们首次提供了对智能体在端到端电子表格任务上的评估，重点关注经济关键的财务工作流程，如建模和情景分析。由于其中的交付物通常由多个利益相关者审查和修订，判断其质量必然涉及高层标准，如可读性或易修改性。为了反映解决方案质量的多维性，我们开发了一个评估分类体系，包含三个维度：准确性、公式和格式，每个维度都包含反映专业标准的细粒度标准。Claude系列在基准测试中领先，并在我们的定性审查中产生了最专业的输出，但即使是最强的智能体也常常达不到专业财务标准，并且随着难度超过几个链式计算而急剧下降。这表明，当前的智能体还无法可靠地生成具有现实工作流程所需复杂性的专业质量电子表格。

Original abstract: LLM agents are increasingly expected to carry out end-to-end workflows, producing complete artifacts from high-level user instructions. To meet enterprise needs, frontier AI labs have developed agents that can construct entire spreadsheets from scratch. This is especially relevant in finance, where core workflows such as financial modeling, forecasting, and scenario analysis are commonly conducted through spreadsheets. Yet, existing spreadsheet benchmarks do not measure this advanced capability, focusing instead on question-answering or single-formula edits. To address this gap, we provide one of the first evaluations of agents on end-to-end spreadsheet tasks, focusing on economically critical financial workflows such as modeling and scenario analysis. Since deliverables therein are routinely reviewed and revised by multiple stakeholders, judging their quality necessarily involves high-level criteria such as readability or ease of modification. To reflect the multidimensional nature of solution quality, we develop an evaluation taxonomy comprising three dimensions: Accuracy, Formula, and Format, each comprising fine-grained criteria that reflect professional standards. The Claude family leads the benchmark and produces the most professional-looking outputs in our qualitative review, but even the strongest agents frequently fall short of professional finance standards and degrade sharply as the difficulty increases beyond a few chained calculations. This suggests that current agents are not yet able to reliably produce professional-quality spreadsheets at the level of complexity real-world workflows demand.

### [50] [Is Capability a Liability? More Capable Language Models Make Worse Forecasts When It Matters Most](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22672v2)
*Nick Merrill,Jaeho Lee,Ezra Karger*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 揭示LLM预测中的逆缩放现象及其评估盲区，对agent预测组件与可靠性评估有参考价值。

TL;DR: LLM在预测超线性增长和尾部风险的时间序列时出现逆缩放：更大模型产生更差分布预测，问题集中在右尾，且不受领域知识影响；推荐使用连续无界度量评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM预测评估多采用单阈值指标，可能掩盖模型在尾部风险上的性能退化，需要更全面的评估方法。

Method: 构建FBSim基准（合成SIR模型与线性对照），并在真实疫情、房价、通胀数据上验证；进行分位数分解和规模/训练后效应分析。

Result: 能力更强的模型在分布预测中右尾偏差增大，导致整体校准变差；单阈值指标无法检测该逆缩放，而尾部评分可反转能力-准确性关系。

Conclusion: LLM预测评估应同时采用连续无界指标和二元阈值指标，以捕捉尾部风险影响。

中文摘要：我们记录了LLMs在预测具有超线性增长和体制转换尾部风险（这在金融和流行病学中很常见）的时间序列时存在逆缩放现象。在这些任务上，能力更强的模型会产生更差的分布预测。这一模式出现在我们发布的免污染模拟世界基准测试ForecastBench-Sim（FBSim）上，在预测合成SIR流行病及其匹配的线性对照时，也在真实世界的COVID-19、麻疹、住房市场和恶性通货膨胀数据集中重现。分位数分解表明，失败集中在分布的右尾，能力更强的模型将右尾向上移动以跟踪激进的增长外推，而左尾保持不变。Llama-3.1的家族内研究表明，模型规模和后期训练各自独立地导致了这一效应。领域知识并不能可靠地改善校准。这种逆缩放并未出现在LLM预测基准测试中常见的单阈值指标上，这反转了同一输出上能力与准确性关系的符号。在常规截断点上的单阈值评分忽略了右尾的代价；而包含尾部信息的评分则反转了同一输出上能力与准确性关系的符号。我们建议LLM预测评估在有限二元阈值指标的同时使用连续（且无界）的准确性度量。

Original abstract: We document inverse scaling in LLMs on forecasting problems whose underlying time series exhibit superlinear growth and tail risk of regime change, a structure common in finance and epidemiology. On these tasks, more capable models produce worse distributional forecasts. The pattern appears on ForecastBench-Sim (FBSim), a contamination-free, simulated-world benchmark we release, in forecasting synthetic SIR epidemics with a matched linear control, and replicates in real-world datasets on COVID-19, measles, housing markets, and hyperinflation. A per-quantile decomposition shows the failure concentrates at the upper tail, which more capable models shift upward to track aggressive extrapolations of growth, while the lower tail stays put. A within-family study of Llama-3.1 shows that both model scale and post-training independently contribute to this effect. Domain knowledge does not reliably rescue calibration. This inverse scaling does not appear on single-threshold metrics common in LLM forecasting benchmarks, reversing the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on identical outputs. Single-threshold scoring at conventional cutoffs misses the upper-tail cost; tail-inclusive scoring reverses the sign of the capability--accuracy relationship on the same outputs. We recommend that LLM forecasting evaluations use continuous (and unbounded) measures of accuracy alongside bounded binary threshold metrics.

</details>


### [51] [AMEL: Accumulated Message Effects on LLM Judgments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22714v3)
*Sid-Ali Temkit*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究LLM作为评估者的上下文偏差，对agent评估一致性与可靠性设计有启发。

TL;DR: LLM评估中，先前对话历史的情感倾向会显著影响后续判断，负面历史的影响尤其大，且不随上下文长度增长，需通过独立上下文或平衡历史来缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨LLM作为评估者时，对话历史中的情感极性是否会系统性地偏向后续判断，影响评估的客观性。

Method: 对12个模型进行84,088次API调用，比较相同测试项目在无上下文、正面历史或负面历史后的评估结果，并分析偏差与不确定性、上下文化和位置的关系。

Result: 模型判断向历史主流情感偏移（d=-0.17），高不确定性时偏差更大（d=-0.36），负面历史偏差是正面的1.52倍，偏差不随上下文长度增加，缩放模型略有改善但无法消除。

Conclusion: 为获得公正评估，每个项目应使用独立对话历史；若需批处理，应平衡历史中的情感极性，避免单一情感偏向。
}

中文摘要：大型语言模型常被用作自动评估者：用于审查代码、审核内容或对输出进行评分，通常在一个对话中处理许多项目。我们询问先前对话历史的情感倾向是否会偏向后续判断，这一效应称为LLM判断的累积信息效应（AMEL）。通过对5家提供商（OpenAI、Anthropic、Google、DeepSeek和四个开源模型）的12个模型进行84,088次API调用，我们呈现相同的测试项目，要么单独呈现，要么在主要包含正面或负面评价的历史之后呈现。模型会向对话的主流情感倾向偏移（d = -0.17，p < 10^-53）。该效应集中在基线时模型真正不确定的项目上（高熵项目d = -0.36，而基线确定时d = -0.15）。偏差不随上下文长度增长：5个先前轮次和50个轮次产生相同的偏移（Spearman |r| < 0.01；OLS斜率p = 0.80）。存在负性不对称：每对项目，负面历史引起的偏差是正面的1.52倍（t = 13.03，p < 10^-36，n = 2,733）。扩展规模有助于缓解但无法解决（Anthropic：Haiku -0.22到Opus -0.17；OpenAI：Nano -0.34到GPT-5.2 -0.17）。三个后续实验缩小了机制范围。令牌概率分布是连续变化的，无阈值。负性不对称同时具有令牌级和语义成分，尽管在我们的样本量下归因平衡是探索性的。位置不重要：在50轮历史中的任何位置放置5个有偏轮次都会产生相同的偏移。评估流程最简单的修复方法是每个项目使用新的上下文；当批处理不可避免时，平衡历史记录会有所帮助。

Original abstract: Large language models are routinely used as automated evaluators: to review code, moderate content, or score outputs, often with many items passing through one conversation. We ask whether the polarity of prior conversation history biases subsequent judgments, an effect we call the accumulated message effect on LLM judgments (AMEL). Across 84,088 API calls to 12 models from 5 providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, DeepSeek, and four open-source models), we present identical test items in isolation or following histories saturated with predominantly positive or negative evaluations. Models shift toward the conversation's prevailing polarity (d = -0.17, p < 10^-53). The effect concentrates on items where the model is genuinely uncertain at baseline (d = -0.36 for high-entropy items, vs d = -0.15 when the baseline is deterministic). Bias does not grow with context length: 5 prior turns and 50 produce the same shift (Spearman |r| < 0.01; OLS slope p = 0.80). And there is a negativity asymmetry: paired per item, negative histories induce 1.52x more bias than positive (t = 13.03, p < 10^-36, n = 2,733). Scaling helps but does not solve it (Anthropic: Haiku -0.22 to Opus -0.17; OpenAI: Nano -0.34 to GPT-5.2 -0.17). Three follow-ups narrow the mechanism. The token probability distribution shifts continuously, not at a threshold. The negativity asymmetry has both token-level and semantic components, though attributing the balance is exploratory at our sample sizes. Position does not matter: five biased turns anywhere in a 50-turn history produce the same shift. The simplest fix for evaluation pipelines
  is a fresh context per item; when batching is unavoidable, balancing the history helps.

</details>


### [52] [HarnessAPI: A Skill-First Framework for Unified Streaming APIs and MCP Tools](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22733v1)
*Edwin Jose*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: HarnessAPI是一个Python框架，通过从单一handler.py自动生成HTTP端点和MCP工具，消除了LLM工具的双重表示，减少了74%的样板代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前每个Python函数作为LLM工具需要维护HTTP端点和MCP工具注册两种形式，导致重复和代码漂移。

Method: 将类型化的技能文件夹作为单一真实来源，从handler.py和Pydantic模式自动推导流式HTTP端点、OpenAPI/Swagger UI和MCP工具；通过双模式内容协商支持SSE和JSON；利用动态代码生成确保类型注释正确传播。

Result: 使用cloc测量，在六个代表性技能上减少了74%的框架面向样板代码。

Conclusion: HarnessAPI通过消除双重表示，简化了LLM工具的开发和维护，并继承了FastAPI的生态系统。

中文摘要：每个作为LLM工具部署的Python函数如今都必须以两种形式存在：面向人类客户端和CI管道的HTTP端点，以及面向Claude和Cursor等代理运行时的MCP工具注册。这些表示共享业务逻辑，但在所有周围机制（路由、验证、序列化、流式传输和模式维护）上存在差异，并且随着底层代码的演变而逐渐偏离。我们提出了HarnessAPI，这是一个Python框架，通过将类型化的技能文件夹视为唯一真实来源来消除这种重复。从一个handler.py加上Pydantic模式，该框架自动派生出一个带有服务器发送事件的流式HTTP端点、一个交互式OpenAPI/Swagger UI和一个零配置的MCP工具，所有这些都在单个进程中提供。双模式内容协商允许同一处理程序无需更改即可为SSE流式传输和JSON返回客户端提供服务。动态代码生成机制确保Pydantic类型注释正确传播到FastMCP的检查层，解决了阻止基于闭包的天真注册的技术限制。使用cloc对六个代表性技能进行测量，与手动维护的双栈实现（FastAPI服务器+FastMCP服务器）相比，HarnessAPI将面向框架的样板代码减少了74%。HarnessAPI继承了FastAPI，继承了其完整的中间件、依赖注入和部署生态系统。该框架可在https://github.com/edwinjosechittilappilly/harnessapi获取，也可通过PyPI（pip install harnessapi）安装。

Original abstract: Every Python function deployed as an LLM tool must today exist in two forms: an HTTP endpoint for human-facing clients and CI pipelines, and an MCP tool registration for agent runtimes such as Claude and Cursor. These representations share business logic yet diverge in all the surrounding machinery (routing, validation, serialisation, streaming, and schema maintenance), and they drift apart as the underlying code evolves. We present HarnessAPI, a Python framework that eliminates this duplication by treating a typed skill folder as the single source of truth. From one handler.py plus Pydantic schemas, the framework automatically derives a streaming HTTP endpoint with Server-Sent Events, an interactive OpenAPI/Swagger UI, and a zero-configuration MCP tool, all served from a single process. Dual-mode content negotiation lets the same handler serve SSE-streaming and JSON-returning clients with no handler changes. A dynamic code-generation mechanism ensures Pydantic type annotations propagate correctly to FastMCP's inspection layer, resolving a technical limitation that prevents naive closure-based registration. Measured across six representative skills using cloc, HarnessAPI reduces framework-facing boilerplate by 74% compared with a manually maintained dual-stack implementation (FastAPI server + FastMCP server). HarnessAPI subclasses FastAPI, inheriting its full middleware, dependency-injection, and deployment ecosystem. It is available at https://github.com/edwinjosechittilappilly/harnessapi and on PyPI (pip install harnessapi)

</details>


### [53] [Towards a General Intelligence and Interface for Wearable Health Data](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22759v3)
*Girish Narayanswamy,Maxwell A. Xu,A. Ali Heydari,Samy Abdel-Ghaffar,Marius Guerard,Kara Vaillancourt,Zhihan Zhang,Jake Garrison,Levi Albuquerque,Dimitris Spathis,Hong Yu,Hamid Palangi,Xuhai "Orson" Xu,David G. T. Barrett,Joseph Breda,Jed McGiffin,Yubin Kim,Yuwei Zhang,Naghmeh Rezaei,Samuel Solomon,Karan Ahuja,Tim Althoff,Jake Sunshine,Ming-Zher Poh,Benjamin Yetton,Ari Winbush,Nicholas B. Allen,James M. Rehg,Isaac Galatzer-Levy,Yun Liu,John Hernandez,Anupam Pathak,Conor Heneghan,Yuzhe Yang,Ahmed A. Metwally,Pushmeet Kohli,Mark Malhotra,Shwetak Patel,Xin Liu,Daniel McDuff*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 使用LLM agent自主搜索预测头，涉及agent应用但领域为健康，对一般agent方法有启发

TL;DR: 提出一个在超万亿分钟无标签可穿戴数据上预训练的基础模型，借助模型和数据规模扩展在35项健康任务上表现优异，并利用LLM智能体搜索和个人健康智能体进一步提升性能和安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决可穿戴传感器数据转化为个性化健康洞察的困难，特别是低层次数据表征高层次状态以及高质量标签数据稀缺的问题。

Method: 在五百万参与者超过一万亿分钟无标签传感器信号上预训练基础模型，联合扩展模型容量和数据量；部署LLM智能体自动搜索下游预测头，并集成到个人健康智能体中。

Result: 模型在35项健康预测任务中性能随规模提升，实现小样本学习和生成能力；LLM智能体搜索进一步改善性能；个人健康智能体响应更相关、安全，经1860项临床评级验证。

Conclusion: 大规模无标签可穿戴数据预训练有效，结合LLM智能体和个人健康智能体能实现更强大、安全的健康预测。

中文摘要：虽然无处不在的可穿戴传感器捕获了丰富的行为和生理信息，但有效将这些信号转化为个性化健康洞察仍具有挑战性。具体来说，由于高度的表型多样性以及个体基线健康、生理和生活方式因素的差异，将低层次传感器数据转换为能够表征高层次状态的表示是困难的。此外，收集与健康结果注释配对的可穿戴数据既费力又昂贵，而回顾性注释实际上不可行，导致高质量标签数据稀缺。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了一种可穿戴健康的基础模型，该模型在来自五百万参与者的大队列中超过一万亿分钟的无标签传感器信号上进行了预训练。我们证明了模型容量和预训练数据量的联合扩展带来了系统性的性能提升，这在涵盖心血管、代谢、睡眠和心理健康以及生活方式选择和人口统计学因素的35项健康预测任务上得到了评估。我们发现，这种人口规模的表示解锁了标签高效的小样本学习和生成能力，用于稳健的日常指标估计。为了进一步利用这种学习到的表示，我们部署了一组LLM智能体来自主搜索基于模型嵌入构建的下游预测头空间，显示了随LLM模型容量增加而广泛性能提升。最后，我们展示了如何将这些下游预测器集成到个人健康智能体中，以支持更相关、更具上下文意识和更安全的模型响应，并通过来自临床医生队列的1,860项评级进行了验证。

Original abstract: While ubiquitous wearable sensors capture a wealth of behavioral and physiological information, effectively transforming these signals into personalized health insights is challenging. Specifically, converting low-level sensor data into representations capable of characterizing higher-level states is difficult due to high phenotypic diversity and variation in individual baseline health, physiology, and lifestyle factors. Moreover, collecting wearable data paired with health outcome annotations is laborious and expensive, and retrospective annotation remains practically unfeasible, contributing to a scarcity of data with high-quality labels. To overcome these limitations, we propose a foundation model for wearable health that is pretrained on more than one trillion minutes of unlabeled sensor signals drawn from a large cohort of five million participants. We demonstrate that the joint scaling of model capacity and pretraining data volume leads to systematic improvements in performance, as evaluated on a diverse set of 35 health prediction tasks, spanning cardiovascular, metabolic, sleep, and mental health, as well as lifestyle choices and demographic factors. We find that this population scale representation unlocks label-efficient few-shot learning and generative capabilities for robust daily metric estimation. To further leverage this learned representation, we deploy a classroom of LLM agents to autonomously search the space of downstream predictive heads built on the model embeddings, showing broad performance improvements that increase with LLM model capacity. Finally, we show how integrating these downstream predictors into a Personal Health Agent can support model responses that are more relevant, contextually aware, and safe, and we validate this via 1,860 ratings from a cohort of clinicians.

</details>


### [54] [Advancing Mathematics Research with AI-Driven Formal Proof Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22763v2)

Horváth,Andrew Ferraiuolo,Henryk Michalewski,Edward Lockhart,Codrut Grosu,Thomas Hubert,Matej Balog,Pushmeet Kohli,Swarat Chaudhuri*

Conclusion: AI辅助形式证明搜索有效，揭示了代理设计的关键因素。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在数学推理方面日益表现出色，但其不可靠性限制了其在数学研究中的实用性。一种缓解方法是使用LLM生成像Lean这样的语言中的形式证明。我们首次大规模评估了该方法解决开放问题的能力。我们最强大的代理自主解决了353个开放Erdős问题中的9个，每个问题的成本为几百美元，证明了492个OEIS猜想中的44个，并且正在组合学、优化、图论、代数几何和量子光学研究中使用。一个基本的代理交替使用基于LLM的生成和基于Lean的验证，复制了Erdős的成功，但在最困难的问题上成本更高。这些发现证明了AI辅助形式证明搜索的力量，并揭示了实现这一目标的代理设计。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly excel at mathematical reasoning, but their unreliability limits their utility in mathematics research. A mitigation is using LLMs to generate formal proofs in languages like Lean. We perform the first large-scale evaluation of this method's ability to solve open problems. Our most capable agent autonomously resolved 9 of 353 open Erdős problems at the per-problem cost of a few hundred dollars, proved 44/492 OEIS conjectures, and is being deployed in combinatorics, optimization, graph theory, algebraic geometry, and quantum optics research. A basic agent alternating LLM-based generation with Lean-based verification replicated the Erdős successes but proved costlier on the hardest problems. These findings demonstrate the power of AI-aided formal proof search and shed light on the agent designs that enable it.

### [55] [LCGuard: Latent Communication Guard for Safe KV Sharing in Multi-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22786v1)
*Sadia Asif,Mohammad Mohammadi Amiri,Momin Abbas,Prasanna Sattigeri,Karthikeyan Natesan Ramamurthy*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent系统KV缓存安全通信，可迁移至coding agent协作防护

TL;DR: LCGuard是一个用于多智能体LLM系统中安全潜在通信的框架，通过对抗训练学习表示级变换，减少KV缓存中的敏感信息泄漏，同时保持任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于KV缓存的潜在通信可能泄漏智能体特定敏感信息，需要防护机制。

Method: 将共享KV缓存视为潜在工作记忆，通过对抗训练学习表示级变换，使对抗解码器难以重构敏感输入。

Result: 跨多个模型和基准，LCGuard降低重构泄漏和攻击成功率，保持任务性能。

Conclusion: LCGuard有效提升潜在通信安全性。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型的多智能体系统越来越依赖中间通信来协调复杂任务。虽然现有系统大多通过自然语言通信，但最近工作表明潜在通信，特别是通过Transformer键值缓存，可以提高效率并保留更丰富的任务相关信息。然而，键值缓存也编码了上下文输入、中间推理状态和智能体特定信息，创建了一个不透明通道，敏感内容可能通过该通道在智能体间传播而无显式文本披露。为此，我们引入了LCGuard（潜在通信防护），一个用于多智能体LLM系统中安全的基于键值的潜在通信框架。LCGuard将共享键值缓存视为潜在工作记忆，并在缓存工件跨智能体传输前学习表示级变换。我们通过重构操作性地形式化表示级敏感信息泄漏：如果对抗解码器能从共享缓存工件中恢复智能体特定敏感输入，则该工件不安全。这引出一个对抗训练框架，其中对抗者学习重构敏感输入，而LCGuard学习保留任务相关语义并减少可重构信息的变换。跨多个模型家族和多智能体基准的经验评估表明，与标准键值共享基线相比，LCGuard持续降低基于重构的泄漏和攻击成功率，同时保持具有竞争力的任务性能。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems increasingly rely on intermediate communication to coordinate complex tasks. While most existing systems communicate through natural language, recent work shows that latent communication, particularly through transformer key-value (KV) caches, can improve efficiency and preserve richer task-relevant information. However, KV caches also encode contextual inputs, intermediate reasoning states, and agent-specific information, creating an opaque channel through which sensitive content may propagate across agents without explicit textual disclosure. To address this, we introduce \textbf{LCGuard} (Latent Communication Guard), a framework for safe KV-based latent communication in multi-agent LLM systems. LCGuard treats shared KV caches as latent working memory and learns representation-level transformations before cache artifacts are transmitted across agents. We formalize representation-level sensitive information leakage operationally through reconstruction: a shared cache artifact is unsafe if an adversarial decoder can recover agent-specific sensitive inputs from it. This leads to an adversarial training formulation in which the adversary learns to reconstruct sensitive inputs, while LCGuard learns transformations that preserve task-relevant semantics and reduce reconstructable information. Empirical evaluations across multiple model families and multi-agent benchmarks show that LCGuard consistently reduces reconstruction-based leakage and attack success rates while maintaining competitive task performance compared to standard KV-sharing baselines.

</details>


### [56] [EVE-Agent: Evidence-Verifiable Self-Evolving Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22905v1)
*Yamato Arai,Yuma Ichikawa*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出证据可验证的自进化agent框架，与agent自我改进直接相关

TL;DR: 提出EVE-Agent，通过证据可验证性确保自我进化搜索代理生成可信且可审计的训练数据，显著提升基于证据的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我进化搜索代理可能奖励流畅但无证据支持的示例，导致训练信号不可靠，缺乏可审计性。

Method: 在提议者-求解器框架中，提议者生成问题、答案和证据片段，证据验证器根据边际准确率增益奖励证据，无需外部标注。

Result: 实验表明EVE-Agent在证据正确性上显著优于先前模型，且训练数据可审计。

Conclusion: 证据可验证性是自我进化代理可信性的关键，EVE-Agent通过可审计的生成实例实现了可靠的自我进化。

中文摘要：自我进化代理不应在其无法证明的例子上进行训练。无数据的自我进化搜索代理提供了一种可扩展的途径，使系统能够自行生成问题、回答问题，并根据自身反馈进行改进，而无需人工标注。然而，在没有可验证证据的情况下，这种循环可能会奖励流畅但缺乏支持的示例，将自我生成的课程转变为不透明且可能不可靠的训练信号。我们认为，证据可验证性是搜索代理中可信自我进化的先决条件：每个生成的实例不仅应包含答案，还应包含一个基于来源的片段，其对该答案的贡献可以被衡量。我们引入了EVE-Agent，一种证据可验证的自我进化代理，通过对提议者-求解器框架的修改来实现这一原则。提议者生成一个问题、一个答案和一个逐字证据片段。然后，证据验证器根据提供证据时的边际准确率增益来奖励该片段。这产生了一个训练信号，倾向于真正有助于回答问题的证据，而无需真实答案、人工标签或外部标注。EVE-Agent保持骨干模型、检索器、搜索工具和优化框架不变。实验表明，与先前的自我进化搜索代理相比，EVE-Agent显著提高了基于证据的正确性。由此产生的课程不仅自我生成，而且可审计：每个训练示例都带有一个可检查的来源片段，解释了为何该示例值得信任。

Original abstract: Self-evolving agents should not train on examples they cannot justify. Data-free self-evolving search agents offer a scalable route to systems that generate their own questions, answer them, and improve from their own feedback without human annotations. Yet, without verifiable evidence, this loop can reward fluent but unsupported examples, turning the self-generated curriculum into an opaque and potentially unreliable training signal. We argue that evidence verifiability is a prerequisite for trustworthy self-evolution in search agents: each generated instance should include not only an answer but also a source-grounded span whose contribution to that answer can be measured. We introduce EVE-Agent, an Evidence-Verifiable Self-Evolving Agent that operationalizes this principle through a modification to the proposer--solver framework. The proposer generates a question, an answer, and a verbatim evidence span. An evidence verifier then rewards the span according to the marginal accuracy gain when the evidence is provided. This produces a training signal that favors evidence that genuinely helps answer the question, without requiring oracle answers, human labels, or external annotations. EVE-Agent leaves the backbone model, retriever, search tool, and optimization framework unchanged. Experiments show that EVE-Agent substantially improves evidence-grounded correctness over prior self-evolving search agents. The resulting curriculum is not merely self-generated but auditable by construction: each training example carries an inspectable source span that explains why it should be trusted.

</details>


### [57] [MOSS: Self-Evolution through Source-Level Rewriting in Autonomous Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22794v2)
*Qianshu Cai,Yonggang Zhang,Xianzhang Jia,Huajiang Zheng,Wei Xue,Jun Song,Xinmei Tian,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 源代码级自我重写的agent自进化系统，直接涉及代码修改和自动修复

TL;DR: MOSS是一个在源码级别上实现自主智能体自我演化的系统，通过生产故障证据自动触发多阶段代码修改和验证，无需人工干预即可提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主智能体系统部署后无法学习，且自我演化仅限于文本层，无法修复涉及代码结构的故障，因此需要一种更通用的源码级适应方法。

Method: MOSS首先自动收集生产故障证据批次，然后通过确定性多阶段流水线进行源码级修改，其中代码修改由外部编码智能体CLI执行，MOSS控制阶段顺序和裁决；候选方案在临时环境中重放批次数据验证，最后通过用户同意和健康检查机制进行容器替换和回滚。

Result: 在OpenClaw基准上，MOSS在一次循环中无需人工干预即将四个任务的平均评分从0.25提升至0.61。

Conclusion: 源码级适应是比文本层更强大的演化媒介，MOSS证明了通过自动化源码修改和验证可以显著提升智能体性能，且无需人类介入。

中文摘要：自主智能体系统在部署后基本上是静态的：它们无法从用户交互中学习，反复出现的故障会持续存在，直到下一次人为驱动的更新发布修复。自我进化智能体应运而生，但所有进化都局限于文本可变的工件——技能文件、提示配置、记忆模式、工作流图——而智能体框架本身保持不变。由于路由、钩子排序、状态不变量和调度存在于代码中而非任何文本工件中，因此整个类别的结构故障在物理上无法从文本层触及。我们认为源码级适应是一种本质上更通用的媒介：它是图灵完备的，是所有文本可变范围的严格超集，通过确定性方式生效而非依赖基础模型合规性，并且不会在长上下文漂移下退化。我们提出了MOSS，一个在智能体生产基底上进行源码级自我重写的系统。每次进化都锚定在一批自动策划的生产故障证据上，并通过确定性的多阶段流水线进行；代码修改被委托给一个可插拔的外部编码智能体CLI，而MOSS保留阶段顺序和裁决。候选方案通过在临时试验工作器中重放批次数据对候选镜像进行验证，然后通过用户同意门控的就地容器交换和健康检查门控的回滚进行升级。在OpenClaw上，MOSS在一次循环中将四个任务的平均评分从0.25提升至0.61，无需人工干预。

Original abstract: Autonomous agentic systems are largely static after deployment: they do not learn from user interactions, and recurring failures persist until the next human-driven update ships a fix. Self-evolving agents have emerged in response, but all confine evolution to text-mutable artifacts -- skill files, prompt configurations, memory schemas, workflow graphs -- and leave the agent harness untouched. Since routing, hook ordering, state invariants, and dispatch live in code rather than in any text artifact, an entire class of structural failure is physically unreachable from the text layer. We argue that source-level adaptation is a fundamentally more general medium: it is Turing-complete, a strict superset of every text-mutable scope, takes effect deterministically rather than through base-model compliance, and does not erode under long-context drift. We present MOSS, a system that performs self-rewriting at the source level on production agentic substrates. Each evolution is anchored to an automatically curated batch of production-failure evidence and proceeds through a deterministic multi-stage pipeline; code modification is delegated to a pluggable external coding-agent CLI while MOSS retains stage ordering and verdicts. Candidates are verified by replaying the batch against the candidate image in ephemeral trial workers, then promoted via user-consent-gated, in-place container swap with health-probe-gated rollback. On OpenClaw, MOSS lifts a four-task mean grader score from 0.25 to 0.61 in a single cycle without human intervention.

</details>


### [58] [PathCal: State-Aware Reflection-Marker Calibration for Efficient Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23074v1)
*Lingyu Jiang,Zirui Li,Shuo Xing,Peiran Li,Tsubasa Takahashi,Dengzhe Hou,Zhengzhong Tu,Kazunori Yamada,Fangzhou Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出推理路径反思校准方法，涉及LLM推理过程中的状态感知控制，可迁移至coding agent的规划与验证。

TL;DR: PathCal通过区分反思标记类型并在局部不确定状态下干预，实现了更好的推理效率与性能权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将反思标记视为单一粗粒度类别，未区分其功能角色和影响时机，导致控制不够精细。

Method: PathCal是一种无训练解码控制器，利用反思标记分布估计局部竞争，并软性重新平衡标记logits以校准推理路径。

Result: 在六个推理基准上，PathCal在减少生成长度的同时提高或保持准确性，无需外部验证器或额外采样。

Conclusion: PathCal通过类型区分和局部干预有效优化了推理路径的效率与性能。

中文摘要：大型推理语言模型（LRMs）的出现为通过测试时缩放处理复杂推理任务铺平了道路，其在推理过程中生成长形式的思维链（CoT）轨迹。与此同时，这些轨迹通常包含显式的反思标记，例如“wait”、“but”和“alternatively”，分别表示犹豫、修正和考虑替代探索。最近关于测试时控制的研究利用这些标记作为轻量级的推理控制手柄，通常将它们视为单一粗粒度类别，而不是区分其不同的功能角色。在本文中，我们进行了类型级抑制和固定前缀干预，揭示了反思标记不仅在功能角色上不同，而且在它们发挥最大影响的时机上也不同。具体地，不同的标记类以不同的方式影响准确性和生成长度，并且标记选择在模型稳定到推理轨迹之前最为重要。受这些发现启发，我们引入了PathCal，一种新颖的无训练解码控制器，通过区分标记类型并仅在局部不确定状态下进行干预来校准推理路径。在每个解码步骤中，PathCal利用反思标记的分布来估计维持当前推理轨迹与启动竞争分支之间的局部竞争，并在竞争分支证据过多时软性重新平衡标记logits。在六个推理基准上的实验表明，PathCal实现了更好的效率-性能权衡，在减少生成长度的同时提高或保持准确性，且无需依赖外部验证器或额外采样。

Original abstract: The emergence of Large Reasoning Language Models (LRMs) has paved the way for tackling complex reasoning tasks through test-time scaling by generating long-form Chain-of-Thought (CoT) trajectories during inference. Meanwhile, these trajectories often contain explicit reflection markers such as ``wait'', ``but'', and ``alternatively'', signaling hesitation, revision, and the consideration of alternative explorations, respectively. Recent studies on test-time control leverage such markers as lightweight handles for steering reasoning, typically treating them as a single coarse-grained category rather than distinguishing their distinct functional roles. In this paper, we conduct type-wise suppression and fixed-prefix intervention, revealing that reflection markers differ not only in their functional roles but also in when they exert the greatest influence. Specifically, different marker classes affect accuracy and generation length in distinct ways, and marker choices are most consequential before the model settles into a stable reasoning trajectory. Motivated by these findings, we introduce PathCal, a novel training-free decoding controller that calibrates reasoning paths by distinguishing marker types and intervening only at locally uncertain states. At each decoding step, PathCal utilizes the distribution over reflection-markers to estimate local competition between maintaining the current reasoning trajectory and initiating a competing branch, and softly rebalances marker logits when competing-branch evidence becomes excessive. Experiments across six reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PathCal achieves a better efficiency--performance trade-off, improving or preserving accuracy while reducing generation length, without relying on external verifiers or additional sampling.

</details>

### [59] [MAVEN: A Multi-stage Agentic Annotation Pipeline for Video Reasoning Tasks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21917v2)
*Han Zhang,Wanting Jiang,Tomasz Kornuta,Tian Zheng,Vidya Murali*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多阶段agentic标注流水线，提出可迁移的workflow与自适应机制。

TL;DR: 提出MAVEN多阶段智能体流水线，自动为视频生成多任务训练数据，在交通视频标注和微调中取得优异性能，超越多个基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手动标注无法支持大规模高质量结构化视频注释，需要自动化方法生成包含时间、空间、因果等多维度信息的训练数据。

Method: MAVEN是一个多阶段智能体流水线，首先合成分层多尺度时空事件描述（MSTED），然后基于它生成多种问答格式的训练数据；支持智能体驱动的领域自适应和层次化精炼循环自动修复标注错误。

Result: 在超过5300个交通视频上应用MAVEN，微调Cosmos-Reason2-8B在私有CCTV集上比Gemini 2.5 Pro和3.1 Flash分别高出38.8 MCU点；在AccidentBench上，仅CCTV训练提升10.7点并匹配Gemini 2.5 Pro，加入行车记录仪数据后接近Gemini 3.1 Flash，RL后训练超越两个基线。

Conclusion: MAVEN能够自动生成高质量的结构化视频标注数据，并有效适应新领域，显著提升视觉语言模型的视频事件推理能力。

中文摘要：训练视觉语言模型（VLM）进行视频事件推理需要高质量的结构化注释，不仅捕获发生了什么，还包括时间、地点、原因和结果，这种规模是手动标注无法支持的。我们提出了MAVEN（多阶段智能体视频事件标注），一个多阶段智能体流水线，将原始视频转化为多任务训练数据，并附带思维链（CoT）推理轨迹，围绕一个指定的事件焦点组织。其核心是，MAVEN从三个互补的标题级别合成一个多尺度时空事件描述（MSTED）；这个显式的中间表示作为下游多种任务格式问答生成的唯一输入。关键的是，MAVEN支持智能体驱动的领域自适应：给定一个新的视频数据集和目标问题示例，智能体自上而下地重新设计所有提示，无需手动重新工程。一个层次化的精炼循环进一步根据分类法对标注错误进行分类，追溯根本原因到原始的流水线阶段，并应用针对性编辑来重写提示或修改流水线结构本身，迭代提高数据质量。我们将MAVEN应用于标注超过5300个交通视频，并在生成的数据上微调Cosmos-Reason2-8B。在私有CCTV评估集上，微调超过了Gemini 2.5 Pro和3.1 Flash，包括在MCQ准确率上比零样本提高38.8个百分点。在AccidentBench上，仅使用CCTV训练使Cosmos-Reason2提高10.7个MCQ点，并与Gemini 2.5 Pro持平，尽管没有见过行车记录仪视频；加入智能体适应的行车记录仪注释缩小了与Gemini 3.1 Flash的差距，而RL后训练推动整体性能超过两个Gemini基线。在仓库监控和公共安全视频上的定性结果进一步表明，该智能体工作流能够轻松地将流水线适应到新领域。

Original abstract: Training Vision Language Models (VLMs) for video event reasoning requires high-quality structured annotations capturing not only what happened, but when, where, why, and with what consequence, at a scale manual labelling cannot support. We present MAVEN (Multi-stage Agentic Video Event aNnotation), a multi-stage agentic pipeline that turns raw videos into multi-task training data with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning traces, organized around a designated Event of Focus. At its core, MAVEN synthesizes a Multi-Scale Spatio-Temporal Event Description (MSTED) from three complementary caption levels; this explicit intermediate serves as the sole input to downstream Q&A generation across multiple task formats. Crucially, MAVEN supports agent-driven domain adaptation: given a new video dataset and target question examples, the agent redesigns all prompts top-down without manual re-engineering. A hierarchical refinement loop further classifies annotation errors against a taxonomy, traces root causes to the originating pipeline stage, and applies targeted edits that rewrite prompts or modify the pipeline structure itself, iteratively improving data quality. We apply MAVEN to label over 5,300 traffic videos and fine-tune Cosmos-Reason2-8B on the resulting data. On a private CCTV evaluation set, fine-tuning surpasses both Gemini 2.5 Pro and 3.1 Flash, including a $+38.8$-point gain in MCQ accuracy over zero-shot. On AccidentBench, CCTV-only training lifts Cosmos-Reason2 by $+10.7$ MCQ points and matches Gemini 2.5 Pro despite seeing no dashcam videos; adding agent-adapted dashcam annotations narrows the gap to Gemini 3.1 Flash, and RL post-training pushes overall performance past both Gemini baselines. Qualitative results on warehouse surveillance and public safety videos further show the agentic workflow readily adapts the pipeline to new domains.

</details>


### [60] [The Neglected Baseline in Model Interpretation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22417v4)
*Yongjin Cui,Xiaohui Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文指出现有模型解释方法忽略基线的缺陷，统一了梯度方法、IG和泰勒展开，并提出了基于合理基线的改进解释方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型解释方法普遍忽略基线，导致解释不精确甚至错误，因此需要重新审视基线的重要性并改进方法。

Method: 重新阐述模型解释任务和原则，统一梯度方法、IG和泰勒展开，分析现有方法缺陷，修正IG并提出基于任意层特征的具有清晰基线的解释方法。

Result: 改进后的方法在解释质量上优于现有方法，并且支持基于不同层特征的合理解释，差异反映特征提取程度。

Conclusion: 明确基线对模型解释至关重要，提出的统一框架和改进方法能有效提升解释精度，为模型解释提供更可靠的工具。

中文摘要：我们观察到现有的模型解释方法通常忽略了基线，这种忽视往往导致不精确甚至错误的解释。在本文中，我们重新阐述了模型解释的任务和模型解释结果的解释原则，以证明基线的重要性。我们首次统一了基于梯度的方法、积分梯度（IG）和泰勒展开，阐明了三者之间的关系，并明确指出了每种方法对应的基线。这可能对某些基于梯度的方法的进一步性能提升产生重要影响。在此基础上，我们分析了相关模型解释方法（IG、LayerCAM、ODAM、差异图）中的缺陷和错误。我们主张通过归因结果与归因目标之间的归因误差来精确评估模型解释的质量，而不是采用有缺陷的评估方法，例如基于边际效应或假设完美模型性能的方法。我们修正了IG，并开发了一种具有清晰合理基线的模型解释方法，取得了更好的结果。我们的方法支持基于任意层特征进行模型解释。基于不同层特征的解释都是合理的，这些结果之间的差异反映了不同特征提取阶段的不同特征提取程度。

Original abstract: We observe that existing model interpretation methods generally ignore the baseline, and such neglect often results in imprecise or even incorrect interpretation. In this paper, we reformulate the task of model interpretation and the interpretation principles for model interpretation results to demonstrate the importance of the baseline. For the first time, we unify gradient-based methods, Integrated Gradients (IG), and Taylor expansion, clarify the relationships among the three, and explicitly identify the corresponding baseline for each method. This may have a significant impact on the further performance improvement of some gradient-based schemes. On this basis, we analyze the flaws and errors in related model interpretation methods (IG, LayerCAM, ODAM, Difference Map). We advocate evaluating the quality of model interpretation results precisely through the attribution error between the attribution result and the attribution target, rather than adopting flawed evaluation methods, such as those based on marginal-effect or the assumption of perfect model performance. We revise IG and develope a model interpretation method with a clear and reasonable baseline, achieving better results. Our method supports model interpretation based on features from any layer. Interpretation based on features from different layers are all reasonable, and the differences among these results reflect varying degrees of feature extraction at different feature extraction stages.

</details>


### [61] [Pre-VLA: Preemptive Runtime Verification for Reliable Vision-Language-Action and World-Model Rollouts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22446v1)
*Zhen Sun,Yongjian Guo,Haoran Sun,Luqiao Wang,Wei Lu,Jiachi Ji,Shengzhe Ji,Junwu Xiong,Zhijun Meng*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出运行时验证架构Pre-VLA，对agent动作进行置信度与安全评估，可迁移至coding agent验证

TL;DR: Pre-VLA 是一种运行时验证架构，通过抢占式动作有效性评估和自适应重采样，提升了 VLA 模型在具身任务中的成功率和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型 VLA 模型和生成式世界模型在长时程具身智能中面临低质量动作导致物理故障或冗余渲染的问题，亟需在部署前对动作质量进行评估。

Method: 提出 Pre-VLA 统一运行时验证架构，包含多模态主干、模态感知池化、轻量级双分支头（预测安全置信度和优势分数），并使用焦点分类、优势回归和软阈值校准的多任务训练，以及双模式抢占式重采样调度器。

Result: 在 LIBERO 基准上，平均闭环成功率从 30.79% 提升至 37.62%，任务执行步数减少，每个动作块平均验证时间 183.9 ms，且减轻了世界模型 rollout 中的误差累积。

Conclusion: Pre-VLA 通过有效的动作质量验证和自适应重采样，显著提升了 VLA 模型在具身任务中的可靠性和效率。

中文摘要：尽管大型视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型和生成式世界模型（WM）推动了长时程具身智能的发展，但其实际部署仍受到基于学习的动作生成中不确定性的挑战。低质量动作可能导致执行过程中的物理故障，或导致冗余渲染成本下的误导性世界模型 rollout。为解决该问题，我们提出 Pre-VLA，一种统一的运行时验证架构，在物理执行或世界模型想象之前执行抢占式动作有效性评估。Pre-VLA 利用高效的多模态主干网络，结合模态感知池化和轻量级双分支头，为候选动作块预测安全置信度和评论家派生的优势分数。为处理严重的类别不平衡和不稳定的边界决策，我们采用多任务目标训练 Pre-VLA，结合焦点分类、优势回归和软阈值校准。在部署时，双模式抢占式重采样调度器过滤低质量动作，并在有限计算预算下触发自适应重采样。在 LIBERO 基准上的实验表明，Pre-VLA 在 RynnVLA-002 基础上将四个套件的平均闭环成功率从 30.79% 提升至 37.62%，减少了任务执行步数，每个动作块的平均前向验证时间为 183.9 毫秒，并减轻了世界模型 rollout 中的误差累积。

Original abstract: While large vision-language-action (VLA) models and generative world models (WM) have advanced long-horizon embodied intelligence, their practical deployment remains challenged by uncertainty in learning-based action generation. Low-quality actions may cause physical failures during execution or lead to misleading world-model rollouts with redundant rendering costs. To address this issue, we propose Pre-VLA, a unified runtime verification architecture that performs preemptive action validity assessment before physical execution or world-model imagination. Pre-VLA leverages an efficient multimodal backbone with modality-aware pooling and a lightweight dual-branch head to predict both safety confidence and critic-derived advantage scores for candidate action chunks. To handle severe class imbalance and unstable boundary decisions, we train Pre-VLA with a multi-task objective combining Focal classification, advantage regression, and soft-threshold calibration. During deployment, a dual-mode preemptive resampling scheduler filters low-quality actions and triggers adaptive resampling under a limited computation budget. Experiments on the LIBERO benchmark show that Pre-VLA improves the average closed-loop success rate across four suites from 30.79\% to 37.62\% over RynnVLA-002, reduces task execution steps, achieves 183.9 ms average forward verification time per action chunk, and mitigates error accumulation in world-model rollouts.

</details>


### [62] [GazeBehavior Annotation Toolkit (GBAT): AI-powered toolkit for automatic annotation of egocentric eye-tracking and video data of child-caregiver interaction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22962v1)
*Iba Baig,Kevin Li,Yanbin Xu,Seiji Cattelain,Marie Hallo,Hayato Ono,Sho Tsuji,Ming Bo Cai*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了一个基于深度学习的GazeBehavior Annotation Toolkit，可自动完成多视频同步、注视目标分类和姿态/手部动作分类，显著提升特征提取效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手动标注儿童-照顾者互动视频数据耗时巨大，限制了大规模和纵向研究。

Method: 开发了深度学习工具包，包含三个关键功能：多视频事后同步、注视目标类别的半自动标注、参与者姿态和手部动作的分类。

Result: 该工具包提高了从眼动追踪和视频数据中提取特征的效率和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 该改进对于支持人类早期发展中注意力动态和自然行为的大规模和纵向研究至关重要。

中文摘要：儿童-照顾者互动的视频记录使得在自然行为中研究注意力动态成为可能。这种多模态记录还允许研究人员实时考察注意力如何与动作和语言使用相互作用。然而，手动标注此类数据非常耗时。在这里，我们介绍了GazeBehavior Annotation Toolkit，这是一个基于深度学习的工具包，旨在促进数据预处理和特征提取中的三个关键过程：多视频的事后同步、注视目标类别的半自动标注，以及参与者姿态和手部动作的分类。该工具包提高了从人类自我中心眼动追踪和视频数据中提取特征的效率和可扩展性。这种改进对于支持人类早期发展中注意力动态和自然行为的大规模和纵向研究至关重要。

Original abstract: Video recordings of child-caregiver interactions enable investigation of attentional dynamics during naturalistic behavior. Such multimodal recording also allows researchers to examine how attention interacts with action and language use in real time. However, manual annotation of such data is time-consuming. Here, we introduce GazeBehavior Annotation Toolkit, a deep-learning-based toolkit designed to facilitate three key processes in data preprocessing and feature extraction: post-hoc synchronization across multiple videos, semi-automatic annotation of gaze target categories, and categorization of participants' poses and hand actions. This toolkit improves the efficiency and scalability of feature extraction from human egocentric eye-tracking and video data. Such improvement is critical in supporting large-scale and longitudinal investigations of attentional dynamics and naturalistic behavior in human early development.
