### [63] [From Reasoning Chains to Verifiable Subproblems: Curriculum Reinforcement Learning Enables Credit Assignment for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22074v1)
*Xitai Jiang,Zihan Tang,Wenze Lin,Yang Yue,Shenzhi Wang,Gao Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出课程强化学习用于LLM推理的信用分配，可迁移至agent的自我改进与探索。

TL;DR: SCRL通过将困难问题分解为可验证的子问题并采用子问题级归一化进行信用分配，显著提升了基于结果的强化学习在数学推理任务中的效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于结果的强化学习在困难问题上效率低，因为正确最终答案的展开样本稀少，且无法利用失败尝试中的部分进展。

Method: 提出SCRL框架，从参考推理链推导可验证子问题，将最终子问题固定为原始问题，并使用子问题级归一化进行细粒度信用分配。

Result: 在七个数学推理基准上，SCRL在Qwen3-4B-Base和Qwen3-14B-Base上分别比GRPO平均准确率提高4.1和1.9个百分点；在AIME24、AIME25和IMO-Bench上，Qwen3-4B-Base的pass@1提高3.7个百分点，pass@64提高4.6个百分点。

Conclusion: SCRL通过子问题课程和细粒度信用分配有效提升了困难推理问题的探索能力和学习效率，优于现有课程学习方法。

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在LLM推理中展现出巨大潜力，但基于结果的RLVR在困难问题上仍然效率低下，因为正确的最终答案展开样本稀少，且样本级别的信用分配无法利用失败尝试中的部分进展。我们提出了SCRL（子问题课程强化学习），这是一种课程RL框架，它从参考推理链中推导出可验证的子问题，并将最终子问题固定为原始问题。这将困难问题上的部分进展转化为可验证的学习信号。在算法上，SCRL使用子问题级别归一化，即在每个子问题位置独立地归一化奖励，并将由此产生的优势分配给对应的答案跨度，从而无需外部评分标准或奖励模型即可实现更细粒度的信用分配。我们的分析表明，子问题课程使困难问题摆脱梯度死区，并且原始问题越难，相对增益越大。在七个数学推理基准上，SCRL优于强课程学习基线，在Qwen3-4B-Base上平均准确率比GRPO提高4.1个百分点，在Qwen3-14B-Base上提高1.9个百分点。在AIME24、AIME25和IMO-Bench上，SCRL进一步将Qwen3-4B-Base的pass@1提高了3.7个百分点，pass@64提高了4.6个百分点，表明在困难推理问题上更好的探索能力。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown strong promise for LLM reasoning, but outcome-based RLVR remains inefficient on hard problems because correct final-answer rollouts are rare and sample-level credit assignment cannot use partial progress in failed attempts. We introduce SCRL (Subproblem Curriculum Reinforcement Learning), a curriculum RL framework that derives verifiable subproblems from reference reasoning chains and fixes the final subproblem as the original problem. This turns partial progress on hard problems into verifiable learning signals. Algorithmically, SCRL uses subproblem-level normalization, which normalizes rewards independently at each subproblem position and assigns the resulting advantages to the corresponding answer spans, enabling finer-grained credit assignment without external rubrics or reward models. Our analysis shows that subproblem curricula lift hard problems out of gradient dead zones, with larger relative gains as the original problem becomes harder. Across seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks, SCRL outperforms strong curriculum-learning baselines, improving average accuracy over GRPO by +4.1 points on Qwen3-4B-Base and +1.9 points on Qwen3-14B-Base. On AIME24, AIME25, and IMO-Bench, SCRL further improves pass@1 by +3.7 points and pass@64 by +4.6 points on Qwen3-4B-Base, indicating better exploration on hard reasoning problems.

</details>


### [64] [Short-Term-to-Long-Term Memory Transfer for Knowledge Graphs under Partial Observability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22142v2)
*Taewoon Kim,Vincent François-Lavet,Michael Cochez*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究短期到长期记忆转移，使用强化学习进行记忆决策，对agent记忆管理有潜在迁移。

TL;DR: 本文提出在时序知识图谱记忆场景下，通过神经符号化的Q学习策略学习符号观测的短期到长期记忆转移决策，在RoomKG基准上优于基线方法，实现了可解释的记忆管理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于记忆的强化学习方法未明确建模符号观测从短期到长期的转移过程，而该过程对于部分可观测性下的决策至关重要。

Method: 将短期到长期记忆转移建模为神经符号化的基于价值决策问题，对每个观测三元组，智能体使用每个项目的Q学习（共享参数）选择保留或丢弃，并通过时序差分更新匹配项目。

Result: 在RoomKG基准（长期记忆容量128）上，学到的转移决策优于符号化及LSTM/Transformer基线；消融实验显示轻量级短期局部变体最佳；策略能保留导航和查询相关事实，丢弃低价值候选事实。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了在记忆约束下明确且可解释的记忆决策，验证了神经符号化记忆转移策略的有效性。

中文摘要：在部分可观测性下的强化学习需要决定保留哪些信息，但大多数基于记忆的方法并未明确建模符号观测从短期到长期的转移过程。我们在时序知识图谱记忆设置中研究这一转移过程，并将其视为一个神经符号化的基于价值决策问题：对于每个观测到的三元组，智能体在长期插入前选择保留或丢弃它。为了处理可变大小的短期缓冲区，我们采用了每个项目的Q学习设计，使用共享参数，并对连续步骤中的匹配项目进行实用的时序差分更新。在长期记忆容量为128的RoomKG基准测试中，学到的转移决策优于符号化基线（包括带时间标注的符号化基线）和基于历史的LSTM/Transformer基线。在转移策略消融实验中，一个轻量级的仅短期局部变体表现最佳，而逐步行为显示该策略保留导航和查询相关的事实，同时丢弃价值较低的候选事实，支持在记忆约束下进行明确且可解释的记忆决策。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning under partial observability requires deciding what information to retain, yet most memory-based approaches do not explicitly model short-term-to-long-term transfer of symbolic observations. We study this transfer process in a temporal knowledge-graph memory setting and cast it as a neuro-symbolic value-based decision problem: for each observed triple, the agent chooses whether to keep or drop it before long-term insertion. To handle variable-sized short-term buffers, we use a per-item Q-learning design with shared parameters and a practical temporal-difference update over matched items across consecutive steps. On the RoomKG benchmark at long-term memory capacity 128, learned transfer decisions outperform symbolic and neural baselines, including symbolic baselines with temporal annotations and history-based LSTM/Transformer baselines. Across transfer-policy ablations, a lightweight local short-term-only variant performs best, and step-level behavior shows that the policy keeps navigation- and query-relevant facts while discarding lower-value candidate facts, supporting explicit and interpretable memory decisions under memory constraints.

</details>


### [65] [One-Way Policy Optimization for Self-Evolving LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22156v1)
*Shuo Yang,Jinda Lu,Kexin Huang,Chiyu Ma,Shaohang Wei,Yuyang Liu,Guoyin Wang,Jingren Zhou,Li Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 针对LLM推理的RLVR策略优化，虽非直接agent但可借鉴训练机制。

TL;DR: OWPO是一种新颖的RLVR方法，通过非对称重加权和迭代参考更新解耦优化方向与幅度，实现了无需外部参考模型的持续自我进化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二元验证器奖励的稀疏性导致低效率和优化不稳定，而现有的令牌级约束无差别地惩罚所有偏差，当策略超越参考时会翻转验证器确定的方向，从而限制性能提升。

Method: OWPO通过让验证器决定更新方向、参考策略仅调整幅度来解耦方向与幅度。它对劣后偏差采用加速对齐，对优越偏差采用增益锁定，并通过迭代参考更新形成棘轮效应以巩固收益。

Result: OWPO在多个强基线（DAPO、OPD、MOPD）上表现更优，打破了固定先验的瓶颈，实现了无需外部参考模型的持续自我进化。

Conclusion: OWPO提出了一种原则性方法，在稳定RLVR训练的同时允许策略无惩罚地超越参考，从而实现持续改进。

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为扩展大型语言模型（LLMs）推理能力的一种有前景的范式。然而，二元验证器奖励的稀疏性常常导致低效率和优化不稳定。为了稳定训练，现有方法通常对参考策略施加令牌级约束。我们识别出，这种约束无差别地惩罚偏差；当策略试图超越参考时，这会翻转验证器确定的方向，从而抑制增益。为了解决这个问题，我们提出单向策略优化（OWPO），一种基于解耦优化方向与更新幅度原则的方法。在OWPO中，验证器决定更新方向，而参考策略仅用于调整幅度。具体来说，OWPO应用非对称重加权：对劣后偏差（策略落后于参考）执行加速对齐，对优越偏差（策略超越参考）执行增益锁定。此外，通过结合迭代参考更新，OWPO创建了“棘轮效应”，持续巩固收益。实验结果表明，OWPO优于强基线方法，包括DAPO、OPD和MOPD，打破了固定先验的瓶颈，实现了无需依赖外部参考模型的持续自我进化。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a promising paradigm for scaling reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the sparsity of binary verifier rewards often leads to low efficiency and optimization instability. To stabilize training, existing methods typically impose token-level constraints relative to a reference policy. We identify that such constraints penalize deviations indiscriminately; this can flip verifier-determined direction when the policy attempts to outperform the reference, thereby suppressing gains. To resolve this, we propose One-Way Policy Optimization (OWPO), a method based on the principle of decoupling optimization direction from update magnitude. In OWPO, the verifier dictates the update direction, while the reference policy serves only to adjust the magnitude. Specifically, OWPO applies asymmetric reweighting: it performs Accelerated Alignment for inferior deviations (where the policy lags behind the reference) and Gain Locking for superior deviations (where the policy surpasses the reference). Furthermore, by incorporating iterative reference updates, OWPO creates a ``Ratchet Effect'' that continuously consolidates gains. Experimental results demonstrate that OWPO outperforms strong baselines, including DAPO, OPD, and MOPD, breaking the bottleneck of fixed priors to enable continuous self-evolution without reliance on external reference models.

</details>


### [66] [Can Transformers Learn to Verify During Backtracking Search?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22221v1)
*Yin Jun Phua,Tony Ribeiro,Tuan Nguyen,Katsumi Inoue*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究transformer在回溯搜索中的验证能力，可迁移到agent规划推理。

TL;DR: 提出局部化和选择性状态注意力机制，解决 Transformer 在搜索轨迹上因历史纠缠和分散检索导致的决策不一致问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Transformer 推理系统在搜索轨迹上训练时，因依赖累积历史而非当前状态，导致决策不一致，影响搜索效率。

Method: 提出轨迹级别的局部化重写以暴露状态特征，以及选择性状态注意力（SSA）掩码强制基于状态决策，无需修改训练数据或参数。

Result: 在 3-SAT、图染色、积木世界和回溯解析任务中，SSA 使得同状态不同历史的输入产生相同决策，而因果基线则不能。

Conclusion: 通过诊断和结构性修复，改善了 Transformer 在搜索轨迹上的决策一致性，并指出预训练语言模型的类似问题可通过推理时上下文清理缓解。

中文摘要：回溯搜索是经典约束求解器、规划器和定理证明器的基础。近年来基于 Transformer 的推理系统在其自身的中间步骤上探索搜索树。一种常见的训练方法是在离线求解器轨迹上拟合自回归的下一个词元损失。模型在每一步的输入是所有先前决策的累积轨迹。最优的继续或回溯决策仅取决于当前搜索状态，因为到达相同状态的两条轨迹允许相同的可行延续。我们展示了仅在累积轨迹上训练的仅解码器 Transformer 在两方面未能满足这一要求：轨迹可能将状态特征分散到多个位置（分散检索），并且预测器可能基于轨迹而非状态条件化（历史纠缠）。我们通过局部化（一种轨迹级别的修复，重写每个决策块以本地暴露状态特征）来解决分散检索。我们通过选择性状态注意力（SSA，一种固定的注意力掩码，强制在结构上基于状态进行决策，而无需修改训练数据、目标或参数）来解决历史纠缠。我们专注于反应式验证，即在传播揭示矛盾之后。我们在 3-SAT、图染色、积木世界和回溯解析上测试了 SSA。在仅历史记录不同的同状态对上，SSA 做出相同的决策，而累积训练的因果基线则不然。我们的贡献在于对 Transformer 在序列化轨迹数据上的行为进行诊断，并配以结构性的修复。预训练语言模型若在其自身推理步骤上进行搜索，可能面临相同的失败。我们的分析为推理时的上下文清理提供了一种候选方法，以在不重新训练的情况下应用相同的隔离。

Original abstract: Backtracking search underlies classical constraint solvers, planners, and theorem provers. Recent transformer-based reasoning systems explore search trees over their own intermediate steps. A common training recipe fits an autoregressive next-token loss on offline solver traces. The model's input at each step is a cumulative trace of all prior decisions. The optimal continue-or-backtrack predictor depends only on the current search state, since two trajectories reaching the same state admit the same viable continuations. We show that decoder-only transformers trained on cumulative traces fail this requirement in two ways: the trace can scatter state features across many positions (scattered retrieval), and the predictor can condition on the trajectory rather than the state (history entanglement). We address scattered retrieval with localization, a trace-level fix that rewrites each decision block to expose state features locally. We address history entanglement with Selective State Attention (SSA), a fixed attention mask that enforces state-based decisions structurally without modifying training data, objective, or parameters. We focus on reactive verification, after propagation has exposed a contradiction. We test SSA on 3-SAT, graph coloring, Blocks World, and backtracking parsing. On same-state pairs that differ only in prior history, SSA emits identical decisions while a cumulative-trained causal baseline does not. Our contribution is a diagnostic of transformer behavior on serialized trajectory data, paired with a structural fix. Pretrained language models that search over their own reasoning steps may face the same failure. Our analysis opens up inference-time context clearing as a candidate way to apply the same isolation without retraining.

</details>


### [67] [What are the Right Symmetries for Formal Theorem Proving?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22257v1)
*Krzysztof Olejniczak,Radoslav Dimitrov,Xingyue Huang,Bernardo Cuenca Grau,Jinwoo Kim,İsmail İlkan Ceylan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 形式定理证明中的对称性，可迁移到coding agent中的推理鲁棒性。

TL;DR: 提出重写范畴形式化定理证明中的对称性，发现LLM证明器缺乏对称性，通过测试时聚合等效重写恢复成功不变性并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM定理证明器对问题表示的表面变化高度敏感，语义等价的语句成功率差异巨大，缺乏对形式数学中结构对称性的尊重，需要明确正确的对称性并加以利用。

Method: 引入重写范畴（范畴论框架），形式化证明等变性和成功不变性；提出测试时方法，聚合输入的等价重写，在采样极限下理论上恢复成功不变性。

Result: 理论证明在采样极限下恢复成功不变性；实验表明在固定推理预算下提高了鲁棒性和性能。

Conclusion: 对称性是基于LLM的定理证明中一个关键缺失的归纳偏置，测试时计算是逼近它的实用途径。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的形式定理证明器对问题表示的表面变化高度敏感：语义等价的语句可能表现出截然不同的证明成功率，这揭示出它们未能尊重形式数学中固有的结构对称性。这引出了一个核心问题：形式定理证明的正确对称性是什么？我们引入了重写范畴（rewriting categories），这是一个范畴论框架，用于捕捉由证明策略引发的组合性、通常不可逆的变换，并用它来形式化两种对称性概念：证明等变性（proof equivariance），控制证明分布在重写下的变换方式；以及成功不变性（success invariance，即成功概率的不变性），要求等价语句以相同概率被解决。我们观察到，基于状态的下一个策略证明器通过操作证明状态自然满足证明等变性。相比之下，最先进的基于LLM的证明器既不满足任何一条性质，在等价表述之间表现出巨大的性能差异。为了缓解这一问题，我们提出了测试时方法，对输入的等价重写进行聚合，理论上表明它们在采样极限下恢复了成功不变性，并在实验中表明在固定推理预算下提高了鲁棒性和性能。我们的结果强调了对称性是基于LLM的定理证明中一个关键缺失的归纳偏置，并建议测试时计算作为逼近它的实用途径。

Original abstract: Formal theorem provers based on large language models (LLMs) are highly sensitive to superficial variations in problem representation: semantically equivalent statements can exhibit drastically different proof success rates, revealing a failure to respect structural symmetries inherent in formal mathematics. This raises a central question: what are the right symmetries for formal theorem proving? We introduce rewriting categories, a category-theoretic framework capturing the compositional, generally non-invertible transformations induced by proof tactics, and use it to formalize two symmetry notions: proof equivariance, governing how proof distributions transform under rewrites, and success invariance (i.e., invariance of success probability), requiring equivalent statements to be solved with the same probability. We observe that state-based next-tactic provers naturally satisfy proof equivariance by operating on proof states. In contrast, state-of-the-art LLM-based provers satisfy neither property, exhibiting large performance variation across equivalent formulations. To mitigate this, we propose test-time methods that aggregate over equivalent rewritings of the input, showing theoretically that they recover success invariance in the sampling limit, and empirically, that they improve robustness and performance under fixed inference budgets. Our results highlight symmetry as a key missing inductive bias in LLM-based theorem proving and suggest test-time computation as a practical route to approximate it.

</details>


### [68] [Tailoring Teaching to Aptitude: Direction-Adaptive Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22263v1)
*Hongbin Zhang,Chaozheng Wang,Kehai Chen,Youcheng Pan,Yang Xiang,Jinpeng Wang,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自适应蒸馏提高LLM推理，非直接agent但方法可参考。

TL;DR: 提出方向自适应自蒸馏（DASD），根据令牌熵值动态调整监督方向：高熵令牌推离教师以保持探索，低熵令牌拉向教师以稳定执行，在数学推理任务上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有同策略自蒸馏（OPSD）通过抑制预测不确定性损害复杂推理，原因是对所有令牌施加统一的教师监督方向，未能区分高熵（需探索）和低熵（需精确执行）令牌的不同需求。

Method: 提出方向自适应自蒸馏（DASD），根据令牌的熵值路由监督方向：高熵令牌被推离特权教师以鼓励探索，低熵令牌被拉向教师以巩固步骤准确性。

Result: 在六个数学推理基准上，DASD在Avg@16宏观指标上优于强RLVR和自蒸馏基线，且Pass@k、推理健康度和泛化分析表明其同时保持了探索和步骤执行。

Conclusion: DASD通过熵路由的方向监督有效平衡了探索与利用，在不牺牲步骤级精度的前提下提升了复杂推理性能，验证了自适应蒸馏方向的重要性。

中文摘要：同策略自蒸馏（OPSD）是一种新兴的大语言模型后训练范式，其中模型作为自身的教师：基于特权信息（如参考轨迹或提示），同一策略在其自身生成上提供密集的令牌级监督。然而，最近的研究表明，OPSD通过抑制预测不确定性（支持探索和假设修订）而损害了复杂推理。我们的令牌级分析表明，这种失败源于对不同不确定性水平的令牌应用统一的教师监督方向：顺从于特权自教师会抑制高熵时的探索，而偏离教师则会降低低熵时的步骤准确性。因此，我们提出了方向自适应自蒸馏（DASD），它将特权自蒸馏从统一的教师模仿重构为熵路由的方向监督：高熵令牌被推离特权教师以保持探索，而低熵令牌被拉向教师以稳定步骤级执行。在六个数学推理基准上，DASD在Avg@16宏观指标上超过了强RLVR和自蒸馏基线。Pass@k、推理健康度和泛化分析表明，这些平均收益源于在保持步骤级执行的同时保留了探索。

Original abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) is an emerging LLM post-training paradigm in which the model serves as its own teacher: conditioned on privileged information such as a reference trace or hint, the same policy provides dense token-level supervision on its own rollouts. However, recent studies show that OPSD degrades complex reasoning by suppressing predictive uncertainty, which supports exploration and hypothesis revision. Our token-level analysis shows that this failure arises from applying a uniform direction of teacher supervision across tokens with different uncertainty levels: conformity to the privileged self-teacher suppresses exploration at high entropy, while deviation from the teacher degrades step accuracy at low entropy. Accordingly, we propose \textbf{Direction-Adaptive Self-Distillation} (\textbf{DASD}), which reframes privileged self-distillation from uniform teacher imitation into entropy-routed directional supervision: high-entropy tokens are pushed away from the privileged teacher to preserve exploration, while low-entropy tokens are pulled toward the teacher to stabilize step-level execution. Across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks, DASD achieves the best macro Avg@16 over strong RLVR and self-distillation baselines. Pass@$k$, reasoning-health, and generalization analyses show that these average gains come from preserving exploration without sacrificing step-level execution.

</details>


### [69] [VeriScale: Adversarial Test-Suite Scaling for Verifiable Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22368v1)
*Yifan Bai,Xiaoyang Liu,Zihao Mou,Guihong Wang,Jian Yu,Shuhan Xie,Yantao Li,Yangyu Zhang,Jingwei Liang,Tao Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出VeriScale框架，通过对抗性实现驱动的测试套件扩展和缩减，构建高质量基准，揭示LLM在代码生成和规约生成中的弱点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准的正负测试用例数量和质量有限，导致高估模型在生成规约和实现方面的能力。

Method: 两阶段框架：测试套件扩展（构建多样挑战性测试用例）和测试套件缩减（提炼紧凑有区分度的套件），实例化为VerinaPlus和VerinaLite。

Result: VerinaPlus将测试套件扩展83倍以上，八个LLM上得分大幅下降，暴露模型弱点；VerinaLite以14倍成本保持区分度。

中文摘要：随着大型语言模型在软件工程中的部署日益增多，构建高质量的基准测试对于评估生成代码的功能正确性以及形式化可验证性至关重要。然而，现有基准测试由于正负测试用例的数量和质量有限，导致在生成规约和实现方面对模型能力的高估。为解决这一问题，我们提出了VeriScale，一种由对抗性实现驱动的新型框架。它包括两个阶段：测试套件扩展，以构建多样且具有挑战性的测试用例；以及测试套件缩减，将其提炼为紧凑但具有区分度的套件。虽然VeriScale是通用的，但我们在Verina上实例化它，构建了VerinaPlus（将原始测试套件扩展超过83倍）和VerinaLite（一个轻量级的14倍变体）。我们在八个最先进的大型语言模型上的实验表明，VerinaPlus暴露了原始基准所隐藏的模型弱点，这在SpecGen和CodeGen任务上的得分大幅下降中得到了证明，而VerinaLite则以极低的评估成本保持了这种区分能力。增强的基准和源代码可在https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/VeriScale公开获取。

Original abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed for software engineering, constructing high-quality benchmarks is crucial for evaluating not just the functional correctness, but also the formal verifiability of generated code. However, existing benchmarks are limited by the quantity and quality of positive and negative test cases, leading to an overestimation of model capabilities in generating specifications and implementations. To address this, we propose VeriScale, a novel framework driven by the adversarial implementations. It consists of two stages: test-suite expansion to construct diverse and challenging test cases, and test-suite reduction to distill them into compact yet discriminative suites. While VeriScale is general, we instantiate it on Verina to construct VerinaPlus, which expands the original test suites by over 83$\times$, and VerinaLite, a lightweight 14$\times$ variant. Our experiments across eight state-of-the-art LLMs demonstrate that VerinaPlus exposes substantial model weaknesses hidden by the original benchmark, evidenced by sharp score drops on both SpecGen and CodeGen tasks, whereas VerinaLite maintains this discriminative power at a fraction of the evaluation cost. The enhanced benchmarks and source code are publicly available at https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/VeriScale.

### [70] [Don't Forget the Critic: Value-Based Data Rehearsal for Multi-Cyclic Continual Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22454v1)
*Benjamin Poole,Andrew Quinn,Li Yang,Minwoo Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 持续RL中数据排练方法，可迁移至agent的灾难性遗忘缓解

TL;DR: 提出了Qreg+NWLU，通过连续数据重演和无等待正则化，在多循环持续强化学习中改进了Q值正则化的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据重演在持续强化学习中仅限于策略梯度框架且仅正则化演员，忽略了值函数逼近的潜力，且评估未考虑多循环环境。

Method: 在深度Q网络中使用Q值正则化，引入连续数据重演（动态收集和更新存储的Q值）和无等待正则化（立即应用而非延迟）。

Result: 在学习效率、遗忘缓解和知识迁移方面优于Qreg和传统方法。

Conclusion: 简单的修改即可显著提升值函数逼近中的持续学习性能。

中文摘要：数据重演已成为缓解持续强化学习中灾难性遗忘的主要方法。然而，现有工作仍局限于策略梯度框架，由于评论家正则化导致的性能下降，仅对演员进行正则化。这种以演员为中心的方法忽视了数据重演在值函数逼近中的潜力。此外，现有的持续强化学习评估很少考虑任务序列重复的多循环环境，这是一种加剧遗忘和可塑性的关键现实场景。我们研究了多循环设置下使用Q值正则化的深度Q网络的数据重演，并提出了Qreg+NWLU，它引入了两个简单修改：(1) 连续数据重演，在训练过程中动态收集和更新存储的Q值，以及(2) “无等待”正则化，该正则化在第一个任务之后立即应用而非延迟。这些修改共同在学习效率、遗忘缓解和知识迁移方面相对于Qreg和传统持续强化学习方法在值函数逼近设置中取得了改进。

Original abstract: Data rehearsal has emerged as a leading approach for mitigating catastrophic forgetting in Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL). However, existing work remains confined to policy gradient frameworks, regularizing only actors due to the performance degradation incurred by critic regularization. This actor-centric approach overlooks the potential of data rehearsal for value function approximation. Moreover, existing evaluations in CRL rarely consider multi-cyclic environments where task sequences repeat, a critical real-world scenario that exacerbates forgetting and plasticity. We investigate data rehearsal for Deep Q-Networks using Q-value regularization in multi-cyclic settings and propose Qreg+NWLU which introduces two simple modifications: (1) continuous data rehearsal that dynamically collects and updates stored Q-values throughout training, and (2) "No-Wait" regularization that applies immediately rather than after the first task. Together, these modifications yield improvements in learning efficiency, forgetting mitigation, and knowledge transfer over Qreg and conventional CRL methods within value function approximation settings.

</details>


### [71] [Understanding Multimodal Failure in Action-Chunking Behavioral Cloning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22493v1)
*Lorenzo Mazza,Massimiliano Datres,Ariel Rodriguez,Sebastian Bodenstedt,Gitta Kutyniok,Stefanie Speidel*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 分析多模态行为克隆失败模式，对agent学习（模仿学习）有启示

TL;DR: 研究了行为克隆中多模态动作分布的问题，分析了潜在变量和动作空间生成策略的失效机制，并通过实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行为克隆中同一观测对应多个有效动作导致学习困难，需要理解不同参数化方法处理多模态性的方式。

Method: 理论分析潜在变量策略的后验-先验正则化权衡以及动作空间生成策略的Lipschitz约束，并在合成和仿真任务上实验验证。

Result: 过度正则化破坏模式区分，不足则依赖先验覆盖；生成策略中多模态需要尖锐过渡或桥接区域。

Conclusion: 不同多模态参数化有不同失效模式，需根据实际任务调整正则化或生成策略的平滑性。

中文摘要：当同一个观测对应多个有效动作时，行为克隆变得困难。我们研究了动作分块策略中的这个问题，并展示了不同的多模态参数化方式以不同的方式失败。对于潜在变量策略，后验-先验正则化使得部署时的采样更可靠，但过度的正则化会移除用于区分演示模式的动作条件信息。减少这种正则化可以保留模式信息，但成功与否取决于先验是否覆盖了相关的潜在区域。对于动作空间生成策略，多模态性受到基础到动作传输平滑度的限制：具有小Lipschitz常数的映射无法为许多分离良好的模式分配显著概率。因此，覆盖许多模式要么需要基础空间中的尖锐过渡，要么需要动作空间中的离支撑桥接区域。在合成多模态任务和机器人仿真基准上的实验支持了这些机制。

Original abstract: Behavioral cloning becomes difficult when the same observation admits several valid actions. We study this problem for action-chunking policies and show that different multimodal parameterizations fail in different ways. For latent-variable policies, posterior-prior regularization makes deployment-time sampling more reliable, but excessive regularization removes the action-conditioned information needed to distinguish demonstrated modes. Reducing this regularization can preserve mode information, but then success depends on whether the prior covers the relevant latent regions. For action-space generative policies, multimodality is constrained by the smoothness of the base-to-action transport: a map with small Lipschitz constant cannot assign substantial probability to many well-separated modes. Covering many modes therefore requires either sharp transitions in base space or off-support bridge regions in action space. Experiments on synthetic multimodal tasks and robotic simulation benchmarks support these mechanisms.

### [72] [The Neural Compiler: Program-to-Network Translation for Hybrid Scientific Machine Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22498v1)
*Lucas Sheneman*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出神经网络编译器，将程序编译为可微模块，直接相关自动代码优化与混合科学ML

TL;DR: 神经编译器将符号方程自动翻译为可微分的PyTorch模块，实现精确物理编码与高精度参数恢复，且支持零误差组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学机器学习方法难以同时融合已知物理规律与数据驱动学习，要么忽略结构、要么需要手动编码，缺乏系统性和可组合性。

Method: 提出神经编译器，将类Scheme表达式语言编写的程序编译为冻结、可微分的PyTorch模块，通过自动求导提供梯度，支持51种基本操作。

Result: 编译模块在六个实验领域与手动编码实现数值匹配，参数恢复误差小于1%（1-4参数），而PINN误差7-93%；模块组合误差为零。

Conclusion: 神经编译器的主要价值在于系统性的可组合性，能够从符号规范自动生成正确、可微分的模块，无需手动重写方程，并为大语言模型提供接口。

中文摘要：科学机器学习通常需要将已知的物理规律与从数据中学习的未知参数或修正项相结合。现有方法要么忽略已知结构，要么将其编码为软惩罚，要么需要为每个方程手动编写PyTorch代码。我们提出了神经编译器，该系统将用一阶类Scheme表达式语言编写的程序翻译成冻结的、可微分的PyTorch模块。这些模块在浮点精度上匹配源程序，并通过自动求导提供梯度。在混合模型中，编译模块精确编码已知物理，而学习组件建模未知剩余部分。我们在六个实验领域评估了编译器：费曼物理方程、洛特卡-沃尔泰拉动力学、阻尼摆、一维热方程、三维矢量力学和组合泛化。对于单个方程，编译模块在数值上匹配手动编码的PyTorch实现，显示编译没有精度损失。仅用1到4个可训练参数，编译模型在大多数情况下恢复物理常数的误差小于1%，而拥有超过8500个参数的标准PINN基线显示出7%到93%的误差。编译模块的组合误差为零，而神经逼近在深层组合链中可能累积大误差。编译器的主要价值不在于比手动编码方程提高精度，而在于系统性的可组合性：它从符号规范生成正确、可微分的模块，无需为每个方程手动重写。该系统支持51种基本操作，包括向量和矩阵代数，支持PDE离散化和混合科学模型。这种字符串输入、模块输出的接口也为将科学描述翻译为可执行可微分模块的大型语言模型提供了自然目标。

Original abstract: Scientific machine learning often requires combining known physics with unknown parameters or correction terms learned from data. Existing approaches either ignore known structure, encode it as a soft penalty, or require hand-written PyTorch code for each equation. We present The Neural Compiler, a system that translates programs written in a first-order Scheme-like expression language into frozen, differentiable PyTorch modules. These modules match the source program to floating-point precision and provide gradients through autograd. In hybrid models, the compiled module encodes known physics exactly while learned components model the unknown remainder. We evaluate the compiler across six experiment domains: Feynman physics equations, Lotka-Volterra dynamics, a damped pendulum, a one-dimensional heat equation, three-dimensional vector mechanics, and compositional generalization. Compiled modules match hand-coded PyTorch implementations numerically for single equations, showing no accuracy loss from compilation. With only 1 to 4 trainable parameters, compiled models recover physical constants to less than 1 percent error in most cases, while standard PINN baselines with more than 8500 parameters show 7 to 93 percent error. Compiled modules also compose with zero error, while neural approximations can accumulate large errors in deep composition chains. The main value of the compiler is not improved accuracy over hand-coded equations, but systematic composability: it generates correct, differentiable modules from symbolic specifications without rewriting each equation by hand. The system supports 51 primitive operations, including vector and matrix algebra, enabling PDE discretizations and hybrid scientific models. This string-in, module-out interface also provides a natural target for large language models that translate scientific descriptions into executable differentiable modules.

### [73] [Post-Training is About States, Not Tokens: A State Distribution View of SFT, RL, and On-Policy Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22731v1)
*Dong Nie*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 从状态分布视角分析后训练方法（SFT、RL、蒸馏），对理解agent学习机制与on-policy训练有启示。

TL;DR: 研究了后训练中状态分布的影响，发现状态来源和局域性比监督信号形式更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练方法分析集中于损失函数，忽略了状态分布的影响，本文旨在补充这一视角。

Method: 使用Qwen3-0.6B-Base在GSM8K上进行受控小规模实验，对比SFT、在线策略蒸馏和在线策略RL，以TruthfulQA和MMLU评估保留性能。

Result: 温和SFT少量遗忘，压力SFT显著遗忘；在线策略蒸馏从退化教师中超越教师；轻量在线策略RL提升目标任务同时保留记忆。

Conclusion: 后训练中状态分布（来源和局域性）与监督信号形式同等重要，支持以状态为中心的观点。

中文摘要：大型语言模型的后训练方法，如监督微调（SFT）、强化学习（RL）和蒸馏，通常通过其损失函数进行分析：最大似然、策略梯度、前向KL、反向KL或相关的目标层面对应物。我们研究了一个补充因素：施加监督的状态分布。对于自回归策略，状态是提示加上生成的前缀。SFT在固定数据集的状态上训练，而RL和在线策略蒸馏（OPD）在当前学习器诱导的状态上训练。我们将后训练形式化为状态分布塑造，并使用Qwen3-0.6B-Base在GSM8K上进行受控的小规模研究，以TruthfulQA和MMLU作为保留评估。我们的结果显示了三个现象。第一，温和的SFT运行在GSM8K上有所提升且遗忘很少，而压力SFT运行导致显著的保留损失。第二，来自退化SFT教师的OPD在GSM8K、TruthfulQA和MMLU上超越了该教师，尽管仅使用教师作为其唯一的监督源。第三，轻量级的在线策略RL运行在提高GSM8K的同时保留了记忆。这些结果支持一种以状态为中心的后训练观点：训练状态的来源和局域性可能与监督信号的形式同等重要。

Original abstract: Large language model post-training methods such as supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning (RL), and distillation are often analyzed through their loss functions: maximum likelihood, policy gradients, forward KL, reverse KL, or related objective-level variants. We study a complementary factor: the state distribution on which supervision is applied. For an autoregressive policy, a state is a prompt plus generated prefix. SFT trains on fixed dataset states, while RL and on-policy distillation (OPD) train on states induced by the current learner. We formalize post-training as state-distribution shaping and run a controlled smallscale study using Qwen3-0.6B-Base on GSM8K, with TruthfulQA and MMLU as retention evaluations. Our results show three phenomena. First, a mild SFT run improves GSM8K with little forgetting, while a stress SFT run causes substantial retention loss. Second, OPD from a degraded SFT teacher surpasses that teacher on GSM8K, TruthfulQA, and MMLU, despite using the teacher as its only supervision source. Third, a lightweight on-policy RL run improves GSM8K while preserving retention. These results support a state-centric view of post-training: the source and locality of training states can be as important as the form of the supervision signal.

### [74] [Vector Policy Optimization: Training for Diversity Improves Test-Time Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22817v1)
*Ryan Bahlous-Boldi,Isha Puri,Idan Shenfeld,Akarsh Kumar,Mehul Damani,Sebastian Risi,Omar Khattab,Zhang-Wei Hong,Pulkit Agrawal*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 训练策略多样化提升测试时搜索，可迁移至agent规划搜索

TL;DR: VPO是一种RL算法，通过训练LLM产生多样化解来适应不同奖励函数，提升推理时搜索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准标量奖励训练导致低熵分布，缺乏多样性，无法满足推理时搜索需求。

Method: VPO利用向量奖励，训练LLM输出一组解决方案，每个方案针对不同奖励权衡。

Result: 在四个任务上，VPO匹配或超越标量RL基线，搜索预算越大优势越明显，进化搜索中解决GRPO无法解决的问题。

Conclusion: 随着测试时搜索标准化，优化多样性应成为默认后训练目标。

中文摘要：语言模型现在必须能够直接泛化到新环境，并在推理时搜索过程（如AlphaEvolve）中工作，这些过程使用各种任务特定的奖励函数来选择rollouts。不幸的是，标准的LLM后训练范式优化的是预先指定的标量奖励，这常常导致当前LLM产生低熵的响应分布，从而难以展示推理时搜索所需的多样性。我们提出了向量策略优化（VPO），一种RL算法，它显式地训练策略以预期多样化的下游奖励函数并产生多样化的解决方案。VPO利用实践中奖励通常是向量值的这一特点，比如代码生成中每个测试用例的正确性，或者多个不同的用户角色或奖励模型。VPO本质上是GRPO优势估计器的即插即用替代方案，但它训练LLM输出一组解决方案，其中各个解决方案专攻向量奖励空间中的不同权衡。在四个任务上，VPO在测试时搜索（如pass@k和best@k）上与最强的标量RL基线相当或更优，并且随着搜索预算的增加，差距扩大。对于进化搜索，VPO模型解决了GRPO模型根本无法解决的问题。随着测试时搜索变得更加标准化，优化多样性可能需要成为默认的后训练目标。

Original abstract: Language models must now generalize out of the box to novel environments and work inside inference-scaling search procedures, such as AlphaEvolve, that select rollouts with a variety of task-specific reward functions. Unfortunately, the standard paradigm of LLM post-training optimizes a pre-specified scalar reward, often leading current LLMs to produce low-entropy response distributions and thus to struggle at displaying the diversity that inference-time search will require. We propose Vector Policy Optimization (VPO), an RL algorithm that explicitly trains policies to anticipate diverse downstream reward functions and to produce diverse solutions. VPO exploits that rewards are often vector-valued in practice, like per-test-case correctness in code generation or, say, multiple different user personas or reward models. VPO is essentially a drop-in replacement for the GRPO advantage estimator, but it trains the LLM to output a set of solutions where individual solutions specialize to different trade-offs in the vector reward space. Across four tasks, VPO matches or beats the strongest scalar RL baselines on test-time search (e.g. pass@k and best@k), with the gap widening as the search budget grows. For evolutionary search, VPO models unlock problems that GRPO models cannot solve at all. As test-time search becomes more standardized, optimizing for diversity may need to become the default post-training objective.

### [75] [Test-Time Training Undermines Safety Guardrails](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22984v1)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时训练虽然能提升模型性能，但其动态调整特性引入了新的安全风险，攻击者可利用这些漏洞绕过安全过滤器，因此需要研究其威胁和防御。

Method: 论文识别了TTT的三种威胁模型，通过实验展示了攻击成功率，并提出了有效性感知评估和基于困惑度变化的检测器。

中文摘要：测试时训练（TTT）是一种新兴范式，使模型在推理过程中能够调整其参数，从而提升在少样本学习、检索增强生成和复杂推理等任务上的性能。然而，这种动态适应引入了新的漏洞，攻击者可利用这些漏洞破解模型。我们识别了TTT的三种威胁模型，并展示了攻击者如何利用它们绕过安全过滤器。我们的结果表明，TTT可以显著提高攻击成功率（ASR）以及在10次生成试验中的ASR（ASR@10）。例如，在LoRA下，少样本和生成阶段的威胁模型在不同模型族和规模上平均ASR@10分别达到95%和93%。这些漏洞可迁移到生产微调API。我们还展示了TTT引发的过拟合可能产生退化输出，从而在标准评判者下虚增ASR，并提出了一个有效性感知评估来纠正这一点。我们的发现表明，TTT暴露了新的攻击面，强化了攻击，并削弱了现有的安全护栏。作为防御的第一步，我们提出了一个轻量级的提供方侧检测器，通过私有有害保留集上的困惑度变化来标记TTT请求，但稳健部署最终需要动态对齐。

Original abstract: Test-Time Training (TTT) is an emerging paradigm that enables models to adapt their parameters during inference, improving performance on tasks such as few-shot learning, retrieval-augmented generation, and complex reasoning. However, this dynamic adaptation introduces new vulnerabilities that adversaries can exploit to jailbreak models. We identify three threat models for TTT and demonstrate how attackers can leverage them to bypass safety filters. Our results show that TTT can significantly increase the Attack Success Rate (ASR) and the ASR over 10 generation trials (ASR@10). For example, under LoRA, the few-shot and generation-phase threat models achieve an average ASR@10 of 95% and 93% respectively, across models from different families and scales. These vulnerabilities transfer to production fine-tuning APIs. We also show that TTT-induced overfitting can produce degenerate outputs that inflate ASR under standard judges, and propose a validity-aware evaluation to correct for this. Our findings suggest that TTT exposes a new attack surface, strengthens attacks, and undermines existing safety guardrails. As a first step toward defense, we propose a lightweight provider-side detector that flags TTT requests via the perplexity shift on a private harmful holdout, but robust deployment will ultimately require dynamic alignment.

### [76] [LLM-AutoSciLab: Closed-Loop Scientific Discovery via Active Experimentation with LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24043v1)

Result: 在NewtonBench、ActiveSciBench-Chem和ActiveSciBench-GRN上，符号准确性分别达67.6%和35.1%，精确图恢复达31.1%，样本效率比最强基线高2-5倍。

Conclusion: 假设指导的实验策略显著提升了样本效率和发现性能，证明了闭环主动学习在科学发现中的有效性。

中文摘要：科学发现是一个闭环过程，其中假设指导数据采集，而观察则精炼假设空间。然而，大多数方法将发现简化为在固定数据集上的监督学习，其中有限的观测可能支持多种合理的机制，这些机制在局部拟合良好但无法泛化。因此，关键挑战在于选择信息丰富的观测以解决不确定性，从而将焦点从静态推断转向自适应数据采集。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了LLM-AutoSciLab，一个将假设生成与假设条件实验选择和机制精炼耦合的闭环框架。LLM-AutoSciLab不是将模型拟合到被动收集的数据上，而是迭代地提出合理的假设，选择信息丰富的实验以区分或精炼这些假设，并利用产生的证据更新其状态。为了评估具有主动数据采集的动态闭环科学发现，我们引入了ActiveSciBench，它包含两个数据集：包含57个酶动力学任务的ActiveSciBench-Chem和包含45个基因调控网络任务的ActiveSciBench-GRN。这些数据集将发现建模为一个受预算约束的过程，需要自适应实验设计、变量选择和真实机制的恢复。在NewtonBench、ActiveSciBench-Chem和ActiveSciBench-GRN上，LLM-AutoSciBench优于先前的方法，在NewtonBench和ActiveSciBench-Chem上分别实现了67.6%和35.1%的符号准确性，在ActiveSciBench-GRN上实现了31.1%的精确图恢复。此外，假设指导的实验比最强的竞争基线样本效率高2-5倍。代码和数据可在https://github.com/scientific-discovery/LLM-AutoSciLab获取。

Original abstract: Scientific discovery is a closed-loop process in which hypotheses guide data acquisition and observations refine the hypothesis space. Yet most approaches reduce discovery to supervised learning over fixed datasets, where limited observations can support multiple plausible mechanisms that fit locally but fail to generalize. Thus, the key challenge is selecting informative observations to resolve uncertainty, shifting the focus from static inference to adaptive data acquisition. To address this, we propose LLM-AutoSciLab, a closed-loop framework that couples hypothesis generation with hypothesis-conditioned experiment selection and mechanism refinement. Rather than fitting models to passively collected data, LLM-AutoSciLab iteratively proposes plausible hypotheses, selects informative experiments to distinguish or refine them, and updates its state using the resulting evidence. To evaluate dynamic, closed-loop scientific discovery with active data acquisition, we introduce ActiveSciBench, comprising two datasets: ActiveSciBench-Chem with 57 enzyme-kinetics tasks and ActiveSciBench-GRN with 45 gene-regulatory-network tasks. These datasets model discovery as a budget-constrained process requiring adaptive experiment design, variable selection, and recovery of true mechanisms. Across NewtonBench, ActiveSciBench-Chem, and ActiveSciBench-GRN, LLM-AutoSciLab outperforms prior methods, achieving 67.6% and 35.1% symbolic accuracy on NewtonBench and ActiveSciBench-Chem, respectively, and 31.1% exact graph recovery on ActiveSciBench-GRN. Moreover, hypothesis-guided experimentation is 2-5x more sample-efficient than the strongest competing baselines. Code and data are available at: https://github.com/scientific-discovery/LLM-AutoSciLab

</details>


### [77] [Mixture of Complementary Agents for Robust LLM Ensemble](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.24048v1)
*Yichi Zhang,Kevin Lu,Yuang Zhang,Jie Gao,Lirong Xia,Fang-Yi Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出互补agent选择方法用于LLM集成，属于多agent协作的通用方法，可迁移至coding agent组合。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于互补性的组合选择方法，使用贪心算法从小规模标注集中评估提议者互补性，以选择LLM进行多AI协作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有提议者选择方法只关注准确性或多样性，忽略了提议者之间以及与摘要者之间的交互，且直接应用特征选择算法在LLM中计算不可行。

Method: 将提议者选择重新定义为类似特征选择的组合选择问题，并探索一系列计算可行的贪心风格算法，利用小规模标注集评估互补性。

Result: 实验验证了互补性是有效的提议者选择指导原则，并确定了在性能-成本权衡上最优的方法。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种实用且有效的提议者选择方法，在LLM协作中平衡了性能与计算成本。

中文摘要：多AI协作，例如对大语言模型（LLM）进行集成或辩论，是一种聚合信息并提升性能的有前景的范式。这些流程的基础步骤是将多个提议者LLM的响应输入到摘要者LLM中，后者综合出更好的答案。然而，选择哪些提议者加入并非易事。现有方法主要关注准确性（选择最强的模型）或多样性（确保多样性），往往忽视了提议者之间以及与摘要者之间的交互。我们将提议者选择重新定义为类似于特征选择的组合选择问题，其中LLM的价值在于其与其他模型的互补性。然而，由于时间复杂度过高，直接应用标准的特征选择算法在LLM设置中不切实际。受此限制，我们探索了一系列计算可行的、贪心风格的选择算法，这些算法使用小规模标注集评估互补性。我们的实验验证了互补性作为提议者选择指导原则的有效性，并确定了在实践中实现最佳性能-成本权衡的方法。

Original abstract: Multi-AI collaboration, such as ensembling or debating large language models (LLMs), is a promising paradigm for aggregating information and boosting performance. A foundational step in these pipelines is to feed the responses of several proposer LLMs into a summarizer LLM, which synthesizes a better answer. However, choosing which proposers to include is non-trivial. Existing approaches primarily focus either on accuracy (picking the strongest models) or diversity (ensuring variety), and often overlook the interactions among proposers and with the summarizer. We reframe proposer selection as a combinatorial selection problem akin to feature selection, where the value of an LLM lies in its complementarity with others. However, directly applying standard feature-selection algorithms is impractical in the LLM setting due to prohibitive time complexity. Motivated by this limitation, we explore an extensive range of computationally feasible, greedy-style selection algorithms that assess complementarity using a small labeled set. Our experiments validate complementarity as a guiding principle for proposer selection and identify methods that achieve the best performance-cost trade-offs in practice.

</details>


### [78] [Decomposing and Measuring Evaluation Awareness](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23055v2)
*Changling Li,Terry Jingchen Zhang,Jie Zhang,Zhijing Jin,Sahar Abdelnabi,Maksym Andriushchenko*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究LLM评估意识检测与行为影响，属于agent可靠性与安全控制，可指导coding agent行为一致性。

TL;DR: 本文通过分解评估意识为环境与模型组件，提出EvalAwareBench基准，发现识别率取决于模型与基准的配对，且识别很少导致行为改变，但安全评估更敏感，叠加因素能提高评估意识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏共同基础，混淆了评估属性与模型属性以及检测与行为响应，无法有效衡量和缓解语言模型在评估中的行为调整问题。

Method: 基于社会心理学分解评估意识为环境组件（八个触发因素）和模型组件；通过思维链监控测量识别与行为；构建EvalAwareBench基准，独立控制八个因素，评估模型行为。

Result: 识别率取决于模型与基准的配对而非单独因素；识别很少导致行为改变，方向依赖评估类型；模型对安全评估更敏感；无单一因素统一影响所有模型，但叠加因素逐步提升评估意识。

Conclusion: 框架和EvalAwareBench可测量和缓解评估意识，未来应追求识别下行为一致性。

中文摘要：前沿语言模型有时会意识到自己正在被评估，并调整其行为，从而削弱了基准测试结果的有效性。然而，该领域的研究缺乏共同基础，混淆了评估属性与模型属性，以及检测与行为响应。我们将评估意识植根于社会心理学，将其分解为环境组件（任务的可识别程度）和模型组件，后者将识别与采取行动的倾向分开。我们通过八个分类的触发因素（例如占位符实体和评分式输出格式）来操作化环境组件，并通过思维链监控来研究识别和行为。在九个前沿模型和四个基准测试中，识别率取决于模型和基准测试的具体配对，而非单独取决于其中任何一个。识别很少导致行为改变，即使发生改变，方向也取决于所感知的评估类型。模型对安全性评估比能力评估更敏感，这使得安全性基准的有效性面临更大风险。为了研究每个模型对哪些因素敏感以及它们如何相互作用，我们提出了\textbf{EvalAwareBench}，这是一个因素控制的基准测试，包含100个配对的安全-能力任务，其中八个因素中的每一个都可以独立切换，在保持底层请求不变的情况下改变评估信号。通过EvalAwareBench，我们发现没有单一因素能统一影响所有模型，但叠加因素会逐渐提高所有模型的评估意识。我们的框架和EvalAwareBench提供了测量、归因和缓解评估意识的工具，指出在识别下保持行为一致性是一条有希望的前进道路。

Original abstract: Frontier language models sometimes recognize that they are being evaluated and adjust their behavior, undermining validity of benchmark results. Yet the field studies it without a shared foundation, conflating properties of the evaluation with properties of the model, and detection with behavioral response. We ground evaluation awareness in social psychology, decomposing it into an environment component (how recognizable the task is) and a model component that separates recognition from propensity to act on it. We operationalize the environment component through eight categorized trigger factors, such as placeholder entities and grading-style output formats, and study recognition and behavior through chain-of-thought monitoring. Across nine frontier models and four benchmarks, recognition rates depend on the specific pairing of model and benchmark rather than on either in isolation. Recognition rarely leads to behavioral change, and when it does, the direction depends on the type of evaluation perceived. Models are also more sensitive to safety than capability evaluations, placing safety benchmark validity at greater risk. To study which factors each model is sensitive to and how they interact, we propose \textbf{EvalAwareBench}, a factor-controlled benchmark of 100 paired safety-capability tasks where each of the eight factors can be independently toggled, varying evaluative signals while holding the underlying request fixed. Through EvalAwareBench, we find that no single factor uniformly affects all models, but stacking factors progressively raises evaluation awareness across all of them. Our framework and EvalAwareBench provide the tools to measure, attribute, and mitigate evaluation awareness, pointing to behavioral consistency under recognition as a promising path forward.

</details>


### [79] [Self-Play Reinforcement Learning under Imperfect Information in Big 2](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28863v2)
*Aalok Patwa*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 自我对弈RL在不完美信息游戏中的对比研究，属于通用agent方法，可启发训练与规划设计。

TL;DR: Big 2游戏上PPO优于其他RL算法，熵正则化和当前策略自对弈有显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不完美信息多玩家游戏中的挑战，并选择Big 2作为测试平台。

Method: 开发自对弈RL框架，比较PPO、MCQ、SARSA、Q-learning，并测试熵正则化和不同自对弈策略。

Result: PPO优于其他方法；中等熵正则化提升PPO；当前策略自对弈优于检查点自对弈和固定对手训练。

Conclusion: Big 2是研究不完美信息、多玩家、延迟奖励和可变动作集深度RL的有效控制环境。

中文摘要：不完美信息多玩家游戏测试智能体是否能在隐藏信息、稀疏奖励和非平稳对手下行动。我们在Big 2（一个四人不完美信息纸牌游戏）中研究这些挑战。我们为Big 2开发了一个自对弈强化学习框架，能够对策略梯度智能体和值近似智能体进行受控比较。在共同的环境、输入表示、训练预算和评估协议下，PPO在对抗随机、贪婪和启发式Big 2对手时优于蒙特卡洛Q近似、SARSA和Q学习。我们进一步发现，适度的熵正则化通过防止策略变得过于确定性来改进PPO，并且当前策略自对弈比检查点自对弈或固定对手训练提供了更强的有限预算课程。这些结果共同表明，Big 2是研究不完美信息、多玩家交互、延迟奖励和可变动作集下深度强化学习的一个有用的受控环境。

Original abstract: Imperfect-information multiplayer games test whether agents can act under hidden information, sparse rewards, and non-stationary opponents. We study these challenges in Big 2, a four-player imperfect-information card game. We develop a self-play RL framework for Big 2 that enables controlled comparisons between policy-gradient and value-approximating agents. Under a common environment, input representation, training budget, and evaluation protocol, PPO outperforms Monte Carlo Q approximation, SARSA, and Q-learning against random, greedy, and heuristic Big 2 opponents. We further find that moderate entropy regularization improves PPO by preventing the policy from becoming overly deterministic, and that current-policy self-play provides a stronger finite-budget curriculum than checkpoint self-play or fixed-opponent training. Together, these results show that Big 2 is a useful controlled setting for studying deep RL under imperfect information, multiplayer interaction, delayed rewards, and variable action sets.

</details>

### [80] [ACC: Compiling Agent Trajectories for Long-Context Training](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21850v2)
*Qisheng Su,Zhen Fang,Shiting Huang,Yu Zeng,Yiming Zhao,Kou Shi,Ziao Zhang,Lin Chen,Zehui Chen,Lijun Wu,Feng Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出将agent轨迹编译为长上下文训练数据，对训练long-context agent有启发。

TL;DR: 提出Agent Context Compilation (ACC)方法，将智能体轨迹转换为长上下文QA对，训练LLM直接回答，提升长上下文推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准智能体SFT存在监督盲点，仅训练工具选择，未利用轨迹中分散的远距离证据。

Method: 将智能体轨迹（搜索、软件工程、数据库查询）转换为长上下文QA对，结合原始问题和多轮工具响应及观察，训练模型直接回答。

Result: 在MRCR和GraphWalks上分别提升18.1和7.6，达到68.3和77.5，与Qwen3-235B-A22B相当，且保持通用能力。

Conclusion: ACC是一种简单有效的长上下文训练数据生成方法，且模型展现出注意力重构和专家专业化。

中文摘要：最近智能体的发展重新引发了对LLM长上下文推理能力的需求。然而，训练LLM这种能力需要昂贵的长文档整理或启发式上下文合成。我们观察到，智能体在解决问题时会产生大量轨迹，在多个轮次中调用工具并接收环境观察结果。回答原始问题所需的证据因此分散在这些轮次中，需要整合远距离的上下文片段。然而，标准的智能体SFT会掩盖工具响应，仅训练轮次级别的工具选择，造成监督盲点，这些分散的信号未被利用。我们提出智能体上下文编译（Agent Context Compilation, ACC），它将来自搜索、软件工程和数据库查询智能体的轨迹转换为长上下文问答对，将原始问题与跨多个轮次收集的工具响应和环境观察结果相结合，训练模型直接回答而不使用工具。这使得问题与证据之间的依赖关系明确，无需额外注释即可对远距离片段的长上下文推理进行直接监督。ACC是一种简单有效的方法，可以与任何现有的长上下文扩展或训练方法结合，提供可扩展的有监督微调数据。我们通过MRCR和GraphWalks任务验证了ACC对长距离依赖建模的能力，这些是具有挑战性的基准，需要跨轮次共指解析和扩展上下文中的图遍历。使用ACC训练Qwen3-30B-A3B在MRCR上达到68.3（+18.1），在GraphWalks上达到77.5（+7.6），结果与Qwen3-235B-A22B相当，同时在GPQA、MMLU-Pro、AIME和IFEval上保持了通用能力。进一步的机制分析表明，ACC训练的模型展现出任务自适应注意力重构和专家专业化。

Original abstract: Recent development of agents has renewed demand for long-context reasoning capacity of LLMs. However, training LLMs for this capacity requires costly long-document curation or heuristic context synthesis. We observe that agents produce massive trajectories when solving problems, invoking tools and receiving environment observations across many turns. The evidence needed to answer the original question is thus scattered throughout these turns, requiring integration of distant context segments. Nevertheless, standard agent SFT masks tool responses and only trains turn-level tool selection, creating a supervision blind spot where these scattered signals go unused. We propose Agent Context Compilation (ACC), which converts trajectories from search, software engineering, and database querying agents into long-context QA pairs that combine the original question with tool responses and environment observations gathered across multiple turns, training the model to answer directly without tool use. This makes the dependencies between the question and the evidence explicit, enabling direct supervision of long-context reasoning over distant segments without additional annotation. ACC is a simple but effective approach that can be combined with any existing long-context extension or training method, providing scalable supervised fine-tuning data. We validate ACC on long-range dependency modeling tasks through MRCR and GraphWalks, challenging benchmarks requiring cross-turn coreference resolution and graph traversal over extended contexts. Training Qwen3-30B-A3B with ACC achieves 68.3 on MRCR (+18.1) and 77.5 on GraphWalks (+7.6), results comparable to Qwen3-235B-A22B, while preserving general capabilities on GPQA, MMLU-Pro, AIME, and IFEval. Further mechanism analysis reveals that the ACC-trained model exhibits task-adaptive attention restructuring and expert specialization.

</details>


### [81] [DeferMem: Query-Time Evidence Distillation via Reinforcement Learning for Long-Term Memory QA](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22411v1)
*Jianing Yin,Tan Tang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出DeferMem记忆框架，含RL蒸馏、检索与重写，可迁移至agent长期记忆

TL;DR: DeferMem提出了一种将长期记忆问答解耦为高召回率候选检索和查询条件化证据蒸馏的框架，通过DistillPO强化学习算法训练记忆蒸馏器，在多个基准上取得了最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长期记忆系统在检索时仅基于相似性而非实用性，导致大量噪声和查询无关信息，使得下游答案生成器难以有效利用。因此需要一种能够根据查询动态蒸馏相关信息的方法。

Method: DeferMem框架包含两个阶段：首先使用轻量级段链接结构在查询时进行高召回率候选检索，然后使用基于DistillPO强化学习算法训练的记忆蒸馏器，将噪声候选蒸馏为忠实、自包含且查询条件化的证据。DistillPO将蒸馏过程形式化为消息选择和证据重写，采用分解并门控的奖励和结构对齐的优势分配。

Result: 在LoCoMo和LongMemEval-S基准上，DeferMem在问答准确性和系统效率上超越了强基线，取得了最高的准确率、最快的运行时间，且无需商业API令牌费用。

Conclusion: DeferMem通过解耦和高召回检索与条件化证据蒸馏，有效解决了长期记忆问答中证据分散和噪声问题，显著提升了性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在长期记忆问答中仍然面临挑战，其中支持答案的证据通常分散在较长的对话历史中，并被大量无关内容所掩盖。现有的记忆系统通常在未来的查询未知之前就处理记忆，然后根据相似性而不是根据它们对回答查询的实用性来检索生成的单元。这种工作流程使得下游的答案生成器需要对检索到的候选信息进行去噪并重建特定于查询的证据。我们提出了DeferMem，一个长期记忆框架，将这个问题解耦为高召回率候选检索和查询条件化的证据蒸馏。DeferMem使用轻量级的段链接结构来组织原始历史，并在查询时检索广泛的候选信息。然后，它应用一个记忆蒸馏器，该蒸馏器使用DistillPO训练，DistillPO是我们的强化学习算法，用于将高召回率但高度噪声的候选信息蒸馏为一组忠实、自包含且查询条件化的证据。DistillPO将检索后的证据蒸馏形式化为一个结构化的动作，包括消息选择和证据重写。它通过分解并门控的奖励管道和结构对齐的优势分配来优化这个动作，从有效性到质量检查对奖励组件进行门控，同时早期暴露任务级别的正确性反馈，并将每个奖励分配给其负责的输出片段。在LoCoMo和LongMemEval-S上，DeferMem在问答准确性和记忆系统效率方面超越了强基线，实现了最高的问答准确率，最快的运行时间，以及记忆操作的零商业API令牌成本。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents still struggle with long-term memory question answering, where answer-supporting evidence is often scattered across long conversational histories and buried in substantial irrelevant content. Existing memory systems typically process memory before future queries are known, then retrieve the resulting units based on similarity rather than their utility for answering the query. This workflow leaves downstream answerers to denoise retrieved candidates and reconstruct query-specific evidence. We present DeferMem, a long-term memory framework that decouples this problem into high-recall candidate retrieval and query-conditioned evidence distillation. DeferMem uses a lightweight segment-link structure to organize raw history and retrieve broad candidates at query time. It then applies a memory distiller trained with DistillPO, our reinforcement learning algorithm for distilling the high-recall but highly noisy candidates into a set of faithful, self-contained, and query-conditioned evidence. DistillPO formulates post-retrieval evidence distillation as a structured action comprising message selection and evidence rewriting. It optimizes this action with a decomposed-and-gated reward pipeline and structure-aligned advantage assignment, gating reward components from validity to quality checks while exposing task-level correctness feedback early and assigning each reward to its responsible output span. On LoCoMo and LongMemEval-S, DeferMem surpasses strong baselines in QA accuracy and memory-system efficiency, achieving the highest QA accuracy with the fastest runtime and zero commercial-API token cost for memory operations.

</details>


### [82] [From Correlation to Cause: A Five-Stage Methodology for Feature Analysis in Transformer Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22462v1)
*Caleb Munigety*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 因果特征分析方法论，可应用于agent内部解读，但非直接agent方法

TL;DR: 提出五阶段因果特征分析方法，在GPT-2 small的IOI任务上验证发现特征部分因果，且检测鲁棒性与因果鲁棒性存在差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了系统性地分析Transformer语言模型中的因果特征，弥补单一分析方法无法全面评估的不足。

Method: 五阶段方法论：探针设计、特征提取（激活修补和稀疏自编码器）、因果验证、鲁棒性测试（分布偏移）和部署集成（成本评估）。

Result: 特征仅部分因果（消融15个特征后98%准确率）；选择性特征解释方差小（31% vs 99.7%）；选择性比率与因果力负相关（r=-0.56）；电路迁移干净但特征消融效果下降；最优监控配置节省99.1%成本；最优组合策略依赖成本比率和基准率。

Conclusion: 单一阶段无法全面揭示因果特征性质，多阶段联合分析才能获得完整发现。

中文摘要：我们提出了一种用于Transformer语言模型中因果特征分析的五阶段方法论（探针设计、特征提取、因果验证、鲁棒性测试和部署集成），并在执行间接宾语识别（IOI）任务的GPT-2 small上进行了端到端演示。激活修补恢复了典型的IOI电路（第9层第9个头单独恢复+1.02）。稀疏自编码器恢复了每个名称的选择性特征，效应大小为30到50个激活单元。因果验证发现这些特征是具体但仅部分因果的：消融其中十五个特征后，模型在98%的提示上仍然准确。两个受NLA启发的评估强化了这一图像：这十五个选择性特征仅解释了31%的激活方差，而SAE解释了99.7%，并且选择性比率与因果力呈负相关（r = -0.56）。在三种分布偏移下的鲁棒性测试发现，电路可以干净地迁移，但特征消融效果大幅下降，揭示了检测鲁棒性和因果鲁棒性之间的差距。基于成本的部署评估（假设假阴性成本50美元，假阳性成本0.42美元，2%的错误率）发现最佳监控配置每1000次查询成本为8.96美元，而基线为1000美元，节省了99.1%。最优组合策略随成本比率和基准率变化。各阶段的结合产生了任何单一阶段都无法得到的发现。

Original abstract: We propose a five-stage methodology for causal feature analysis in transformer language models (probe design, feature extraction, causal validation, robustness testing, and deployment integration) and demonstrate it end-to-end on GPT-2 small performing the Indirect Object Identification (IOI) task. Activation patching recovers the canonical IOI circuit (layer-9 head 9 alone gives recovery +1.02). A sparse autoencoder recovers per-name selective features with effect sizes of 30 to 50 activation units. Causal validation finds these features specifically but only partially causal: ablating fifteen of them leaves the model accurate on 98% of prompts. Two NLA-inspired evaluations strengthen this picture: the fifteen selective features explain only 31% of activation variance versus the SAE's 99.7%, and selectivity ratio anticorrelates with causal force (r = -0.56). Robustness testing under three distribution shifts finds that the circuit transfers cleanly but feature ablation effects degrade substantially, exposing a gap between detection robustness and causal robustness. A cost-based deployment evaluation (assumed $50/FN, $0.42/FP, 2% error rate) finds an optimal monitor configuration yielding $8.96 per 1000 queries against a $1000 baseline, a 99.1% saving. Optimal composition strategy varies with cost ratio and base rate. The conjunction of stages produces findings no single stage would.

### [83] [SynAE: A Framework for Measuring the Quality of Synthetic Data for Tool-Calling Agent Evaluations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22564v1)
*Shuaiqi Wang,Aadyaa Maddi,Zinan Lin,Giulia Fanti*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了SynAE框架，用于评估合成数据在工具调用智能体测试中的质量，从有效性、保真度和多样性多维度评估，表明单一指标不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 内部生产数据集往往敏感、稀疏或不可用，需要合成数据，但缺乏量化合成数据与真实数据关系的方法。

Method: 提出SynAE评估框架，包含四个指标类别（任务指令与中间响应、工具调用、最终输出、下游评估），并设计受控生成方案测试常见失效模式。

Result: SynAE能检测数据有效性、保真度和多样性的细微变化，且单一指标无法完全表征合成数据质量。

Conclusion: 需要多轴评估合成数据质量，SynAE为此提供了有效工具。

中文摘要：如今，工具调用智能体通常在包含输入命令、智能体响应及相关工具调用的执行轨迹静态数据集上进行评估或测试。然而，内部生产数据集往往不足以测试或无法使用；例如，它们可能包含敏感或专有数据，或者过于稀疏以至于无法支持全面测试（尤其是在部署前）。在这些情况下，从业者越来越多地使用合成数据集来替代或增强真实数据集以用于评估。一个关键挑战是量化这些合成数据集与真实数据之间的关系。我们提出SynAE，一个用于评估多轮工具调用智能体的合成基准如何复制和增强真实数据轨迹特征的评估框架。SynAE从四个指标类别评估合成数据的有效性、保真度和多样性：(i) 任务指令与中间响应，(ii) 工具调用，(iii) 最终输出，以及 (iv) 下游评估。我们使用最近的智能体基准测试SynAE，并通过现实且受控的生成方案测试常见的合成数据失效模式。SynAE检测到数据有效性、保真度和多样性的细微变化，并表明没有单一指标足以完全表征合成数据质量，从而激励在智能体测试中对合成数据进行多轴评估。SynAE的演示可在https://synae-2026-synae-demo.static.hf.space/index.html获取，代码在https://github.com/wsqwsq/SynAE。

Original abstract: Today, tool-calling agents are commonly evaluated or tested on static datasets of execution traces, including input commands, agent responses, and associated tool calls. However, internal production datasets are often insufficient or unusable for testing; for example, they may contain sensitive or proprietary data, or they may be too sparse to support comprehensive testing (especially pre-deployment). In these settings, practitioners are increasingly replacing or augmenting real datasets with synthetic ones for evaluation purposes. A key challenge is quantifying the relation between these synthetic datasets and the real data. We introduce SynAE, an evaluation framework for assessing how well synthetic benchmarks for multi-turn, tool-calling agents replicate and augment the characteristics of real data trajectories. SynAE assesses the validity, fidelity, and diversity of synthetic data across four metric categories: (i) task instructions and intermediate responses, (ii) tool calls, (iii) final outputs, and (iv) downstream evaluation. We evaluate SynAE using recent agent benchmarks and test common synthetic data failure modes via realistic and controlled generation schemes. SynAE detects fine-grained variations in data validity, fidelity and diversity, and shows that no single metric is sufficient to fully characterize synthetic data quality, motivating a multi-axis evaluation of synthetic data for agent testing. A demo of SynAE is available at https://synae-2026-synae-demo.static.hf.space/index.html, with code at https://github.com/wsqwsq/SynAE.

</details>


### [84] [Agentic CLEAR: Automating Multi-Level Evaluation of LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22608v1)
*Asaf Yehudai,Lilach Eden,Michal Shmueli-Scheuer*

Result: 在四个基准、七个代理设置和数万次LLM调用中，反馈质量高，与人工标注错误高度一致，并能预测任务成功率。

Original abstract: Agentic systems are becoming more capable: agents define strategies, take actions, and interact with different environments. This autonomy poses serious challenges for overseeing and assessing agent behavior. Most current tools are limited, focusing on observability with basic evaluation capabilities or imposing static, hand-crafted error taxonomies that cannot adapt to new domains. To address this gap, we present Agentic CLEAR, an automatic, dynamic, and easy-to-use evaluation framework. It produces textual insights into the agent behavior on three levels of granularity: system, trace, and node. Agentic CLEAR operates above the observability layer, enabling seamless integration and featuring an intuitive UI that makes agent evaluation highly accessible. In our experiments on four benchmarks, seven agentic settings, and tens of thousands of LLM calls, we show that Agentic CLEAR produces high-quality, data-driven, insightful feedback. Our analysis shows strong alignment with human-annotated errors and the ability to predict task success rate.

### [85] [Graph Alignment Topology as an Inductive Bias for Grounding Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22963v1)
*Paul Landes,Pranav Herur,Adam Cross,Jimeng Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 图对齐拓扑检测幻觉，对agent可靠性验证有潜在启发

TL;DR: 利用对齐拓扑作为归纳偏差，通过构建二部图并训练GNN进行消息传递，在幻觉检测和问答任务上取得SOTA，超越GPT-4o。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成内容常与参考不一致，现有检测方法未直接利用对齐拓扑，限制了在事实关键领域的应用。

Method: 构建参考信息与LLM输出之间的对齐二部图，训练GNN通过消息传递建模对齐结构。

Result: 在四个数据集上达到SOTA，优于所有基线方法，包括GPT-4o。

Conclusion: 对齐拓扑可作为有效归纳偏差提升事实性检测性能。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）被优化以产生分布上合理的延续，而不是显式验证生成的命题是否被源文档蕴含。这种归纳偏差使得泛化成为可能，但它并未编码回应是否与参考信息一致。这些问题限制了LLMs在需要严格事实正确性的领域（如临床决策支持）中的应用。现有的幻觉检测方法通过检索增强、自一致性或主张验证来提高事实性，但通常不直接学习对齐拓扑。为了利用对齐拓扑作为归纳偏差，我们在参考信息和LLM输出之间构建对齐的二部图，并训练一个图神经网络（GNN）通过消息传递来建模对齐结构。该方法在四个不同的幻觉和问答数据集上取得了最先进的结果，优于所有比较的方法，包括基础LLMs如GPT-4o。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are optimized to produce distributionally plausible continuations rather than to explicitly verify whether generated propositions are entailed by source documents. This inductive bias enables generalization, but it does not encode whether responses are grounded with respect to a reference. These issues limit the use of LLMs in domains where strict factual correctness is crucial, such as clinical decision support. Existing hallucination detection approaches improve factuality through retrieval augmentation, self-consistency, or claim verification, but generally do not learn directly over alignment topology. To leverage alignment topology as an inductive bias, we construct aligned bipartite graphs between reference information and LLM outputs and train a graph neural network (GNN) to model alignment structure using message passing. The method achieves state-of-the-art results on four diverse hallucination and question-answering datasets, outperforming all compared methods, including foundational LLMs such as GPT-4o.

### [86] [A Proactive Multi-Agent Dialogue Framework for Assessing Social Language Disorder Traits in Autism](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22993v1)
*Chuanbo Hu,Minglei Yin,Bin Liu,Wenqi Li,Lynn K. Paul,Shuo Wang,Xin Li*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent对话规划框架，通用方法可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 提出TPA框架，通过主动选择提问策略显著提升自闭症SLD特征评估效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前临床评估中提问策略选择未被充分利用，且LLM能否主动引导提问策略以揭示潜在SLD特征尚不清楚。

Method: 提出了多代理对话框架TPA，包含医生代理和基于真实数据的患者代理，通过思考、计划、提问的流程选择临床策略并生成问题。

Result: 在35名患者的484个片段上，TPA实现82.1%特征覆盖率，比临床医生重放高16.6%，AUCC从0.458提升到0.628。

Conclusion: 主动提问策略选择能显著提高SLD评估效率，对AI辅助临床筛查有直接意义。

中文摘要：与自闭症谱系障碍的社会语言障碍（SLD）相关的特征性语言行为，包括回声性重复、代词错位和刻板的媒体引用，在自发的对话中基本不存在，只有在特定的对话条件下才会出现。在结构化的临床评估中，这种延迟意味着提问策略的选择是一个关键但未被充分重视的决定因素，它决定了对话能产生多少诊断信息。大型语言模型（LLMs）是否可以被引导主动选择提问策略，以系统地揭示这些潜在特征，这在很大程度上仍未得到探索。在这里，我们提出了TPA（思考、计划、提问），一个主动的多代理对话框架，应用于自闭症诊断观察量表模块4（ADOS-2）的语言评估部分，其中医生代理在生成有针对性的问题之前，明确推理哪些特征尚未观察到，然后选择临床基础的策略。一个基于真实ADOS-2临床数据的患者代理能够在没有真实患者参与的情况下进行可重复的评估，并通过三个独立实验验证，确认了对真实患者语言足够的保真度。在来自35名患者的484个片段上进行评估，TPA在所有主要指标上优于六个竞争性的对话规划基线，实现了82.1%的SLD特征覆盖率，比训练有素的临床医生进行的真实临床对话的自动重放（65.5%）高出16.6%，并且每轮诊断效率显著提高（AUCC：0.628 vs. 0.458，绝对增益+0.170）。这些结果表明，主动提问策略选择显著提高了自动化SLD特征评估的效率，对可扩展的AI辅助临床筛查具有直接意义。

Original abstract: Characteristic linguistic behaviors associated with Social Language Disorder (SLD) in autism spectrum disorder, including echoic repetition, pronoun displacement, and stereotyped media quoting, are largely absent from spontaneous conversation and only emerge under specific conversational conditions. In structured clinical assessments, this latency means that questioning strategy selection is a critical yet underappreciated determinant of how much diagnostic information a conversation yields. Whether large language models (LLMs) can be guided to proactively select questioning strategies that systematically surface these latent traits remains largely unexplored. Here we present TPA (Think, Plan, Ask), a proactive multi-agent dialogue framework applied to the language assessment component of the Autism Diagnostic Observation Schedule Module 4 (ADOS-2), in which a doctor agent explicitly reasons about which traits remain unobserved before selecting a clinically grounded strategy and generating a targeted question. A patient agent grounded in real ADOS-2 clinical data enables reproducible evaluation without real patient participation, validated across three independent experiments confirming adequate fidelity to real patient language. Evaluated on 484 episodes from 35 patients, TPA outperforms six competitive dialogue planning baselines across all primary metrics, achieving 82.1% SLD trait coverage, 16.6% higher than automated replay of real clinical dialogues conducted by trained clinicians (65.5%), with substantially greater per-turn diagnostic efficiency (AUCC: 0.628 vs. 0.458, absolute gain +0.170). These results demonstrate that proactive questioning strategy selection substantially improves the efficiency of automated SLD trait assessment, with direct implications for scalable AI-assisted clinical screening.

### [87] [Incentive-Aligned Vehicle-to-Vehicle Energy Trading via Nash-Integrated Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22363v1)
*Yujin Lin,Yue Yang,Hao Wang*

Main category: math.OC

Selection reason: 基于纳什协商的多智能体强化学习，提出可迁移的多agent协作方法

TL;DR: 提出Nash-MADDPG方法，通过纳什谈判实现V2V能量交易的激励对齐，显著提升社会福利、交易量和公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有V2V能量交易方法依赖集中优化或缺乏公平性，无法有效协调自私的EV代理。

Method: 将纳什谈判解集成到MADDPG中，通过纳什引导的价格接近奖励对齐代理策略。

Result: 在30天仿真中，社会福利提升61.6%，交易量提升62.9%，Jain公平指数提升40.1%，并在6-100代理规模下保持稳定。

Conclusion: Nash-MADDPG实现了高效、公平且可扩展的V2V能量交易。

中文摘要：车辆到车辆（V2V）能量交易使得电动汽车（EVs）之间能够进行去中心化的点对点能量交换，减少对电网的依赖，同时将剩余容量货币化。然而，协调具有不同充电需求和不确定到达-离开时间表的自私EV代理仍然具有挑战性。现有方法要么需要具有计算局限性的集中优化，要么缺乏公平性保证。本文将纳什谈判解集成到多智能体深度确定性策略梯度中，即Nash-MADDPG，用于激励一致的V2V能量交易。纳什谈判确定高效的双边定价，而纳什引导的价格接近奖励将智能体学习导向谈判最优策略。在连续30天运行中的评估显示，与双拍卖相比，社会福利提高了61.6%，交易量提高了62.9%，同时实现了优越的公平性，例如Jain指数提高了40.1%。在6-100个智能体和连续30天的时间范围内进行测试，确认了跨人口规模的可扩展性以及经验上接近纳什谈判基准的稳定定价。

Original abstract: Vehicle-to-vehicle (V2V) energy trading enables decentralized peer-to-peer energy exchange among electric vehicles (EVs), reducing grid dependency while monetizing surplus capacity. However, coordinating self-interested EV agents with diverse charging needs and uncertain arrival-departure schedules remains challenging. Existing approaches either require centralized optimization with computational limitations or lack fairness guarantees. This paper integrates Nash Bargaining Solution into Multi-Agent Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient, namely Nash-MADDPG, for incentive-aligned V2V energy trading. Nash bargaining determines efficient bilateral pricing, while Nash-guided price proximity rewards align agent learning toward bargaining-optimal strategies. Evaluation over 30-day continuous operation demonstrates an improvement of 61.6% in social welfare and 62.9% improvement in trading volume over Double Auction, while achieving superior fairness, such as 40.1% improvement in Jain's index. Testing across 6-100 agents over a 30-day horizon with continuous vehicle turnover confirms scalability across population size and empirically stable pricing near the Nash Bargaining benchmark.

### [88] [Sibyl-AutoResearch: Autonomous Research Needs Self-Evolving Trial-and-Error Harnesses, Not Paper Generators](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22343v1)
*Chengcheng Wang,Qinhua Xie,Wei He,Jianyuan Guo,Shiqi Wang,Chang Xu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Sibyl-AutoResearch框架，通过科学试错试验形式化两个转换单元，使自主研究系统能从试验中学习并改进，并在SIBYL系统中实现，审计显示高置信度转换事件和失败修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主研究系统虽然使工作流可执行，但缺乏研究判断能力，无法从试验经验中学习，导致弱证据被夸大、失败重复发生。

Method: 设计Sibyl-AutoResearch框架，核心是科学试错框架，包含两个可审计的转换单元：试验到行为转换和试验到框架行为转换，并在SIBYL系统中实现，通过回顾性审计和失败注册表验证。

Result: 回顾性审计发现8个高置信度转换事件，中位延迟1次迭代；失败注册表显示5类失败被有效处理；这些痕迹表明转换单元可在现实场景中恢复。

Conclusion: 所提出的转换单元是可行的，能从现实自主研究工作中恢复，但未建立比较性能优势，未来可用于改进自主研究系统的判断能力。

中文摘要：自主研究系统越来越使科学工作流可执行：代理可以提出想法、运行代码、检查结果和起草论文。但可执行的工作流本身并不产生研究判断。我们分析了当前系统在哪些方面丢失了试验经验：薄弱的证据变成散文，初步信号变成广泛声明，记忆仍然是文本性的，重复的过程失败不会改变后续行为。我们引入了Sibyl-AutoResearch，一种围绕科学试错框架构建的自我进化的AutoResearch框架。框架让代理运行有边界的试验，保留正面和负面结果，并将经验教训用于后续规划、验证、声明范围、调度、批评、写作和框架修复。我们通过两个可审计的转换单元对其进行形式化：试验到行为转换，将试验信号链接到后续研究行动；以及试验到框架行为转换，将重复的过程失败链接到系统更新。我们在SIBYL中实现了该框架，SIBYL是一个基于文件的自主研究系统，暴露了检查这些转换路径所需的状态、角色、记忆、门和工件痕迹。回顾性审计识别出八个高置信度的转换事件，中位延迟一次迭代，最大延迟三次迭代。一个恢复的失败注册表进一步显示了五种自然发生的失败类别（包括重复结果、过时的数字和不受支持的统计数据）如何被阻止、降级或路由到后续修复中。这些痕迹并不建立比较性能声明；它们表明所提出的转换单元可以从现实自主研究工作空间中恢复。SIBYL框架和系统可在https://github.com/Sibyl-Research-Team/AutoResearch-SibylSystem获取。

Original abstract: Autonomous research systems increasingly make the scientific workflow executable: agents can propose ideas, run code, inspect results, and draft papers. But executable workflows do not by themselves produce research judgment. We analyze where current systems lose trial experience: weak evidence becomes prose, pilot signals become broad claims, memory remains textual, and recurring process failures do not change later behavior. We introduce Sibyl-AutoResearch, a self-evolving AutoResearch framework built around Scientific Trial-and-Error Harnesses. A harness lets agents run bounded trials, preserve positive and negative outcomes, and route lessons into later planning, validation, claim scope, scheduling, critique, writing, and harness repair. We formalize this through two auditable conversion units: trial-to-behavior conversion, which links trial signals to later research actions, and trial-to-harness-behavior conversion, which links recurring process failures to system updates. We implement the framework in SIBYL, a file-backed autonomous research system that exposes the state, roles, memory, gates, and artifact traces needed to inspect these conversion paths. A retrospective audit identifies eight high-confidence conversion events, with a median latency of one iteration and a maximum latency of three iterations. A recovered-failure registry further shows how five naturally occurring failure classes, including duplicate results, stale numbers, and unsupported statistics, were blocked, downgraded, or routed into later repair. These traces do not establish a comparative performance claim; they show that the proposed conversion units are recoverable from realistic autonomous-research workspaces. The SIBYL framework and system are available at https://github.com/Sibyl-Research-Team/AutoResearch-SibylSystem.

</details>

### [89] [MadEvolve: Evolutionary Optimization of Trading Systems with Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23007v1)
*Yurii Kvasiuk,Tianyi Li,Owen Colegrove,Moritz Münchmeyer*

Main category: q-fin.TR

Selection reason: 进化优化交易系统，框架可迁移至自动代码优化

TL;DR: 本文展示了MadEvolve框架在比特币交易中优化特征、策略组件及联合进化上的显著效果，并与Claude Code对比，验证了AI驱动进化算法在量化金融中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLM驱动的算法优化在量化金融中的潜力，特别是用于优化算法交易策略和alpha生成。

Method: 使用MadEvolve框架，通过进化特征集、优化交易策略组件、联合进化特征管道和执行策略，并与Claude Code等代理搜索方法比较，同时评估p-hacking概率。

Result: 在模拟和回测中，所有任务（如信号生成、策略优化、联合进化）均获得显著改进。

Conclusion: AI驱动的代理和进化算法在算法交易和量化金融中具有强实用性。

中文摘要：我们探讨了将LLM驱动的算法优化应用于量化金融中几个常见任务的方法。MadEvolve是一个受DeepMind的Alpha-Evolve启发的通用算法优化框架，最近被开发用于优化计算宇宙学中的算法。这里我们展示了MadEvolve在以比特币交易为例的算法交易策略和alpha生成中的效用。在我们的模拟和回测设置中，我们在所有考虑的任务上都取得了显著改进，例如进化用于信号生成的特征集、优化交易策略的独立组件，以及联合进化特征管道与执行策略。此外，我们将我们的方法与其他代理搜索方法（特别是Claude Code）进行了比较，并仔细评估了我们模拟设置中的p-hacking概率。我们的发现强烈支持AI驱动的代理和进化算法在算法交易和量化金融中的效用。

Original abstract: We explore the application of LLM-driven algorithm optimization to several common tasks in quantitative finance. MadEvolve, a general-purpose algorithm optimization framework inspired by DeepMind's Alpha-Evolve, was recently developed to optimize algorithms in computational cosmology. Here we demonstrate the utility of MadEvolve to optimize algorithmic trading strategies and alpha generation at the example of Bitcoin trading. On our simulation and backtesting setup, we achieve significant improvements on all tasks we considered, such as evolving feature sets for signal generation, optimizing separate components of the trading strategy, and jointly evolving the feature pipeline together with the execution strategy. Additionally, we compare our method to other agentic search approaches, specifically Claude Code, and carefully evaluate p-hacking probabilities on our simulation setup. Our findings strongly support the utility of AI-driven agentic and evolutionary algorithms for algorithmic trading and quantitative finance.

### [90] [Blind Spots in the Guard: How Domain-Camouflaged Injection Attacks Evade Detection in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22001v1)
*Aaditya Pai*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究多agent系统注入攻击盲区，对agent安全设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文发现LLM注入检测器对领域伪装注入存在系统性盲点，检测率大幅下降，并形式化定义了伪装检测差距（CDG）。实验表明该盲点普遍存在，多智能体辩论架构会放大攻击，针对性的检测器增强仅能部分缓解，揭示了对弱模型而言该漏洞是架构性的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有注入检测器仅在静态模板上校准，无法识别模仿领域词汇和权威结构的伪装注入，导致严重安全风险。本文旨在揭示并量化这一盲点。

Method: 提出领域伪装注入概念，通过生成模仿目标文档词汇和权威结构的有效载荷，在多个模型和任务上测量检测率，并定义伪装检测差距（CDG）。评估多智能体辩论架构和检测器增强的效果。

Result: 标准检测器检测率从93.8%降至9.7%（Llama）和100%降至55.6%（Gemini）；CDG统计显著；Llama Guard 3检测率为0；多智能体辩论架构放大攻击9.9倍；检测器增强仅部分改善（10.2%和78.7%）。

Conclusion: 领域伪装注入暴露了LLM检测器的架构性漏洞，尤其在较弱模型上，当前检测机制亟需根本性改进。

中文摘要：为了保护LLM代理而部署的注入检测器是在静态、基于模板的有效载荷上校准的，这些有效载荷自我宣告为覆盖指令。我们发现了一个系统性的盲点：当有效载荷被生成以模仿目标文档的领域词汇和权威结构时（我们称为领域伪装注入），标准检测器无法标记它们，在Llama 3.1 8B上检测率从93.8%下降到9.7%，在Gemini 2.0 Flash上从100%下降到55.6%。我们将此形式化为伪装检测差距（CDG），即静态和伪装有效载荷之间的注入检测率差异。跨越三个领域和两个模型家族的45个任务中，CDG很大且统计显著（Llama: chi^2 = 38.03, p < 0.001; Gemini: chi^2 = 17.05, p < 0.001），两种情况下零反向不一致对。我们还评估了生产安全分类器Llama Guard 3，它检测到零个伪装有效载荷（IDR_camouflage = 0.000），证实盲点不仅限于少样本检测器，还扩展到专用安全分类器。我们进一步表明，多智能体辩论架构在较小模型上放大了静态注入攻击高达9.9倍，而较强模型表现出集体抵抗。有针对性的检测器增强仅提供部分补救（Llama上10.2%改进，Gemini上78.7%），表明对于较弱模型，该漏洞是架构性的而非偶然的。我们的框架、任务库和有效载荷生成器已公开发布。

Original abstract: Injection detectors deployed to protect LLM agents are calibrated on static, template-based payloads that announce themselves as override directives. We identify a systematic blind spot: when payloads are generated to mimic the domain vocabulary and authority structures of the target document, what we call domain camouflaged injection, standard detectors fail to flag them, with detection rates dropping from 93.8% to 9.7% on Llama 3.1 8B and from 100% to 55.6% on Gemini 2.0 Flash. We formalize this as the Camouflage Detection Gap (CDG), the difference in injection detection rate between static and camouflaged payloads. Across 45 tasks spanning three domains and two model families, CDG is large and statistically significant (chi^2 = 38.03, p < 0.001 for Llama; chi^2 = 17.05, p < 0.001 for Gemini), with zero reverse discordant pairs in either case. We additionally evaluate Llama Guard 3, a production safety classifier, which detects zero camouflage payloads (IDRcamouflage = 0.000), confirming that the blind spot extends beyond few-shot detectors to dedicated safety classifiers. We further show that multi-agent debate architectures amplify static injection attacks by up to 9.9x on smaller models, while stronger models show collective resistance. Targeted detector augmentation provides only partial remediation (10.2% improvement on Llama, 78.7% on Gemini), suggesting the vulnerability is architectural rather than incidental for weaker models. Our framework, task bank, and payload generator are released publicly.

</details>


### [91] [Benchmarking Autonomous Agents against Temporal, Spatial, and Semantic Evasions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22321v1)
*Jianan Ma,Xiaohu Du,Ruixiao Lin,Yaoxiang Bian,Jialuo Chen,Jingyi Wang,Xiaofang Yang,Shiwen Cui,Changhua Meng,Xinhao Deng,Zhen Wang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出针对LLM代理系统的多维规避框架，通过时间、空间和语义攻击向量将风险触发率从28.3%提升至52.6%，揭示系统性架构漏洞，现有防御失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前漏洞分析仅关注单轮无状态行为，忽略了有状态多轮交互和动态工具调用带来的扩大的攻击面。

Method: 提出包含时间、空间和语义隐蔽向量的多维规避框架，构建包含2,254条真实轨迹的A3S-Bench基准，评估10个主流LLM骨干在20个威胁场景下的表现。

Result: 风险触发率从28.3%基线提升至52.6%。

Conclusion: 自主代理系统存在架构级漏洞，现有防御措施无法应对，需开发针对性的防御机制。

中文摘要：随着自主代理（例如OpenClaw）越来越多地以深度系统级权限运行以执行复杂任务，它们引入了严重且未得到缓解的安全风险。当前的漏洞分析绝大多数集中于单轮、无状态的行为，忽视了有状态、多轮交互和动态工具调用中固有的攻击面。在本文中，我们提出了一种针对基于LLM的代理系统的新型多维规避框架。我们引入了三种隐蔽攻击向量：（1）时间规避，将恶意负载分散到连续的交互轮次中；（2）空间规避，将负载隐藏于复杂的工件中，从而规避标准LLM解析机制；以及（3）语义规避，在良性上下文噪声下掩盖恶意意图。为了系统量化这些威胁，我们构建了A3S-Bench，一个包含2,254条真实世界代理执行轨迹的综合基准。通过评估标准代理框架分别集成10个主流LLM骨干在20个实际威胁场景下的表现，我们展示了该规避框架将平均风险触发率从28.3%的基线提升至52.6%。这些发现揭示了当前自主代理系统中系统性的架构级漏洞，而现有防御措施未能解决这些问题，突显出迫切需要针对这些独特威胁的防御机制。

Original abstract: As autonomous agents (e.g., OpenClaw) increasingly operate with deep system-level privileges to execute complex tasks, they introduce severe, unmitigated security risks. Current vulnerability analyses overwhelmingly focus on single-turn, stateless behaviors, overlooking the expanded attack surface inherent in stateful, multi-turn interactions and dynamic tool invocations. In this paper, we propose a novel, multi-dimensional evasion framework targeting LLM-based agent systems. We introduce three stealthy attack vectors: (1) Temporal evasion, which fragments malicious payloads across sequential interaction turns; (2) Spatial evasion, which conceals payloads within complex external artifacts that evade standard LLM parsing mechanisms; and (3) Semantic evasion, which obscures malicious intents beneath benign contextual noise. To systematically quantify these threats, we construct A3S-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark comprising 2,254 real-world agent execution trajectories. Evaluating a standard agent framework separately integrated with 10 mainstream LLM backbones against 20 practical threat scenarios, we demonstrate that our evasion framework elevates the average risk trigger rate from a 28.3\% baseline to 52.6\%. These findings reveal systemic, architecture-level vulnerabilities in current autonomous agent systems that existing defenses fail to address, highlighting an urgent need for defense mechanisms tailored to the unique threats.

</details>

*Sahar Abdelnabi,Chris Hicks,Konrad Rieck,Ahmad-Reza Sadeghi*

Conclusion: 需要构建更鲁棒和可信的评估框架，以准确衡量AI代理在安全关键任务中的表现。

Original abstract: The benchmarks used to evaluate AI agents in security-critical roles suffer from crucial weaknesses. We then outline practical directions toward building more robust and trustworthy evaluation frameworks.

### [93] [Innovations in Cardless Artificial Intelligence Banking: A Comprehensive Framework for Cyber Secure and Fraud Mitigation using Machine Learning Algorithms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22604v1)
*Md Israfeel*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个增强无卡AI银行系统安全性和防欺诈的框架，利用AI加密、虚拟卡和机器学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决传统银行的安全问题，提升无卡AI银行的安全性和便利性。

Method: 采用AI数据加密生成虚拟卡、安全通信渠道、AI授权和机器学习算法。

Result: 框架能有效减少信息暴露和欺诈风险，增强系统安全。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了全面的网络安全和欺诈缓解方案，使未来银行更安全便捷。

中文摘要：无卡人工智能（AI）银行业的出现预示着金融领域的范式转变，为用户提供了前所未有的安全性和便利性。本文概述了一个全面的框架，旨在增强网络安全、引入自动生成的虚拟卡并减轻无卡AI银行系统中的欺诈风险。该框架设想了一种未来的银行架构，采用AI驱动的数据加密技术来创建安全的虚拟卡，以实现无缝交易。通过强调安全通信渠道，它确保了银行系统、持卡人和第三方供应商之间金融活动的完整性。基于AI的授权方法在验证每笔交易的同时主动识别潜在欺诈方面发挥着关键作用，证明了该框架在加强无卡AI银行安全性方面的有效性。最初的方法采用AI驱动的基于特征的银行系统，确保生成具有加密数据的虚拟卡，从而最大限度地减少信息暴露并降低欺诈风险。集成机器学习算法为潜在欺诈活动增加了额外的保护层。总之，所提出的框架为无卡AI银行系统建立了整体的网络安全和欺诈缓解范式。其实施使金融机构能够解决与传统银行相关的安全问题，为未来的银行格局铺平道路，这种格局不仅具有防欺诈性，而且对用户来说安全便捷。

Original abstract: The advent of cardless artificial intelligence (AI) banking heralds a paradigm shift in the financial landscape, offering users unprecedented security and convenience. This paper outlines a comprehensive framework designed to enhance cybersecurity, introduce auto-generated virtual cards, and mitigate fraud risks within cardless AI banking systems. The framework envisions a future banking architecture that employs AI-powered data cryptography to create secure virtual cards for seamless transactions. By emphasizing secure communication channels, it ensures the integrity of financial activities among banking systems, cardholders, and third-party vendors. AI-based authorization methodologies play a pivotal role in authenticating each transaction while proactively identifying potential fraud, demonstrating the framework's efficacy in fortifying cardless AI banking security. The initial approach, featuring an AI-driven, feature-based banking system, ensures the generation of virtual cards with encrypted data, minimizing information exposure and reducing fraud risks. Integrating a machine learning algorithm adds an additional layer of protection against potential fraudulent activities. In conclusion, the proposed framework establishes a holistic cybersecurity and fraud-mitigation paradigm for cardless AI banking systems. Its implementation empowers financial institutions to address security concerns associated with traditional banking, paving the way for a future banking landscape that is not only fraud-resistant but also secure and convenient for users.
